Chapter 201: All Drills Have Their Uses

The Everlasting Immortal was glad that he possessed the memories of all his followers, especially those of the creed leader and other stellar followers well-versed in criminal law.

What a lifesaver!

My case is considered a special one. In the cultivation world, children mature fast, so the age of criminal liability set by the Great Xia Dynasty is very low. However, no matter how low it is, it can’t possibly consider a five-day-old infant capable of committing a crime.

I have really been born for only five days. It’s just that when I was born, I possessed immense power and a wealth of knowledge.

At present, the penal code of the Great Xia Dynasty had no specific provisions on how to handle individuals like him. Under circumstances where there is no clear legal stipulation stated, decisions will usually apply the principles of criminal law. Based on the principle of protecting minors, I won’t be deemed guilty of committing a crime. Even if it constituted a crime, my failed attempt wouldn’t justify a death sentence.

These righteous sects are definitely law-abiding and won’t behave like the diabolic creeds that indiscriminately kill and dispose of bodies to erase all traces.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned. She felt that the Everlasting Immortal did make some sense, but upon closer thought, something seemed off. That said, she couldn’t pinpoint exactly what was wrong.

I know too little about the current laws.

Lu Yang pondered for a bit and muttered, “You make a fair point. However, if we just get rid of you here and make sure no one knows about it, the law shouldn’t be able to do anything to us, right?”

The Great Xia Dynasty naturally can’t do anything about something they don’t know.

“Oh~ I didn’t know that’s an option. Lu Yang, you’re as clever as always!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised him. As expected of the creed founder I have personally appointed; he is truly quick-witted.

The Everlasting Immortal had exclamation marks shooting out of his head. Is this what people from the righteous path should be saying?!

After learning that Lu Yang was from the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Everlasting Immortal had assumed that all his antics during the tournament were just an act. But from the looks of it now, he was simply unleashing his true nature!

Yun Zhi offered a different solution for dealing with the Everlasting Immortal. “The Five Great Immortal Sects have the authority to enforce the law. In theory, you can be handed over to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Since you possess the memories of all your followers, that knowledge could be valuable to us. As long as you are obedient and cooperate fully, we can imprison you within the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

The Everlasting Immortal was over the moon to hear that he wouldn’t have to die. Now this is what the righteous path should be like! As for imprisonment and whatnot, those are all trivial matters.

“However, if any of your information turns out to be false, we’ll directly proceed with a soul search.”

The Everlasting Immortal immediately vowed his loyalty to the Dao-Seeking Sect, promising to answer all questions truthfully and turn over a new leaf. He even swore an oath to the real immortal, Huang Doudou.

Yun Zhi said, “Senior, you can return the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit to him.”

Understanding Yun Zhi’s intentions, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded and stuffed the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit into the Everlasting Immortal’s soul.

Sensing the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit again, the Everlasting Immortal could feel his strength recovering, and his pain from the beating earlier also seemed to have abated.

They even returned the Dao Fruit to me. Good people are still the majority in this world.

Yun Zhi then said, “Senior, as the master of the Everlasting Lineage, you can control the person in possession of the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit. With you around, the Everlasting Immortal can be restrained.”

The Everlasting Immortal, “...”

Is the Incipient Dao Fruit actually so insignificant?

This was something both Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal were unaware of.

~~~

By the time Lu Yang left the secret chamber, the Great Xia Dynasty had already commenced their operations. After receiving the tipoff from Yun Zhi, they took the matter very seriously, even specially designating someone to deliver the information directly to the Xia Emperor, who was moved when he saw the contents of the report.

The Dao-Seeking Sect managed to locate the headquarters of a diabolic creed, yet the diabolic creed is completely in the dark! This is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity!

The Four Great Diabolic Creeds were scourges of endless trouble. Now that there was a chance to uproot and eradicate one of them, the Xia Emperor was not going to pass it up. He immediately issued orders to mobilize the troops and coordinate with the Dao-Seeking Sect, determined to capture every last member of the Everlasting Creed. The Great Xia Dynasty sealed off all exits, and a dozen Fusion cultivators held the line while dispatching their subordinates to arrest them all.

In this life-or-death juncture, the Everlasting Creed demonstrated a high degree of sophistication—they voluntarily laid down their weapons and surrendered.

“We surrender!”

All efforts bear fruits. Even their seemingly pointless surrender drills turned out to be crucial at this moment.

Since the Great Xia Dynasty dares to arrest us, they must have made surefire preparations. These dozen Fusion cultivators are just the visible ones; there’s definitely at least one Transcendent Tribulation expert hiding.

Faced with such a situation, no member of the Everlasting Creed could escape. Rather than resist, it was better for them to surrender quietly. If we’re lucky, we might even stay alive.

“Lu Yang, you dare to betray the Everlasting Creed!” The creed leader glowered at Lu Yang, wishing he could rip him apart. Unfortunately for him, he was sealed and his power frozen. With his cultivation gone, he was unable to move.

Even now, he still didn’t know that Lu Yang was actually a spy sent by the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Creed Leader, that’s where you’ve got it wrong! Rebelling against superiors is a tradition in our diabolic creed!” Lu Yang explained to the creed leader, believing that the creed leader had yet to fully grasp the true meaning of the diabolic path. How could someone like this lead the Everlasting Creed?

The two Fusion cultivators holding the creed leader down couldn’t stop their eyelids from twitching. As expected of the Dao-Seeking Sect, there’s nothing strange about them disguising themselves as members of a diabolic creed.

The space distorted, and a tall, slender figure stepped through the spatial gate, stopping right before Lu Yang. The delicate-looking man cupped his hands in greeting to Lu Yang. “I am Ming Ge. Please ask Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi to come out for a meeting.”

Yun Zhi left Lu Yang’s mental world and returned the greeting to Ming Ge. “Lord Ming.”

Ming Ge hurriedly replied, “I don’t dare to refer to myself as ‘Lord’ in front of you, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi.”

Although Ming Ge might appear young, he was older than the Taciturn Daoist Priest. He was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the Great Xia Dynasty and the leader of this operation. As a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, he knew far more than ordinary people, and that included Yun Zhi’s true strength. Even if the Great Xia Dynasty did not take action, he was well aware that Yun Zhi alone was sufficient to wipe out the whole Everlasting Creed. In terms of strength and contribution to the mission, Ming Ge dared not be haughty in front of Yun Zhi.

Just as Ming Ge was about to speak, one of his subordinates came to report. “Your Excellency, we have captured two Everlasting Creed followers whose cultivation is only at the Foundation Establishment Stage but are already at the position of branch leader. They should be diabolic spawns meticulously groomed by the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed. However, these two people insist that they are spies from the righteous path and not true members of the Everlasting Creed.

“We also received intelligence that the Everlasting Creed recently organized a competition for their Foundation Establishment cultivators, and these two placed second and third. Such achievements make it very hard to believe that they belong to the righteous path.”

Lu Yang, “...”

How does that make us not belong to the righteous path?!

Ming Ge rubbed his forehead in distress and sighed. “Is one of them called Meng Jingzhou? He’s the young master of the Meng Family. I even drank wine at his one-month-old birthday banquet. Both of them are spies sent by the Dao-Seeking Sect. Since Meng Jingzhou is a member of the Meng Family and the Dao-Seeking Sect, it’s only natural for him to blend in so well within the Everlasting Creed. Let them go.”

“Understood.”

Chapter 202: Joined For Two Months, The Everlasting Creed Destroyed

When the creed leader saw Yun Zhi emerge from within Lu Yang, he felt his heart sink. Initially, he wondered whether the Everlasting Immortal had taken over Lu Yang’s body successfully and that everything he had done just now was an act.

But from the looks of it now, it seems like even the Everlasting Immortal is doomed.

“So you, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu are all from the Dao-Seeking Sect!” The creed leader was a clever person, immediately piecing together what had happened.

This trio aren’t spies sent by us to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect but sent by the Dao-Seeking Sect to infiltrate us!

The despicable Dao-Seeking Sect!

He glared fixedly at Lu Yang. Despite coming from the righteous path, he could disguise himself as someone from the diabolic creed without revealing a single flaw.

So scheming!

Ming Ge waved his hand, signaling for the creed leader to be taken away.

“The success of this operation is all thanks to the intelligence you have provided, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi. Otherwise, who knows when the Everlasting Creed could be apprehended? Once I return, I will request for His Majesty to reward you.”

“It was nothing. You were the ones who did the hardest work. I didn’t contribute much. Please, you don’t have to reward me,” Yun Zhi replied casually. She then added, “There’s also no need for you to report to the Xia Emperor. I’ll be visiting him shortly.”

Seeing Yun Zhi’s firm stance, Ming Ge did not insist further. He cupped his hands and bid goodbye to everyone. “Only the headquarters have been seized. It’s now a race against time to locate all the branches and take them down. We must act before they realize what’s happening. I shall take my leave first!” Ming Ge hastily said before leaving to continue dealing with the matters of the Everlasting Creed.

Yun Zhi made no further comments, simply fishing out the Everlasting Immortal. The latter was visibly nervous, thinking that Yun Zhi wanted to renege on the deal.

“You are an important witness. Come with me to meet the Xia Emperor and sect leaders of the other four Great Immortal Sects.” The least troublesome way to elucidate the situation of the Everlasting Creed was to bring the Everlasting Immortal himself.

The Everlasting Immortal heaved a sigh of relief. As long as they’re not going to refine me. He had heard from Lu Yang in his mental space earlier that the Dao-Seeking Sect had a tradition of refining powerful souls into magical treasures.

The more I listened to it, the more they didn’t seem to be from the righteous path.

The Everlasting Immortal began to doubt the reliability of his followers’ memories. Aren’t the Five Great Immortal Sects supposed to be united in upholding the righteous path?

Yun Zhi told the rest, “You, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu may go back first. Dai Bufan is waiting for you outside.” Then, she lifted the Everlasting Immortal as though he were a small chick and departed.

As the trio reconvened, Meng Jingzhou giggled. “At long last, we have dealt with the Everlasting Creed. It’s another great achievement!”

Man Gu hesitantly asked, “Did we act a little too fast? We haven’t even joined the Everlasting Creed for two months, and we’ve already wiped it out.” The Everlasting Creed has existed for fourteen thousand years and is a massive scourge. How did it get decimated right after Brother Lu and Brother Meng joined?

Even if we’re upholding the righteous path, isn’t it a bit too efficient?

Lu Yang put on a stern expression. “Man Gu, you must be clear about one thing. Are we the ones who destroyed the Everlasting Creed? No, of course not!

“Everything that happened today was retribution for the Everlasting Creed’s evil deeds. We merely made an infinitesimal contribution.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded vigorously. The Everlasting Creed was blind to recruit the three of us. What did that have to do with us?

Man Gu felt as if he had seen the light. “I understand now.”

The trio chatted jovially as they left the headquarters. Sure enough, Dai Bufan was waiting for them.

“You three did well!” Dai Bufan commended them cheerfully, clapping each of their shoulders in turn with zest. He could now relax much more. One less diabolic creed is one less major threat.

Dai Bufan randomly plucked a leaf from a tree and used some technique to transform it into a small vessel. “Hop on.” He then flew the three back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Lu Yang shuddered as he looked down, feeling as if he could fall anytime. Dai Bufan laughed out loud at that. “Lu Yang, I didn’t know you have a fear of heights. How are you going to become a sword cultivator in the future?”

~~~

Returning to the Great Mission Hall, Dai Bufan and the trio began to calculate the rewards for the mission.

“Before Big Senior Sister left, she told me that even though the maximum contribution points for a Foundation Establishment cultivator’s mission is one thousand, considering that you three made tremendous contributions to the destruction of the Everlasting Creed, exceptions will be made for all three of you.

“Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu, each of you will receive two thousand contribution points.

“Lu Yang, you contributed the most during the Everlasting Creed’s tournament, so you will receive two thousand five hundred points.”

The trio was overjoyed. They still had considerable contribution points remaining from before, and they had earned even more this time. We have the highest contribution points among the Foundation Establishment cultivators!

“Senior Brother Dai, do you think this saber can be exchanged for contribution points?” Lu Yang pulled out the devil saber and asked for Dai Bufan’s appraisal.

As Dai Bufan examined the devil saber, he tapped it lightly and listened to the reverberating sound. “This is a rare fine saber. Aren’t you planning to keep it for yourself?

“Oh, right, you have the Qingfeng Sword given to you by your Big Senior Sister. You don’t need this devil saber.

“The quality of this saber is pretty good, but the forging method is too shoddy. Moreover, the excessive slaughter has tarnished its unique characteristics with karmic debt and tainted blood. I’ll give you one thousand seven hundred contribution points for this.”

After calculating their respective contribution points, the case was finally settled. The trio yawned continuously. This operation had exhausted them both physically and mentally.

Meng Jingzhou could barely keep his eyes open. “Let’s go back and get some sleep. We’ll talk about redeeming the rewards tomorrow.”

Man Gu almost made the ground his bed.

Lu Yang was not any better. Since the battles had mostly taken place within his mental space, it had drained his mental capacity the most.

That said, there was another reason for his lack of spirit.

“Why don’t I have contribution points?! It must be that little lass Yun Zhi. She’s afraid of letting me become the sect leader again!

“Why don’t I have contribution points?! It must be that little lass Yun Zhi. She’s afraid of letting me become the sect leader again!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was causing a ruckus in his mental space.

“Immortal Fairy, could you be quiet for a moment? I need to sleep.” Lu Yang mumbled sleepily upon returning to his cave abode.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy simply replied with an “oh” and stayed in his mental space obediently.

~~~

After the trio left, Dai Bufan inspected the devil saber once more, uncertain about what to do with it. “Forget it, I’ll just put it in the warehouse for now. I shall ask Fifth Elder when I get the chance.” He casually placed the devil saber in a corner of the warehouse.

It was almost pitch-black in the warehouse, with only the vague silhouettes of various magical treasures discernible. The devil saber emanated an ominous aura, making it particularly conspicuous. No matter where it was, it was always domineering, flickering with a dark red glow and declaring itself as the boss of the warehouse—it would cut down anyone or anything who defied it!

A precious lamp hovered in the air, radiating the aura of a high-tier magical treasure, enveloping the devil saber.

A jade ruyi scepter[1] lit up with a cyan luster, enveloping the devil saber.

A paper fan opened with a swish, gently fanning the air.

A sickle, brush, gourd, chessboard, and multifarious magical treasures seemed to come to life as they surrounded the devil saber.

The devil saber trembled in fear, swiftly retracting its ominous presence to appear harmless.

What on earth is this place? It’s so terrifying.

1. Yuruyi was initially used for scratching the back. Now it’s mainly used as an auspicious display for decoration. ☜

Chapter 203: The Paradox of the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage

After a night of rest, Lu Yang yawned as he stepped out of his cave abode, feeling completely refreshed. His face glowed with vitality like he had been revived.

“Mmm, I’m alive again!” Lu Yang stretched his body, feeling that his body was surging with power. A good night’s rest really does work wonders.

Lu Yang recalled the destruction of the Everlasting Creed vividly, as though it had happened just yesterday.

He noticed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy sleeping soundly inside his mental space. When she was sleeping, she exuded a sense of serene elegance. Along with her unparalleled beauty and curves, she perfectly fit the image people had of an “immortal fairy.”

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy doesn’t speak, she can easily bluff those who don’t know her.

It’s a rare moment of quiet.

“Do souls need to sleep too?” Lu Yang remembered that the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow the Everlasting Immortal Fairy used and could only attribute her sleeping to her “personal interest.”

Sensing the hazy morning light, the speed of the spirit energy in him involuntarily flowed faster, as if new energy was coursing through him. “I’m almost at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage,” Lu Yang mumbled to himself.

He sat cross-legged as he silently activated the Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra. As the spirit energy in him followed the path of his cultivation technique, it flowed faster and faster, constantly cleansing him and strengthening every part of his body.

Lu Yang tried to use this opportunity to strengthen his hair but to no avail. “I wonder how Meng Jingzhou managed to train his hair.” He remembered Meng Jingzhou using his hair to knock his opponent from the Five-Elements Sect and achieving outstanding results.

Casting away all distracting thoughts, he settled down and let himself become one with nature. Spirit qi from heaven and earth continuously streamed into him while he exhaled spirit qi back to them.

Throughout this process, his cultivation realm climbed without stopping.

“Hmm? What are you doing? Cultivating?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy woke up, rubbing her eyes in a daze. She could sense Lu Yang’s cultivation stage rising, yet something felt amiss.

“No, I’m trying to advance to the next stage,” Lu Yang explained seriously. “I’m already at the Half-Step Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.”

“Oh, so you’re almost at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

“Soon, a question came to mind.”

“What’s that?”

“Since I’m now at the Half-Step Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, if I take a half-step of the half-step, wouldn’t I be closer to reaching the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

“That’s right.”

“Then if I take a half-step of the half-step of the half-step, wouldn’t I be even closer?”

“That’s right.”

“If I keep taking such half-steps forever, wouldn’t I keep getting closer to the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded blankly.

“I keep breaking through, but I still can’t reach the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. Does this mean that the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage is just an elusive realm that no one has actually reached?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy furrowed her brow as she contemplated for a moment. I’m probably half-asleep. I should go back to sleep. With a tilt of her head, she continued to sleep.

After she fell asleep, Lu Yang continued pondering this philosophical question. What exactly is the answer? Is it meaningless for me to keep breaking through? Could it be that the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage doesn’t even exist?

The puppet hiding in the dark could no longer watch on. It sneakily ran up behind Lu Yang and delivered a kick to him.

As Lu Yang relaxed at that moment, he successfully took another half-step.

Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage!

“Who kicked me?!” Lu Yang spun around deftly, but the puppet had long fled.

However, even if it had already escaped, Lu Yang could still guess that it was the puppet’s doing. Aside from Lu Yang, the puppet was the only one that could move on Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“Forget it, it’s beneath my level to bother with it. I’ll go to the Great Mission Hall to redeem my rewards!” Lu Yang reckoned that even if he found the puppet, he wouldn’t be able to defeat it. Getting beaten up first thing after breaking through isn’t worth it.

That’s inauspicious.

~~~

Only after Lu Yang waited at the entrance of the Great Mission Hall for a while did Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu rush over. It had also been very tiring for the both of them; they had slept straight through from last night until now.

Meng Jingzhou headed into the Great Mission Hall to buy premium fodder which he would mix according to the proper ratio before feeding his old horse later.

“The Ice-Making Talismans are so cheap! I’ll have twenty!”

Lu Yang looked at Meng Jingzhou in surprise. “Why are you buying so many low-grade Ice-Making Talismans?” These Ice-Making Talismans were only effective against those at the Intermediate and Advanced Qi Training stages, mainly to fill up the list of items on the board.

“Hehe, that you don’t understand. We’re now entering summer, and do you know what’s most important in summer? Coolness!”

Man Gu was puzzled. “But don’t the cave abodes have a Summer-Heat Relieving Array? Isn’t that enough?”

Meng Jingzhou waved his index finger. “Come, I’ll demonstrate it for you.” He whipped out a wooden barrel from his identity jade tablet and filled it with cool water. Then, he jumped in with a splash, leaving only his head exposed.

As he took out an Ice-Making Talisman, the entire barrel of water instantly froze into ice, freezing him inside.

“Refreshing!” Meng Jingzhou shouted. His whole body had turned into an ice block, with only his head able to move. The sensation was so exhilarating that he felt he could fly.

This was the benefit of being a cultivator. Had it been an ordinary person, they would have gotten sick from the cold by now.

Lu Yang’s eyes lit up. He yanked Meng Jingzhou out of the wooden barrel along with the ice block, then pushed it down, sending it rumbling across the Great Mission Hall.

Such an artistic display was rare even in the progressive Dao-Seeking Sect. It immediately attracted the attention of numerous senior disciples.

“Lu Yang, you bastard!” Meng Jingzhou cursed out loud. He felt as if the whole world was spinning around him, and he couldn’t differentiate north from south.

As Lu Yang continued rolling the ice block, he explained. “You don’t understand! What was the biggest problem when the three of us fused? It was being unable to handle too much spinning! We can use this method to train ourselves and get used to spinning in advance.”

Man Gu nodded by the side. As expected of Brother Lu. He is truly quick-witted. I thought that he was purely messing with Brother Meng.

Meng Jingzhou held a dissenting opinion. “Anyone can talk about the theory. Lu Yang, if you’re so capable, let’s switch places. I’ll push you!”

“You were the first to get frozen, so you should train first!” Lu Yang was not getting fooled. What a childish provocation tactic.

In the end, it was a senior male disciple on duty in the Great Mission Hall who stopped Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou with a foul expression. Only then did the two become obedient and go back to redeem their rewards.

“Give me one Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill.” Lu Yang saw a golden core version of the Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill which cost one thousand five hundred contribution points and bought it without hesitation. This price is definitely a bargain!

“Hmm? A Golden Core Stage Experience voucher? What is this?” Meng Jingzhou discovered something strange; even the description was nebulous. He mused, “Could this be for Foundation Establishment cultivators to temporarily enter the Golden Core Stage and experience what it’s like?” There were instances of expert cultivators letting their disciples experience a higher cultivation realm in advance to benefit their future cultivation.

Lu Yang egged him on. “Just buy one and try it out. It’s not like there’s anything to lose.”

Meng Jingzhou felt that Lu Yang made a valid point. It’s not expensive anyway. I’ll just buy one.

He ran to the reception and found the senior male disciple on duty. “Senior Brother, I would like to use this experiential voucher.”

After the senior male disciple ascertained that it was real, he nodded. “You can use it now.”

Meng Jingzhou asked curiously, “Senior Brother, what is this experience voucher for?”

As the senior male disciple contacted someone, he casually replied, “It lets you experience the combat power of a Golden Core cultivator.”

Meng Jingzhou immediately had an ominous feeling. Just as he was about to say something, he felt a pat on his shoulder.

He turned around to see a Golden Core senior male disciple with a bald head. He had a benevolent countenance and revealed a neat row of teeth as he smiled. “Junior Brother, I heard you want to experience the combat power of a Golden Core cultivator? Come, let’s fight on the stage outside.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Lu Yang, you set me up!

Chapter 204: Uphold the Righteous Path

Meng Jingzhou struggled to break free, but it was futile. After he was dragged away, wails of agony soon followed.

On the other hand, Lu Yang and Man Gu focused on selecting their rewards.

“Man Gu, what do you want to buy?”

“Probably a calligraphy copybook. Shifu said that my handwriting isn’t good, so I need to practice more.” Man Gu was drawn to a calligraphy copybook on the rewards board.

“Thunderstrike Copybook. What a powerful name! I’ll buy it.”

Lu Yang wanted to advise Man Gu to reconsider, but before he could say anything, Man Gu had already purchased the copybook.

The cover of the Thunderstrike Copybook depicted a gigantic lightning bolt. Flipping it open, the first page was an instruction manual.

“Let me look at the rules...

“Write on the copybook with a brush. If you go beyond the borders, this copybook will unleash ten thousand bolts of thunder. Please use this with caution.

“Note: Do not immerse this copybook in water. There is a risk of electrical leakage.”

Man Gu, “...”

Even writing is so dangerous now?

Man Gu didn’t buy anything else. He wanted to use his remaining contribution points to strengthen his iron hammer at the Artifact Refinement Peak. The automatic chanting of Words of Sages still couldn’t fully reflect his identity as a Confucian cultivator, so Man Gu wanted to engrave “Words of Sages” on his hammer and add two sharp corners. That way, he could ensure that every strike of his hammer would puncture a deep hole.

Perfect.

~~~

In the imperial palace, the Great Xia Emperor sat on his throne in a dignified manner. The eunuch supervisor had served the emperor for forty years. He originally thought he was fairly acquainted with this ruler, but what happened next shattered his understanding.

When the Xia Emperor saw Yun Zhi walking over slowly, he stood up and took the initiative to greet her with a broad smile. “Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, you’ve arrived. Please, take a seat.”

The Xia Emperor even personally carried a chair for Yun Zhi and sat beside her, not returning to his throne. “Servants, bring over the fruits just offered as tribute by the south. Let Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi have a taste.”

Soon, a young eunuch carried a plate of assorted fruits. Some were shaped like lychees, while some resembled bananas.

Yun Zhi peeled the lychee-like fruit, revealing golden flesh packed with incredible natural treasures. Just eating one would allow a cultivator to leap from the Advanced Qi Training Stage to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.

“The taste is not bad.” Yun Zhi’s compliment greatly delighted the Xia Emperor.

“Quick, give Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi one whole box to take away!”

Even the eunuch supervisor who had mastered the art of keeping a straight face couldn’t prevent the slight crack in his expression upon witnessing this scene. I’ve never seen His Majesty treat someone so eagerly.

Yun Zhi stopped the Xia Emperor. “There’s no need for that, Your Majesty. If you have any request, just speak.”

The Xia Emperor dismissed everyone, including the eunuch supervisor. After everyone had left, he rubbed his hands, slightly excited. “Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, I heard that your cultivation is much higher than our family’s old ancestor’s?”

Yun Zhi shook her head slowly. “It’s just a minute difference. Please don’t exaggerate, Your Majesty.”

“It’s like this, the old ancestor has recently been thinking that he’s number one in the world and unbeatable. Such a mindset is detrimental to his cultivation, so I was wondering if I could find someone to teach him a lesson. After much consideration, I believe that you’re the most suitable, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi.”

Yun Zhi asked, “...Your Majesty, do you have some kind of grudge with your old ancestor?” From Yun Zhi’s impression, the Xia Emperor’s old ancestor wasn’t such a person.

“Haha, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, you really know how to jest. My old ancestor has beaten me ever since I was a child. How could there be any enmity?”

Yun Zhi, “...”

“Alright, fine, I was just making a small joke. Please don’t take it seriously, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi.” The Xia Emperor retracted the smile from his visage.

Yun Zhi wanted to say, “But Your Majesty, you didn’t look like you were joking.” However, it’s probably best that I don’t say such things that can ruin their relationship. I understand these basic social niceties.

“Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, you have summoned the Great Xia Dynasty and four of the Great Immortal Sects here. It must be because you have made some significant discovery while eradicating the Everlasting Creed?”

“Yes.” Yun Zhi nodded and spoke no further.

The Xia Emperor thought that Yun Zhi was keeping quiet because of some concerns, so he reassured her, “Are you worried that the information might leak? You needn’t worry. The old ancestor has set up an immortal-tier array to protect this place. Even an immortal can’t eavesdrop.

“Or are you thinking that heavenly secrets cannot be disclosed by words and must be hinted through actions instead?” The Xia Emperor pondered over what Yun Zhi’s behavior was alluding to.

Is she insinuating that enemies are everywhere? Is she indicating that silence is the best way to deal with the enemies? Or is she implying that the Taciturn Daoist Priest is the key to resolving this situation?

Yun Zhi hesitated for a bit before speaking, “I just didn’t want to tell Your Majesty now, only to repeat myself later to the sect leaders of the four Great Immortal Sects.”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

The four sect leaders soon arrived at the imperial palace. Among them was Qiu Jin’an, sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect, who they had just parted ways with not long ago.

Qiu Jin’an hadn’t expected the Dao-Seeking Sect to act so quickly. In less than five days, they had not only wiped out the Everlasting Creed but also sealed the breeding ground of the creed leader.

He cupped his hands at Yun Zhi. “Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, we meet again.”

“That was impressive, Dao-Seeking Sect.” The sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect laughed heartily. “One of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds is now done. I wonder how the remaining three will react to this. I bet they’ll be so scared that they scurry away like rats!”

There’s no better news than this to lift my spirits. He decided that once he returned to his sect, he would give everyone a five-day vacation to celebrate.

“Excellent.” The abbot of the Hanging Monastery commented as he held the Buddha beads with his fingers. He was someone of little words, but his expression revealed his joy.

The palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, Luo Hongxia, didn’t dare to speak to Yun Zhi, fearing that the latter might remember the marriage contract and force Lu Yang and Lan Ting to get married.

Through this operation, the four Great Immortal Sects had refreshed their perception of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Their previous evaluation was “The four Great Immortal Sects uphold the righteous path; the Dao-Seeking Sect uproots the righteous path.”[1]

Now, they had changed their assessment to “The Five Great Immortal Sects uphold the righteous path.”

Yun Zhi was aware of their thoughts and directly stated her purpose. “I have gathered all of you here to share some intelligence I had obtained from the Everlasting Creed. Even the creed leader is unaware of this information.

“I’ll start with the conclusion.

“The existence of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds might have overturned our previous postulation. In the past, we thought that the existence of the diabolic creeds was merely cults of diabolic cultivators banding together and that their threat was less significant compared to the imminent Great Era.

“However, I have revised my view. I believe that the masterminds behind the Four Great Diabolic Creeds are ancient immortals. The objective of these diabolic creeds is to form Incipient Dao Fruits. At the right time, the ancient immortals will sweep in to harvest the Incipient Dao Fruits and transform them into their own power.”

All five other people were astonished. With their backgrounds, they were cognizant of many secrets related to immortals, including matters of the Dao Fruits and Incipient Dao Fruits.

The Xia Emperor asked solemnly, “Do you have any evidence?”

If the Four Great Diabolic Creeds exist to condense the Incipient Dao Fruits for the ancient immortals to harvest, then this could mean that an immortal can possess two Dao Fruits!

That would be absolutely terrifying!

“Of course, I do. I have brought a witness.” Yun Zhi snapped her fingers, and a decrepit immortal appeared from another space.

“This is the faith of the Everlasting Creed, the Everlasting Immortal.”

“Greetings, seniors. You may call me Little Face.”[2]

1. The meaning of the original text is that the four immortal sects uphold and safeguard the righteous path, while the Dao-Seeking Sect shakes and disrupts its foundation. The verb used sounds similar (“hanwei” vs “handong”), though the characters used are completely different. Hope the joke is communicated in the English version. ☜

2. If you remember, the Everlasting Immortal’s name is Bu Yaolian, and the last character means “face.” ☜

Chapter 205: Three Great Diabolic Creeds

The instant the Everlasting Immortal appeared, he drew everyone’s attention.

“Little Face?”[1]

Although the Everlasting Immortal was only five days old, his decrepit face looked as if he had only five days left to live. It was hard for anyone to associate the name “Little Face” with his appearance.

“Are all immortals this humble?” Qiu Jin’an found the Everlasting Immortal’s reserved and flattering behavior odd. Casting a glance in Yun Zhi’s direction, he could only attribute it to Yun Zhi having frightened the Everlasting Immortal into obedience.

“Looking at his cultivation stage, he doesn’t seem to be an immortal?” Apart from Yun Zhi, the abbot of the Hanging Monastery possessed the highest cultivation among those present.

He had unleashed his heavenly eye to size up the Everlasting Immortal from head to toe and realized that his cultivation stage hadn’t reached that of an immortal. At most, he is on par with myself or perhaps even weaker.

The Xia Emperor looked at the Everlasting Immortal hesitatingly. He couldn’t shake the feeling that something about the Everlasting Immortal seemed familiar. “This is...the power of incense offerings and faith?”

The foundation of the Great Xia Dynasty was similar to incense and faith, but it was a concept above that. In the Xia Emperor’s words, it was the “heart of people.” Hence, the Xia Emperor understood the origin of the Everlasting Immortal the most clearly. Other sect leaders might have discerned some clues, but they wouldn’t be as incisive as he was. “Could it be that he is a soul born from the consciousness of the Everlasting Creed’s followers?”

Yun Zhi nodded. “That’s right, and not only was he born this way, but his Incipient Dao Fruit was also born in the same manner.”

“He has an Incipient Dao Fruit?!” Everyone present was floored.

To the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Incipient Dao Fruit was half-baked and unpresentable trash. This was because she herself was an immortal and also the wielder of the Everlasting Dao Fruit, which was almost synonymous with immortals and a supreme treasure.

On the other hand, the Incipient Dao Fruit was an incomplete version of the Dao Fruit, ranked just a tier below. In ancient times, it would have been sufficient to start a war that could destroy the stars.

As the golden Incipient Dao Fruit was displayed before everyone, the supreme rules of “Everlasting” within it flickered nonstop. Since the Everlasting rules were too profound, if one’s will was not firm or their cultivation stage inadequate, just a glimpse could affect their mind and future path. This was also why the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had forbidden Lu Yang from laying his eyes on the Incipient Dao Fruit. All the people present were formidable experts, with the minimum cultivation at the Fusion Stage, and each had already grasped their own path, so they wouldn’t lose their minds to the supreme rules of “Everlasting.”

“This is the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit.”

“Everlasting Dao Fruit?” Everyone else was not aware of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

From a bystander’s perspective, the Everlasting Immortal’s existence was an ultimate ancient mystery and a taboo hidden in the dust of history, unknowable and untraceable. If the existence of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were to be exposed, it would spark an inconceivable event that reverberated through the ages. However, this was not something Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had any concept of.

Yun Zhi had no intention of revealing the matters of the Everlasting Immortal. The people present were trustworthy, and there was no fear of eavesdropping, but if the four ancient immortals decided to investigate with extreme methods like soul-searching, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s secret would no longer be safe. She had no idea what the four ancient immortals might do upon learning of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s resurrection.

She explained calmly, “According to my deduction, the Everlasting Dao Fruit is just as its name implies—it can let someone become everlasting.”

The Xia Emperor asked, “What’s the difference between ‘everlasting’ and an immortal’s long lifespan?” From what he knew, after one ascended to an immortal, one would transcend the limits of their lifespan, never aging or dying, achieving true eternal life.

During the previous meeting of the Five Great Immortal Sects, Yun Zhi had introduced the method of reviving the Everlasting Immortal, so the other sects had learned the meaning of ‘everlasting.’ However, the Xia Emperor wasn’t present at that meeting.

Yun Zhi explained, “Immortals have a long lifespan, but they can still die from battle or be killed at someone else’s hands, and they won’t be able to revive. However, it’s different for an immortal who possesses the Everlasting Dao Fruit. As long as someone calls out their title and real name, they’ll be able to resurrect the immortal on the spot, achieving the true meaning of imperishable and everlasting.

“In other words, as long as someone knows of this immortal’s existence, the immortal will never die. Even if someone accidentally calls their title and real name, the immortal can also be revived.”

The Xia Emperor’s pupils constricted. As expected of a Dao Fruit that is said to be capable of changing the rules of the world. This ability is really tyrannical and unreasonable.

“Since this Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit was created through the faith of the creed’s followers, even though it’s not as potent as a mature Dao Fruit, given enough time, it also has the potential to mature.”

The sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect knitted his brow. “That is to say that the Radiant Sun Creed, Nine-Netherworlds Creed, and the Heartless Creed could also have similar Incipient Dao Fruits?”

The Radiant Sun Creed, Nine-Netherworlds Creed, and Heartless Creed were three of the other Great Diabolic Creeds.

The Radiant Sun Creed believed that the sun was a supreme entity, the origin and terminus of all beings. It encompassed the power to birth and end all lives. Even the pervasive spirit qi had seeped out from the sun.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed believed that souls traveled to a place called the “Nine Netherworlds” after death, washing away their sins before they were reincarnated and returned to the mortal world.

The Heartless Creed was the most unique. Although all its members were humans, the cultivation world mainly referred to them as “perverse devils,” not acknowledging them as humans. The creed believed that emotions were shackles imposed by the heavens upon living beings, limiting their potential. They advocated for breaking these chains and pursuing freedom to unlock their maximum potential.

The members of the Heartless Creed were those who had freed themselves from the fetters, heartless people who would stop at nothing to achieve their goals. According to a captured follower of the Heartless Creed, when he was unbound from his manacles, he felt light, as if the world had opened up before him. Family, friends, lovers...these were no longer obstacles to one’s cultivation but rather materials for it.

“The remaining three diabolic creeds may also have Incipient Dao Fruits, but this is just my conjecture. It may not be true.” Yun Zhi couldn’t guarantee that her speculation was correct. For instance, when she previously discussed the purpose of the Everlasting Creed’s existence with the Dao Amplification Savant of the Heaven Strategy Sect, the latter’s theory was closer to the truth, while Yun Zhi found hers somewhat lacking.

“In any case, the Everlasting Creed has been eradicated. Fortunately, the problem was exposed in time, which allowed us to gain new insights into the other three diabolic creeds,” the Xia Emperor wrapped up the discussion. Following that, he proposed a series of stratagems to strengthen measures against the diabolic creeds, eliciting repeated nods from the other sect leaders. This was his area of expertise.

Before the meeting adjourned, Yun Zhi brought up another matter. “Your Majesty, after the interrogation of the Everlasting Creed’s creed leader and vice creed leaders are complete and all intelligence has been collected, could you hand these two people over to the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The Xia Emperor was stunned momentarily but then nodded. Strictly speaking, the whole Everlasting Creed is Yun Zhi’s spoils of war. She simply didn’t claim them and gifted them to the Great Xia Dynasty, so she can certainly take them back if she wants to.

“May I ask one more question, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi? What do you plan to do with these two people?”

“Our sect lacks a slaughterhouse.”

“Hmm?”

1. ”Little face” can also be a way to indirectly compliment someone for their looks. Saying that someone’s face is small can also mean that they’re shy and bashful. ☜

Chapter 206: Draw Ground as Prison

After the Xia Emperor sent off the leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects, he heard his old ancestor’s summon for him, instructing him to head to the forbidden ground.

“Old Ancestor, what’s the matter?” The Xia Emperor greeted his old ancestor respectfully upon arriving at the forbidden ground. However, he didn’t receive a response for a long time, so he stealthily raised his head. Just as he did so, he saw his old ancestor’s insincere smile and subconsciously took a few steps back.

“I heard you were inciting Yun Zhi to teach me a lesson?”

The Xia Emperor was flabbergasted. The imperial palace is shielded by an immortal array, and Yun Zhi and I were the only ones present. How did the old ancestor find out?!

“Nonsense! I was the one who set up the immortal array, so I can naturally listen to whatever I want! You brat! I must have beaten you too little when you were a kid!” The old ancestor extended his large hand and dragged the Xia Emperor into the forbidden ground.

“Old...Old Ancestor, please go easy on me! You watched me grow up. You may be hitting me, but it’s hurting your heart!”

“Don’t worry, my heart is as tough as iron!”

Heart-wrenching screams soon echoed from the forbidden ground. It was no wonder there were rumors in the imperial palace about an undying ominous being that was suppressed in the forbidden ground. The ominous being would often be tormented by the array, emitting plangent wails.

Of course, there were also eunuchs and palace maids who speculated that the shrieks might belong to the Xia Emperor. However, such conjectures were highly disrespectful and didn’t become widespread. Even if it did, people would probably dismiss it as mere gossip.

~~~

Clad in a crisp white outfit, Lu Yang was practicing his swordsmanship when Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou came looking for him. “Brother Lu, do you want to learn a new spell? Senior Brother Ji Hongwen is offering to teach.”

Meng Jingzhou clarified with a smile. “Man Gu called me over too.” After all, why pass up the chance to learn another spell?

Lu Yang was puzzled. “Why would Senior Brother Ji Hongwen suddenly think of teaching us a spell?”

Ji Hongwen was the eldest disciple of the Confucian cultivator, Fourth Elder. He was well-versed in the Dao of Painting, and his cultivation rivaled that of Dai Bufan.

Man Gu explained, “Oh, it’s like this. I felt that Confucian cultivators should fight with more elegance. Fighting with a big iron hammer like I do is not what you’d expect from a normal Confucian cultivator, so I wanted to learn some refined spells.”

Lu Yang stared at Man Gu in astonishment. Could Man Gu be on the verge of breaking through the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s curse on the Barbarian Tribe? That’s truly a cause for celebration!

“Besides, my hammer is currently with Li Haoran for upgrades, so I can’t practice hammering techniques for a while. I might as well find something else to do. That was when I decided to look for Senior Brother Ji and ask whether he could teach me one or two spells for Confucian cultivators. He said yes, and I asked if I could bring you two along. He agreed, so here I am, looking for you and Brother Meng.”

Lu Yang nodded. “That’s thoughtful of you.”

Man Gu hurriedly replied, “You’re too kind, Brother Lu. I’ve learned so much by following you and Brother Meng. I’m just going with the goat, taking this opportunity to let Senior Brother Ji also teach you both while he’s teaching me.”

Meng Jingzhou patted Man Gu on the shoulder. “That’s called going with the flow.” [1]

“Brother Meng, you’re indeed erudite.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

~~~

As soon as the three arrived at the bamboo grove, Ji Hongwen woke up from his nap.

Lu Yang shook his head. His sleep quality is far worse than that of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Even now, she is still sound asleep.

“You’re here?” Ji Hongwen greeted them with a smile.

“Greetings, Senior Brother Ji!” The three cupped their hands in unison.

Ji Hongwen switched to a stern expression. “Junior Brother Man Gu asked me to teach him a Confucian spell, and I naturally have no objections. However, Confucian spells are notoriously difficult to learn, and there’s no guarantee of success. The three of you are talented, but even if you don’t manage to learn it, I hope you won’t be disheartened.”

Man Gu was extremely confident in Lu Yang. “Brother Lu’s talent in spells far surpasses mine. He’ll definitely master it!”

Ji Hongwen chuckled as he shook his head, thinking that Man Gu’s praise was over the top. Aside from Big Senior Sister, who else can guarantee that they’ll certainly master a spell just by learning it?

“The spell I’m going to teach you is called ‘Draw Ground as Prison.’[2] You have probably heard of this spell before. As long as you draw a circle on the ground, you can confine your opponent within it. Combined with offensive tactics, the other party will have nowhere to run and be forced to bear the brunt of your attacks!”

The trio’s eyes lit up, not expecting it to be this spell. Draw Ground as Prison was quite renowned. Casually drawing a circle can trap the other party—how elegant! It’s a top-tier tactic!

I’ll demonstrate it for you.”

Ji Hongwen used his finger as a brush and gently drew a circle around the trio. Instantly, they realized that they were blocked by an invisible barrier and unable to leave.

Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou tried to break the barrier by brute force, but it was futile.

Lu Yang tried to escape through the ground by using Shrinking Earth, but he collided with the solid ground and also failed.

“Haha, this is Draw Ground as Prison.” Ji Hongwen nonchalantly canceled the circle.

“To master Draw Ground as Prison, the first thing you need is the ability to draw a circle with your bare hands. Then, you need to memorize the mantra.”

Ji Hongwen instructed the three to draw a circle, but the circles were all crooked, resembling several worms forming a circle.

“Look at what you drew. It looks like an egg,” Meng Jingzhou mocked Lu Yang.

Lu Yang glanced at Meng Jingzhou’s drawing. “You’re worse than me. Yours looks like a tea egg[3].”

“Tea eggs are more expensive than your egg,” Meng Jingzhou retorted.

“But also more troublesome to prepare,” Lu Yang snapped back.

The two’s argument gradually drifted away from the topic of drawing.

Ji Hongwen advised the trio, “Practice more. As cultivators, controlling our bodies to draw should not be difficult.” Only then did Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stop their meaningless bickering.

Just as Ji Hongwen had mentioned, as long as they consciously controlled their bodies, they were soon able to draw circles freehand.

“Now, I’ll teach you part of the mantra. Listen carefully. You need to remember not just the characters but also their intonation!”

“Not to enter, not to confront...”[4]

The trio listened carefully, striving to remember every single word and their intonation. After fumbling several times, they finally managed to memorize the whole thing.

“Finally, and this is the hardest step, you must fully understand this mantra. Only by letting it naturally transform into the flow of spirit energy within your body will you be able to successfully cast this spell!” Ji Hongwen warned the three not to slack off while learning the spell.

Man Gu silently recited the mantra and attempted to cast Draw Ground as Prison. He spun again and again but still failed.

Meng Jingzhou fared slightly better than Man Gu, perhaps because he had more sublime comprehension. After trying several times, he occasionally formed a few invisible barriers, but the success rate was too low to be useful in actual combat.

“You don’t need to rush,” Ji Hongwen reassured them. “Back when I learned this spell, I was already at the Golden Core Stage. Even then, it took me five days to master it.” In reality, he had learned it in two days, but he feared that it might be too much emotional trauma for them.

At this moment, Lu Yang closed his eyes, repeatedly reciting the mantra in his mind. He imagined himself as the creator of the spell and envisaged the mindset that had led them to invent this spell.

Lu Yang opened his eyes, which were now shining brightly.

“I got it!” Lu Yang was brimming with confidence. With an unruffled deportment, he was like a martial arts master with fifty years of experience, stepping into the arena and defeating formidable opponents while adorning a smile.

Lu Yang’s voice caught the attention of Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu. They stopped practicing to check on how Lu Yang was doing.

Could it be that Lu Yang succeeded on the first try?

Even Man Gu, who believed in Lu Yang’s extraordinary talent in spells, didn’t think that Lu Yang could succeed. At the very least, he should practice a few more times before succeeding.

Following Ji Hongwen’s example, Lu Yang extended his index finger and drew an impeccable circle.

“Draw Ground as Prison!”

Then, Lu Yang realized that the scenery around him had changed. It had turned dark and silent. Pillars surrounded him, and above him was solid earth.

This was a dungeon—an underground prison.

Lu Yang remarked, “...So what I learned is Draw Underground Prison?”

1. The first idiom translates to something like “lead a goat away while passing by,” which refers to how one takes the opportunity to steal something. The second idiom translates to something like “pushing the boat with the current,” which refers to how one acts astutely according to the situation and takes advantage of the opportunity. Both idioms start with the same character, and the second character also sounds somewhat similar (“shou” vs “shui”). ☜

2. This is actually a real idiom. The literal meaning is that one draws a circle on the ground and confines themselves in it. People sometimes use this idiom as advice, telling others not to be shackled by imaginary chains. ☜

3. Chayedan are eggs boiled in tea. It is a popular option for breakfast, snacks, and is known for its fragrant flavor. ☜

4. These two phrases originally came from the prose the spell originated from. It eventually became a well-known poem and is supposed to depict people’s abhorrence toward jails and jailers. ☜

Chapter 207: Senior Brother Ji said, “I know where the problem lies.”

Just as Lu Yang was trapped and contemplating how he should escape, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy woke up from her sleep. Noticing that Lu Yang was locked in a dungeon, her eyebrows arched with delight. “Lu Yang, have you finally been caught and punished for too many evil deeds?”

Lu Yang replied, “...Immortal Fairy, can’t you wish me well?

“Fine then, I wish you success in reducing your sentence.”

Lu Yang inhaled two deep breaths of air and forced himself to explain, “I was practicing a spell, but there just happened to be a small mishap.”

“What spell were you practicing?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was curious what kind of spell could lock its caster in a dungeon.

“Draw Ground as Prison.”

“Got it.”

While the two were conversing, a large hand suddenly appeared and yanked Lu Yang out of the ground. It was none other than Ji Hongwen.

Just moments ago, he had watched in a daze as Lu Yang burrowed underground and built a prison for himself out of earth. Ji Hongwen couldn’t process what had happened. Is there even anything similar between the spell I taught you and the spell you learned?

Oh, the names are similar.

But that makes it even more ridiculous!

Faced with Ji Hongwen’s helpless gaze, Lu Yang blinked innocently. “Senior Brother Ji, is there still hope for my Draw Ground as Prison?”

Ji Hongwen nodded steadily. “The sages advocate for education for all, irrespective of background.[1] As long as the method is appropriate, all students can be taught. I will definitely be able to teach you!”

Lu Yang was delighted. See? Senior Brother Ji is still reliable.

“Try casting the spell you have learned again. This time, draw a circle around me. Let me see where the problem lies.”

“Alright.”

Lu Yang recalled how he had cast the spell earlier as he drew a circle around Ji Hongwen with his finger.

The circle was perfect, in accordance with pi, the ratio of the circumference of a circle to its diameter.

Then, Ji Hongwen felt his body sink and found himself locked in an underground prison.

Ji Hongwen, “...”

He blinked, still stunned as to what had just happened. As a Fusion cultivator, if he had the intention of resisting, Lu Yang would have no way of locking him in the dungeon. However, that would have prevented him from figuring out how Lu Yang had learned it off-kilter.

As Ji Hongwen frequently substituted Fourth Elder to teach his lessons, he was effectively half a teacher. As a teacher, I should teach the students until they truly understand. But before teaching the students until they truly understand, I have to understand them.

Ji Hongwen knocked the earth pillars and found the dungeon to be quite sturdy, enough to trap an Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator. It can be considered a form of combat tactic.

That said, he still didn’t understand how Lu Yang had learned it off-kilter.

Ji Hongwen darted out of the underground prison. “Try again.”

Lu Yang used his finger again and locked Ji Hongwen back inside.

Ji Hongwen was like a groundhog, constantly burrowing in and out of the ground. After repeating this dozens of times, just as Lu Yang was about to cast the spell again, Ji Hongwen stopped him.

“I know where the problem lies.” Ji Hongwen nodded firmly with a profound gaze.

Lu Yang was overjoyed and hurriedly asked him what the problem was.

“The problem is that I shouldn’t be teaching you.”

“Ah?”

Ji Hongwen sighed inwardly. It’s not that I’m not putting the sages’ ideologies into practice. I simply have limited perceptiveness to understand.

He also suspected that it wasn’t that he couldn’t teach Lu Yang. Perhaps even if the sages were here, they would also be unable to teach him.

“Man Gu, Meng Jingzhuo, remember to practice diligently.”

“Yes.”

Ji Hongwen left gracefully, leaving the three of them to continue drawing circles on the ground.

After practicing for so long, Meng Jingzhou gradually grasped the key to Draw Ground as Prison, and his success rate increased significantly. On the other hand, Man Gu was still not progressing. The circles he drew couldn’t confine anyone.

“It’s over, Senior Brother Ji has given up on you,” Meng Jingzhou mocked Lu Yang with schadenfreude.

“Draw Underground Prison!” Humiliated, Lu Yang flew into a rage and swiftly drew a circle around Meng Jingzhou.

With a yelp, Meng Jingzhou was thrown into an underground prison.

He broke free with brute force and immediately drew a circle at Lu Yang, trapping him inside. “Draw Ground as Prison!”

“Draw Underground Prison!”

“Draw Ground as Prison!”

“Draw Underground Prison!”

“Draw Ground as Prison!”

“Wicked creature, you have caused endless bloodshed and countless grievous souls! Watch as I suppress you in this underground prison, never to rise again for eternity!”

“Old bald donkey, it’s still uncertain who will suppress whom. I’d like to see if you can walk out of the circle this Devil Sovereign has drawn!”

“Ha! Take this!”

“Take that!”

As the two applied the spell they had just learned in actual combat, their proficiency grew at a remarkable rate.

Only Man Gu remained focused as he drew circles repeatedly by the side.

In the end, the two were exhausted with their powers depleted, so both ceased fire. They sat on the ground, panting heavily. While they fought, they had been shouting out their moves so much that their throats were dry and hoarse. With the last bit of their power, they formed water orbs in the air and drank heartily.

“Senior Brother Man Gu, I’ve finally found you.” A figure walked into the bamboo grove and approached Man Gu.

“Li Haoran?” Lu Yang recognized the visitor.

“Oh, Senior Brother Lu, Senior Brother Meng, both of you are here too,” Li Haoran greeted them.

“Senior Brother Man, the giant hammer you requested for modifications has been completed.”

“So fast? Quick quick quick, take it out and let me see.” Excited by the news that his weapon had been upgraded and fitted with new parts, Man Gu could hardly wait.

Li Haoran didn’t say anything as he pulled out the giant hammer—as tall as a person—from his identity jade tablet.

The head of the hammer resembled a huge red agate, giving it a solid and heavy appearance as it sparkled under the sunlight. The color of the handle was changed to pure white, matching Man Gu’s white Confucian robe.

“Not bad, not bad.” Man Gu weighed the large iron hammer in his hands and swung it a couple of times, extremely satisfied with the whooshing sound it created.

Li Haoran had also retained the pivotal feature of broadcasting Words of Sages during combat.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wore strange expressions. “Junior Brother Li, are you sure this is a hammer?”

“Yes.” Li Haoran nodded as if it was the most natural thing.

Meng Jingzhou grumbled, “What do you mean by yes? This is nothing but a super-sized lollipop! Man Gu even licked the head of the hammer just now!”

Li Haoran elucidated the reasons for his modification. “Originally, Senior Brother Man Gu told me to add two sharp edges to both ends of the hammer. However, considering that he is a Confucian cultivator, I suggested that using an iron hammer to hit people isn’t elegant and that it would go against the public’s impression of Confucian cultivators.

“Furthermore, since Senior Brother Man Gu likes to use the hammer in combat, I figured out a compromise—transforming the hammer into the appearance of a super-sized lollipop. That way, it’s more approachable and can be used as a weapon during battle. When not in use, it can also be eaten. Carrying the large hammer while walking on the streets can even attract children’s attention and increase its friendliness. This is effectively killing many birds with one stone!”

Indeed, when it comes to approachability, no weapon can compare to a super-sized lollipop.

Lu Yang, “...”

I’m doomed. I actually think that Li Haoran has a point. Could I have been converted by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Man Gu added, “Also, the lollipop Junior Brother Li makes is twenty percent cheaper than what the dining hall offers.”

Only then did Lu Yang remember that the dining hall was also a business under the Artifact Refinement Peak. Li Haoran, are you sure you’re not trying to open a lollipop shop in the dining hall and experimenting with your skills on Man Gu first?

“This is not a matter of whether it is cheap...forget it, as long as you’re happy with it,” Lu Yang remarked weakly, giving up on trying to persuade them.

“Hmm?” Lu Yang heard someone transmitting him an auditory message.

“What’s the matter?”

“Big Senior Sister has returned, and she told me to go back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.”

1. This seems to be a very popular quote in education. The meaning is already translated in the text. ☜

Chapter 208: The Everlasting Creed’s Immortal Treasures

“Big Senior Sister, you’re back?” Hearing Yun Zhi calling for him, Lu Yang eagerly scampered back to Heaven’s Gate Peak

Yun Zhi still maintained her usual aloof demeanor. “Mmm, I had gone to the imperial palace to discuss some matters. I heard that you’ve reached the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, The puppet must have told Big Senior Sister.

Yun Zhi swept a glance over Lu Yang, as though she was seeing right through him. “Now that you’ve reached the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, the next step is planning how to form your golden core.

“The formation of the golden core is a pivotal step for cultivators. In ancient times, before the advent of artifacts such as flying vessels, Golden Core cultivators were viewed as the dividing line between immortals and mortals because of their unique ability to fly in the sky. Some people even called this stage the ‘Golden Core Great Dao,’ underscoring the significance of this cultivation realm.

“If you form a high-grade golden core, transitioning to the Nascent Soul Stage will come naturally and effortlessly.

“Of course, given your Sword Spirit Root and exceptional talent, forming a first-grade golden core shouldn’t be a challenge for you. What you need to consider is what type of first-grade golden core you wish to form.

“Our sect disciples have formed manifold types of Golden Cores, and they are all recorded in the scripture library. You can go there to browse and seek some inspiration.”

“Understood,” Lu Yang acknowledged.

“Also, take this. It will be of help to you.” Yun Zhi handed Lu Yang a small medicine bottle before leaving.

“What is this?” Lu Yang mused, Could it be a pill to prevent my foundation from being damaged in case I fail to form a golden core, or is this an immortal pill that can guarantee me a first-grade golden core?

As expected of Big Senior Sister. She can even obtain good stuff like this.

“Eye drops. Use them when you’ve read too much.”

Lu Yang didn’t know how to respond. “Many thanks for your concern, Big Senior Sister.”

Yun Zhi then called out to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Senior, please come out for a moment.”

“What’s the matter?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked a bit nervous, quickly running through her mind to check if she had done anything wrong. I’ve been behaving myself lately and haven’t caused Lu Yang any trouble, right? At most, I was napping while he was cultivating.

Yun Zhi took out a pile of immortal treasures, each with distinctive shapes. They radiated a divine glow, making it apparent at one glance that they were no ordinary items.

“These are immortal treasures confiscated from the Everlasting Creed. Is there anything here that you desire, Senior?” Yun Zhi wanted to return them to their original owner.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gave them a once-over and pouted. “There’s nothing I want.”

“Senior, what is this?” Yun Zhi picked up a bamboo needle. Among the immortal treasures, there were many items whose original uses remained a mystery to her. She and the Great Xia Dynasty had studied them for half a day without success, so now was the perfect opportunity for her to ask the original owner of these items.

The bamboo needle could be easily manipulated with one’s consciousness to move at astonishing speed and pierce through defenses. It was a king among covert weapons.

“Toothpick.”

“What about this?” Yun Zhi picked up an iron rod.

Through their preliminary inspection, they concluded that it was smeared with lethal poison, some of its toxins only recorded in ancient texts and others with indiscernible composition. The scholars of the Great Xia Dynasty deduced that this must have been a stirring rod used by ancient immortals when concocting poison. It was the long exposure to various poisons that had resulted in its current state.

“Chopsticks.”

“What about this?” Yun Zhi lifted the lid of a water vat, releasing an acrid stench. The water vat was filled with black liquid, looking like it was brewing countless grievous souls.

“Oh oh oh, that’s the vinegar I fermented. I didn’t expect the Everlasting Creed to have preserved such a treasure. Could you return it to me?”

Yun Zhi fell silent for a moment. Out of safety considerations, she rejected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s request.

“You’re going back on your word!” the Everlasting Immortal objurgated Yun Zhi with her hands on her hips.

Yun Zhi pretended she didn’t hear a thing.

“What is this for?” Yun Zhi pointed at a piece of square cloth that was nine zhang long and wide.

According to the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed, this cloth contained spatial powers. It could envelop all things, including a living person. Whoever stood on the cloth could not leave its range even if they had expended all their power.

“Bedsheet. I refined it to replace my mattress so that I could roll around on the bed as much as I wanted without falling off. Now that I don’t have a physical body, this thing is no longer useful to me. You can keep it.”

“What about this?” Yun Zhi took out a round disk.

The round disk was very sturdy and tough. Some scholars surmised that it was a shield from ancient times, albeit a smaller one, while other scholars speculated that as long as one activated it with the correct method, it could appear above an enemy’s head and immobilize them.

“My personalized dining plate.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy complained, “Back in my time, the quality of dining plates was poor, and they would leak easily, so I specially crafted a set for myself.”

After the whole series of questions, Lu Yang realized that the so-called immortal treasures of the Everlasting Creed were merely the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s daily household items.

One could only remark that these indeed belonged to an immortal. All the items bore their own mystical properties. For example, a wooden barrel that could accommodate the vast rivers and lakes was just her swimming pool, and her Yellow Millet Dream Pillow was still revered as a precious treasure by First Elder.

“Barbeque skewers! Freshly grilled skewers, tender and juicy!

“Exclusive recipe guaranteed to keep you hooked!

“One skewer makes you crave two, and two will have you dreaming of ten more!”

In the bustling commercial district of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the loud voices of hawkers reverberated through the air, while the tantalizing aroma of barbeque drew countless customers.

Night had just fallen. After a day of rigorous cultivation, this was a favorite retreat of disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect, who loved to come here to relax, shop, and exchange insights on their cultivation.

Just as the vendors proclaimed, the skewers from “One More Skewer” Barbeque Shop had a unique flavor that left many disciples coming back for more the very next night. Some suspected that the barbeque shop had added addictive substances, but after an investigation by Seventh Elder of the Pill Cauldron Peak, it was verified that their food was simply delicious with no foul play involved.

Three hooded figures in black robes stood in front of the barbeque shop in a daze. The vibrant scene before them felt exceedingly distant, while the lively patrons gradually blurred in their vision.

One of the black-robed figures removed their hood, lamenting as they gazed at the busy barbeque shop, “Little Liu, Little Gao, you are still alive?”

Hearing a familiar voice, Chef Liu and Chef Gao froze momentarily, thinking that they must have misheard. When they looked up and saw who had spoken, their faces were filled with incredulity.

“Creed Leader?!”

“And me too.” The second black-robed figure lifted their hood, revealing the face of Vice Creed Leader Jin.

At this moment, the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed—one creed leader and three vice creed leaders—were reunited here. Once influential figures who commanded absolute power over one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds, they could now only convene at a humble barbeque stand.

The creed leader had never viewed the downfall of the Everlasting Creed as the responsibility of the two vice creed leaders, Liu and Gao. He knew that he was the one who had invited the wolf into their den; no one else could be blamed.

“Have a seat first. Let us finish these last few orders, and we’ll close up for the day.”

There was still a long line of customers at the shop, so Chefs Liu and Gao could only ask the people waiting behind to stop queuing; they would grill five more orders and call it a day.

The creed leader noticed that the waiter cleaning the tables and clearing the skewers was formerly an elder from the creed. He shook his head lightly, a swirl of unidentifiable emotions stirring within him.

After Chefs Liu and Gao were finished with their last order, they announced that the opening hours were over and pulled down the shutters before reminiscing with the creed leader.

“How did all of you end up here?”

Only a few knew the full story of the Everlasting Creed’s destruction. Chefs Liu and Gao were simply ordinary barbeque shop owners here, completely oblivious to what had transpired in the outside world.

“It’s a long story...” The creed leader let out a long sigh that encompassed much helplessness. He recounted in detail how Lu Yang’s trio had infiltrated the headquarters of the Everlasting Creed and how the creed was eventually surrounded by the Great Xia Dynasty.

The news of the Everlasting Creed’s annihilation was too heavy, leaving silence draped over the group for a while. Chef Liu was the first to accept reality and soon lifted his spirits.

“It’s fortunate that you have come! The Dao-Seeking Sect is currently divided into many internal factions. It’s a great opportunity to make our move. We were just fretting over a lack of manpower, and here you are now!” Chef Liu’s eyes sparkled as he gazed at the creed leader and Vice Creed Leader Jin.

The creed leader’s eyes lit up.

Chapter 209: The Three Major Powers of the Dao-Seeking Sect

Now that they had been reduced to this state, the creed leader thought that they were destined never to rise again, living out the rest of their lives muddleheadedly in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

I didn’t expect Vice Creed Leader Liu to have found a new hope here! Looks like the Dao-Seeking Sect is not as united on the inside. And what do we diabolic creeds excel at? Isn’t it sowing discord?

“Quick, tell me, how many factions are there within the Dao-Seeking Sect?” The creed leader’s voice was tinged with urgency.

Chef Liu set up a barrier and several arrays to ensure that the place was soundproof and that no one could eavesdrop with their spiritual consciousness.

Noticing how thorough Vice Creed Leader Liu’s preparations were, the creed leader felt a twinge of shame. In my haste earlier, I had forgotten to put in place proper measures to prevent information from leaking.

The five elders of the Everlasting Creed hesitated, unsure whether they should continue listening. This sounded like a highly confidential meeting people of their rank were not qualified to listen in on.

The creed leader beckoned them over. These are the last remaining forces of the Everlasting Creed. They have the right to sit in.

Once everyone was seated, Chef Liu lowered his voice. “As of now, there are three factions we can interact with. These three factions are the three major powerhouses in the Dao-Seeking Sect. The numerous disciples within the sect remain under the control of these three major powers, each guarded by several Fusion cultivators, including experts at the Advanced Fusion Stage!”

The creed leader nodded. It’s not surprising that the three major factions of the Dao-Seeking Sect consist of formidable Fusion experts. “Are there any Transcendent Tribulation experts?”

Chef Liu shook his head. “We haven’t discovered any so far. Those old monsters won’t easily declare their stance, so they shouldn’t be among the three major powers!”

Vice Creed Leader Jin breathed a sigh of relief. “That’s good. Without Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, based on our methods, it shouldn’t be hard to navigate between the three major powers. What are the relationships between these three factions like? Is there any room for us to act?”

Chef Liu agreed with Vice Creed Leader Jin’s view. The threat posed by Transcendent Tribulation cultivators was too massive. In the face of absolute power, any stratagem would be useless. He continued, “Don’t think I’m just barbecuing on the streets every day. In fact, I have been paying close attention to the conversations of the disciples. From the myriad information, I have managed to extract the critical details and deduce the relationship between the three major powers.”

Chef Liu placed three bowls on the table, each representing one of the three major powers. “The three major powers are the long-established Hundred Fragrance Restaurant, the Food Stall Federation focused on stir-fry, and the Great Hotpot Alliance with sundry hotpot dishes as its selling point.

“The Hundred Fragrance Restaurant has been around the longest on the commercial street. From what I know, some disciples have been eating there ever since they joined the sect, and even after reaching the Fusion Stage, they still enjoy dining there. Their dishes are not only excellent in flavor but also embody a nostalgic charm. They are at the top of the three major powers!” Chef Liu turned the large bowl upside down, representing the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant.

“The Food Stall Federation is not a single shop but a coalition of stores that specialize in stir-fry. Each of these dishes has its distinct flavors, attracting disciples from diverse backgrounds. This faction is ranked second among the three major powers!” Chef Liu flipped over the medium-sized over, representing the Food Stall Federation.

“Then there’s also the Great Hotpot Alliance, the largest hotpot store on the commercial street. Many hotpot shops are affiliated with it in the background. It is like an invisible black hand controlling the rise and fall of the hotpot shops and their menus as it pleases. However, compared to stir-fry, the variety of hotpot dishes is more limited, so its business doesn’t match up to that of the Food Stall Federation. It is at the bottom of the three major powers.” Chef Liu turned the small bowl facedown, representing the Great Hotpot Alliance.

“The Hundred Fragrance Restaurant offers high-end dishes, some of which have effects comparable to top-tier medicine, aiding cultivators in increasing their cultivation rapidly. Disciples who frequent the place are either wealthy or noble. As such, the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant holds a superior position, finding it beneath themselves to compete with the other two major powers.

“In the competition between the Food Stall Federation and Great Hotpot Alliance, the latter’s foundation is weaker, putting them at a disadvantage.

“Although our barbeque shop is just starting out, business is booming. Given time, we won’t be inferior to the three major powers. The potential is enormous. I believe that we can form an alliance with the Great Hotpot Alliance to challenge the Food Stall Federation!”

Chef Gao cut in, “Moreover, from a geographical standpoint, the Great Hotpot Alliance is very close to us, only half a street away. It also aligns with the art of war principles of Vertical and Horizontal Alliance[1], befriending those nearby and striking those distant!”

As Chef Gao was familiar with military tactics, he was the brains of the barbeque shop. “Above the three major powers is a supreme force—the dining hall! Whether it is their background, flow of customers, or consumption level, their position is far superior to the three major powers! The good news is that disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect go to the dining hall not to buy food but weapons.
