From a functional standpoint, there is no overlap between us, so we need not worry about future conflicts with the dining hall.”

From the comprehensive yet concise analysis explicated by Chefs Liu and Gao, the creed leader and Vice Creed Leader Jin finally grasped a rough understanding of the current situation. Although the beginning may be arduous, with proper management, it’s possible for us to become the fourth major power!

Chef Gao expressed his concern, “In theory, we can join forces with the Great Hotpot Alliance, but they are an established brand after all. They may not be willing to cooperate with a barbeque shop of such shallow foundation like ours.” Chef Gao was prepared to discuss with the Great Hotpot Alliance the next day, but he was already mentally prepared to be turned away at their doorstep.

Despite Chef Gao’s misgivings, the creed leader smiled faintly. He took out a piece of paper representing the will of the Dao-Seeking Sect and placed it in front of everyone. “Look at what this is.”

Chef Liu, Chef Gao, and five other higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed stared at the characters on the paper, their pupils constricting.

One of the higher-ups exclaimed, “This...this is the business license for a breeding farm!”

The creed leader’s smile was brimming with confidence. “That’s right. This is our qualification to ally with the Great Hotpot Alliance! What do barbeque shops and hotpot shops need most? Fresh ingredients, of course! If we get the chance, we can breed some rare demon beasts and supply them to the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant. That way, we can already link up with them!”

Everyone inhaled sharply. As expected of the creed leader. He has already made preparations.

“The surprise doesn’t stop here.” The creed leader stepped aside, revealing the identity of the third cloaked figure.

All this time, this person had remained silent while listening to their discussions. Now, his hood was removed, showing his benevolent yet weathered face.

“Followers, it’s a pleasure to meet you. You may call me the Everlasting Immortal.”

“The Everlasting Immortal?!!” Everyone was genuinely shocked. They hadn’t expected the Everlasting Immortal to have been resurrected.

With the creed leader vouching for him, no one doubted the Everlasting Immortal’s identity. More importantly, they could feel an inexplicable connection with the Everlasting Immortal that could not be faked.

“We pay our respects to the Everlasting Immortal!” Chefs Gao and Liu took the lead in kneeling.

“Paying respects to the Everlasting Immortal!” The five higher-ups also knelt and kowtowed.

“You may rise.” The Everlasting Immortal said cooly, “I’ve already reached an agreement with the Dao-Seeking Sect. As long as I don’t leave the sect, I’m free to move around within the sect! After much thought, I figured it’d be best to come here.

“However, having listened to all your discussions earlier, I am somewhat disappointed.” The Everlasting Immortal’s gaze flickered with frustration. “All of you are Fusion cultivators. Do you intend to spend your whole lives running a barbeque shop and breeding farm in the Dao-Seeking Sect? Are you resigned to this?!”

“Please bless us with your teachings, Immortal!” Everyone was ashamed. They were once puissant figures, but now, they were already basking in vanity at just the prospect of becoming the fourth major power.

“Is a mere Dao-Seeking Sect really your ultimate goal? If you’re going to set up something, you should aim to open chain stores across the entire Central Continent!

“If we’re going to do something, we must go all in—make it the biggest and the best!”

1. This tactic originated from the Warring States or Zhanguo Period. It refers to uniting all the weak to attack one strong opponent and destroying alliances to prevent being the target of multiple enemies, and these collaborations were based on their geographical locations. As time passed, it evolved to the second phrase of this dialogue, where they foster diplomatic ties with their neighbors to attack the adversaries that are far away. ☜

Chapter 210: The Strongest Golden Core

Lu Yang heeded Yun Zhi’s advice and obediently made his way to the scripture library. At the entrance, he bumped into Zhou Lulu, who he hadn’t seen ever since she accompanied him to the dining hall to purchase weapons.

“Senior Sister Zhou Lulu, it’s been a long time.”

Zhou Lulu was engrossed in the world of books when she heard Lu Yang’s voice. She looked up and smiled. “Oh, it’s you, Junior Brother Lu! You are the one who hasn’t seen me for a long time. Who didn’t see you when you were the sect leader a few days ago?”

Lu Yang smiled awkwardly, unsure of what to say. I mean, I can’t possibly say that I wasn’t the one who wanted to become sect leader but rather the sixteen-year-old immortal fairy within me who wanted to.

“It’s been two to three months since you last came to the scripture library. Are you looking for any particular book?” Zhou Lulu switched the topic.

“I’m hoping to find some books related to forming a golden core,” Lu Yang stated his purpose.

“Oh, right, you’re now at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. It’s indeed time for you to think about forming your golden core.”

“How did you form your golden core back then, Senior Sister Zhou?”

Zhou Lulu tried to recall the situation at that time. “It was a rainy day. I was reading under the eaves, and for some reason, I suddenly felt like the characters in the book were dancing. They entered my mind and flowed downward, passing through my organs and into my dantian. My spirit energy transformed from mist into liquid, morphing into a trickling stream. When it merged with the characters once more, it condensed into a golden core.”

“Senior Sister Zhou, you’re truly gifted!” Lu Yang complimented. He had heard that forming a golden core was a natural progression that required minimal effort for individuals with exceptional talent. Some prodigies even succeeded after their sleep. For instance, the ancient prodigy Huang Doudou had formed her golden core while sleeping.

Zhou Lulu waved her hand, slightly embarrassed. “You shouldn’t say that, Junior Brother Lu. There are many senior brothers and sisters who are more talented than I am, yet they had to expend much effort when forming their golden cores. You can’t judge someone’s talent just based on how easily they form their Golden Core.

“I heard that Senior Brother Dai Bufan and Senior Brother Ji Hongwen went through extensive preparations for their golden core formation, but they still relied on assistance from the sect to form their golden cores successfully.

“The books you are looking for can be found on the easternmost bookshelf on the first floor of the scripture library.”

After thanking Zhou Lulu, Lu Yang walked into the scripture library, though he couldn’t help but be slightly baffled. The scripture library is so huge with who knows how many bookshelves lining the walls. In the past, Senior Sister Zhou Lulu would give me precise directions down to the row and column. Why was she so vague today?

It didn’t take long for Lu Yang to find out why.

The entire eastern wall was displayed with books related to the formation of golden cores. A small portion originated from the outside world, while the majority was the result of 120,000 years of accumulation by the Dao-Seeking Sect. That said, books from 120,000 years wouldn’t be placed here; the ones here were all replicas

“Immortal Fairy, do you have any advice on forming a golden core?” Lu Yang decided to consult the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who was the (self-proclaimed) leader of the five ancient immortals.

“In ancient times, I once saw a type of golden core that could be called the strongest first-grade golden core. Even the golden core I formed was inferior to it.”

“There’s such a Golden Core?” Lu Yang was astonished. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s mouth has always been tougher than her face, unwilling to admit that she was the most embarrassing out of the five ancient immortals. I didn’t expect her to concede that she pales in comparison to someone else. Besides, different golden cores place emphasis on different aspects, so how does one assess which is the best?

“In the ancient era, before anyone became an immortal, various prodigies competed fiercely, contending with their methods, backgrounds, and talents. Back then, I was the undisputed number one. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the rest were no match for me. I beat them up so badly that they pissed their pants in fear.

“At that time, there was a prodigy who had extremely good luck in love. When he formed his golden core, he had seven female confidantes, including the renowned talented lady, a female devil, and a holy maiden. He formed the golden cores with the seven of them, and all became first-grade golden cores. His golden core was the main one, while the seven female confidantes’ golden cores served as auxiliaries, forming a seven-star alignment. During battles, that prodigy could transform the golden cores of his female confidantes for his own purpose, enhancing his combat power by at least sevenfold.

“That’s the strongest golden core I know of.”

“Thank you, it has totally no reference value.” Lu Yang rolled his eyes. I’ll just treat it as listening to another story from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Where am I supposed to find seven female confidantes?

You think I’m gathering Calabash babies? [1]

“I also know of another type of golden core that is extremely powerful. However, it’s just hearsay, so I can’t vouch for its authenticity. It is said to have happened before my era.

“There was a husband and wife who were cultivators. In the beginning, there were no abnormalities when the wife formed her golden core; it was an ordinary first-grade golden core. But as time went on, her golden core grew bigger and bigger, as if she was pregnant.

“After being ‘pregnant’ for three years, the golden core left the wife’s body of its own accord, shattered and turned into an infant, becoming a nascent soul[2] outside her body.”

“What happened after that?”

“After that, the wife realized that it was not her nascent soul but her son.”

“...Immortal Fairy, maybe you should just go back to sleep.”

“These are all ancient secrets! I don’t share them with just anyone!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was visibly displeased with Lu Yang’s dismissive attitude. As the mighty head of the ancient immortals and the wielder of the Everlasting Dao Fruit, every piece of information I share is priceless! You oughta cherish it!

As usual, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s story only reinforced Lu Yang’s impression of her—unreliable.

Realizing that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unreliable, Lu Yang no longer sought shortcuts and became down-to-earth, reading through the takeaways of golden core formation from the senior disciples, senior uncles, and ancestors.

If he followed the guidance of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it was uncertain whether he would take a shortcut or the wrong path.

“Single’s Golden Core: a first-grade golden core that resembles the sun. It is upright and unyielding, sitting at the center of the dantian and commanding the eight directions. Demons and other monsters cannot approach the individual. If one succumbs to the temptations of women, their golden core will be destroyed, and they will die.”

Lu Yang was quite fortunate. He had picked up a random book and already found a golden core related to Meng Jingzhou after just flipping through a few pages. He closed the book and noticed that the title read Golden Core Formation Insights: Written by the Cautious Solitary Daoist Priest.

The Cautious Solitary Daoist Priest was the senior who had given the Single’s Spirit Root its name. This senior was a cultivator from the early days of the Great Yu Dynasty. It was unknown whether he had passed away due to his lifespan having run out or if he had buried himself, waiting to awaken when the Great Era arrived.

Lu Yang continued reading the book and realized that rather than containing insights on golden core formation like its title suggested, it seemed more like a record of the Cautious Solitary Daoist Priest’s complaints.

“To hell with your Single’s Spirit Root! Why do I have such an unprecedented spirit root?

“Is this my retribution for committing too many evil deeds in my past life, or did I have too many wives in my past life, so this life is balancing it out?!

“Isn’t cultivation about embracing wives and concubines left and right?! Why am I so different from others?! What’s the point of cultivating anymore?!”

Lu Yang closed the book silently and returned it to its original position. He pretended as though nothing had happened and continued looking for the next book.

“Hmm? This records the insights on Big Senior Sister’s golden core formation?” Lu Yang felt that he had discovered a treasure. It was a thick book that detailed the methods and insights of multiple senior disciples when they formed their golden cores.

Naturally, the first section was devoted to Yun Zhi.

He suppressed his excitement as he read on.

“My method of forming a golden core has no reference value. Please do not imitate. Those who learn from me will die, and those who resemble me will die. To prevent others from emulating me, I shall not disclose my method.”

1. It might be referring to a Chinese donghua series or a game. ☜

2. As explained in an earlier chapter, the original Chinese term for “Nascent Soul” contains the character for “infant.” ☜

Chapter 211: Golden Core Formation Methods of the Senior Disciples

Lu Yang naturally skipped the page on Yun Zhi and checked how his other senior brothers and sisters formed their golden cores.

From Lu Yang’s understanding of Yun Zhi, there was no way to replicate her method of forming a golden core. He had heard that Yun Zhi had pushed every cultivation stage to its extreme. When she shattered her golden core to form her nascent soul, it was a terrifying sight as she elicited bolts of heavenly lightning as punishment. It was known that one would typically attract a lightning tribulation when breaking through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Facing a lightning tribulation at the Nascent Soul Stage was unprecedented.

A senior male disciple attempted to imitate Yun Zhi’s method, intending to form a nascent soul capable of calling forth a heavenly tribulation. After pouring in countless efforts and repeatedly suppressing his power at the Golden Core Stage to solidify his foundation, he finally fulfilled his wish. As his golden core shattered to form a nascent soul, it called down heavenly lightning.

Right then, something surprising happened. That senior male disciple’s nascent soul took the initiative to withstand the might of the heavenly lightning and vanquished it; even Yun Zhi’s nascent soul could not accomplish that. It was equivalent to gaining a powerful clone, boosting his combat power immensely.

Just as everyone thought that history was about to be made again, that senior male disciple’s nascent soul suddenly attacked him, beating him into a pulp. Despite his utmost resistance, he was still defeated.

Although that senior male disciple was already at the Nascent Soul Stage, he could not defeat his own nascent soul—in some sense, he had indeed made history.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest tried to help that senior male disciple control his nascent soul. After numerous failed attempts, he could only smash the nascent soul to pieces, forcing the senior male disciple to find other methods to form his nascent soul without blazing a new trail and bringing misery upon himself.

Since this matter was too embarrassing, only those within the Dao-Seeking Sect knew about it. As for the senior male disciple’s name, almost no one knew.

However, Lu Yang had heard some gossip from Meng Jingzhou that this embarrassing senior male disciple was actually the second disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest—in other words, his second senior brother.

Lu Yang still didn’t have the chance to meet him because he was currently training in the Golden Buddhist Kingdom in the west. Sometimes, when Lu Yang prayed for his second senior brother’s successful training, Lu Yang would light an incense for him. To avoid showing favoritism, Lu Yang would also offer an incense stick for his third senior sister.

“Let me take a look at Senior Brother Dai Bufan’s Golden Core.

“Desirable Water Golden Core: first-grade golden core.

“It has a clear and fresh fragrance and is spiritual but not cold, its golden hue tinged with blue. Sitting in the dantian, it automatically cultivates, turning one’s spirit energy into waves and spreading it throughout the body to ensure that the level of spirit energy is always at its peak.

“Cultivation Method: Drink water every day until you get poisoned. Then, immerse yourself in a lake for ten days without emerging from the water. Imagine yourself as a fish swimming freely in the lake, your form as you desire. Finally, use your dantian as a storage ring, merging the space with the entire lake of water in your abdomen. Upon integrating it with your spirit energy, it will be compressed into a golden core.

“Precaution One: Do not go too deep in your imagination as a fish, lest you may be tempted by fish bait and bite the book.

“Precaution Two: When absorbing the entire lake of water into your abdomen, please report it in advance to avoid suffering the fate of imprisonment like I did.

“Precaution Three: Water poisoning is a normal phenomenon. Please prepare the relevant medicinal pills before drinking water.”

When Lu Yang saw the three precautionary notes, he found it hard to imagine what Dai Bufan had experienced.

“Eh, it’s a water-type golden core.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s voice suddenly sounded.

Lu Yang was surprised. “Immortal Fairy, you’re not asleep yet?”

“I’ll sleep once I’m done having fun.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “Speaking of water-type golden cores, I remember I had once met two opponents with water-type golden cores, both first-grade. Hardly anyone at the Golden Core Stage was their match, and if they joined hands, they would be invincible.

“One of them had a Three Rivers Five Lakes Golden Core, able to summon the power of the rivers and the lakes and draw forth their water. The other person had a Boundless Sea Golden Core, able to summon the power of the seas and draw forth their water.”

“Which of these two golden cores is stronger? Is it the Boundless Sea Golden Core?” Lu Yang asked curiously. After all, how could the power of the rivers and lakes compare to that of the sea?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “The power of the rivers and lakes indeed pales in comparison to the sea, but at the Golden Core Stage, you can’t summon all of it at once. Since there’s a limit, the maximum power of these two golden cores is almost identical.”

Lu Yang was now even more intrigued. These two were first-grade water-type golden cores, and their functions and power seemed to have negligible differences.

“Then what exactly is the difference between the two?”

“Naturally, one releases freshwater, while the other releases saltwater,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated in a matter-of-fact tone and with an expression that said, “Lu Yang, you’re so dumb.”

Lu Yang, “...”

You bunch of cultivators had nothing to do in ancient times, huh? You even distinguished between freshwater and saltwater golden cores.

“These two might have been rather strong, but in front of my Water-Repelling Mantra, they were no match for me,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy tried to say as nonchalantly as she could, exuding the confidence of someone who could exterminate their enemies with a smile. However, judging by how she couldn’t stop the corners of her mouth from curling upward, Lu Yang could tell how pleased she was with herself.

Lu Yang exclaimed inwardly, As expected of the Immortal Fairy. Although she’s often not serious and unreliable, now that I think about it carefully, the ancient era was full of prodigies and talents, just like the countless stars that twinkle in the sky and the dense trees that dot the forest. It was the most prosperous cultivation period.

Moreover, competition then was fierce and ruthless. Despite such an environment, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could still emerge as one of the five ancient immortals. The journey must have been smooth sailing while she defeated numerous seemingly indomitable enemies. How could someone like that be poor in combat?

There were nine grades to golden cores, with the first grade being the strongest and the ninth grade the weakest. First-grade golden cores were extremely rare, like finding gold in sand. Even in the Dao-Seeking Sect where every disciple was considered a prodigy in the outside world, they could only guarantee that all disciples’ golden cores would minimally be at the third grade; first-grade golden cores belonged to a select few. This was a testament to the strength of a first-grade golden core.

I can only imagine how undefeatable the alliance of two opponents with first-grade golden cores must have been. Despite that, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy still crushed them in one move. Such a battle achievement is certainly terrifying.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, what cultivation were you at then?”

“Nascent Soul Stage.”

“...I knew it.”

“What did you say?”

“Nothing.”

As Lu Yang continued to read, he moved on to the next section about Ji Hongwen.

“Four Seasons Green Bamboo Golden Core: first-grade golden core.

“The pill marks encompass a bamboo forest. The four seasons change, but the green bamboo never changes. It is cyan and green, serene and elegant, tenacious and unyielding, and gentle like a noble person.

“Cultivation Method: As the bamboo’s life begins, it sprouts a shoot of one inch, leaves growing at each segment. Therefore, when one draws bamboo, one must first form a bamboo in their heart and hold the brush with a careful gaze. Then, they should have bamboo for meals and have bamboo as water, approaching nature and comprehending nature. Wherever one’s sight lands, it will be full of lush greenery. Only then can one form a golden core.

“Precaution One: Those with poor painting skills should refrain from forming this golden core.

“Precaution Two: Be wary of attacks from Iron-Eating Beasts[1] while meditating in the bamboo forest; they will think that you are stealing their food.

“Precaution Three: This golden core formation method only applies to green bamboo. Do not attempt to extend this to other plants such as cacti and the night-blooming cereus.”

It was clear that Dai Bufan and Ji Hongwen had gone through some unexpected experiences when forming their golden cores.

1. As mentioned in an earlier chapter, “Iron-Eating Beasts” are actually pandas. ☜

Chapter 212: Make a Footprint With Every Step

The more Lu Yang flipped through the records, the more he felt that the senior disciple’s golden core formation methods screamed the notion of letting loose, with no apparent sign of concern for “regrets.”

“I can’t say that either. Perhaps these senior brothers and sisters felt that adhering to traditional methods would be the true regret?” Lu Yang could roughly guess their reasoning.

This also aligns with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s usual philosophy.

However, Lu Yang firmly opposed such a mindset. He believed that the future Dao-Seeking Sect would need the leadership of someone like him—an ambitious cultivator resolved to rectify the sect’s off-kilter ethos at its roots and guide the whole sect toward the proper way!

The methods the senior disciples had employed to form their golden cores were multifarious.

For instance, a senior male disciple had read ancient texts and discovered that many experts in the ancient era were born with unique traits, such as double pupils, colorful eyebrows, or three eyes. Since he was already born, he couldn’t retroactively become an innate divine sage. That said, he believed that diligence made up for shortcomings and that ingenious solutions had to be devised by people. Hence, he placed his golden core at the center of his brow, simulating a third eye. It achieved an extremely divine effect, especially when the golden core emitted light, intimidating people into a daze.

“You’re talking about those natural-born unique traits? Hai, they’re all nonsense,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed. “They were added afterward. Back then, the competition between geniuses was too intense. If you didn’t come up with some unconventional trait or offbeat legend to stand out, you couldn’t spread your reputation far and wide.” She turned up her nose at such false promotion tactics.

“However, there were also real innate unique traits. For example, two humans gave birth to a child with wings. It caused a huge sensation for a while. Later, upon investigation, they found out that the father had been cuckolded. The child’s real father was from the Winged Tribe, and the whole matter became even more of a sensation.”

Lu Yang asked, “So, Immortal Fairy, what was your most famous trait back then?”

“My beauty, of course!

“I’m not trying to brag, but all the holy maidens and female devils were not as pretty as I was! If there had been a rank board of the top ten beauties in ancient times, I would undoubtedly have been number one!”

Lu Yang pretended that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was speaking the truth.

He also read about another senior male disciple who studied the astrological phenomena of the night sky and comprehended for a long time before concluding that the entire sky of stars was not as powerful as the sun. With that, he formed a Sun Golden Core that harnessed the energy of the sun. During the day, the golden core was incredibly powerful, but when night fell, it languished.

Fortunately, the Dao-Seeking Sect offered a myriad of cultivation techniques that covered all grounds, including one that allowed the storage of solar energy, which compensated for that senior male disciple’s flaw.

Despite browsing through all the records of the senior disciples, Lu Yang felt that nothing could be used as a reference. That said, he did gain some insights. He now understood the specific process of forming a golden core. Achieving the Apex Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage with complete power was just the most basic requirement and not worth mentioning.

Beyond that, comprehension was necessary. Some actively pursued comprehension, just like how Dai Bufan pursued water and Ji Hongwen pursued bamboo, while others let nature take its course, like what Zhou Lulu had done. Neither of these two methods was inherently superior; it was entirely a matter of personal choice.

For now, Lu Yang still hadn’t decided on a method to form his golden core.

Just then, he spotted another book. “This should contain the methods from my shifu’s generation.” Flipping to the first page, he saw “Taciturn Daoist Priest” written in large characters. It documented his master’s insights when forming his golden core.

“Haha, I have formed a first-grade Sword Golden Core. Those who come after me need not be envious. Of course, if you do envy me, there’s nothing I can do about it. After all, this is a culmination of my hard work. Cultivation cannot tolerate the slightest carelessness and slackness. It requires you to sensibly plant your feet on the ground and make a footprint with every step.

“However, comprehension is not something you can learn from me. Everyone knows my talent in the Dao of Sword. I can effortlessly learn the sword techniques of my predecessors. Look at Big Senior Brother, Second Senior Brother, and the others—they worked themselves to death to form their golden cores. But I don’t think it’s all that difficult!

“Ah, Big Senior Brothers and the rest are truly lacking in talent.”

Next was an evaluation of the Taciturn Daoist Priest from the eight elders.

“Make a footprint with every step. What Old Nine said is right.”

Lu Yang turned the page again. It was a picture of the Taciturn Daoist Priest who had accidentally fallen to the ground and ended up with footprints all over his body. Lu Yang counted them—there were exactly eight footprints.

“Sword Golden Core...”

The Sword Golden Core was unique to those with Sword Spirit Roots. If Lu Yang wanted, forming a Sword Golden Core wouldn’t be a challenge. It could very likely happen the same way as it did for the Taciturn Daoist Priest—everything falling into place naturally after a comprehension in his dream.

“Should I form a Sword Golden Core?”

Lu Yang proceeded to shake his head. I have just reached the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. I still have time; there’s no need to rush into a decision.

“Immortal Fairy, do you have any recommendations, apart from the Harem Golden Core?”

“Hehe, of course. That would be the golden core I had formed—the Unbeatable Golden Core. It is the second most powerful golden core in the world.”

“How do you form it?” Lu Yang had never heard of such a golden core. The name is so straightforward.

“Engage in continuous battles with cultivators, never fear challenges, and attain a hundred victories in a hundred battles to cultivate an unbeatable aura that says ‘there’s no one better than me.’ Then, use this aura to guide your spirit energy and condense it into a golden core!

“This was the golden core I invented, and I named it the Unbeatable Golden Core.

“I don’t reveal the method to just anyone! Now you see the benefits of following me, right?” The Everlasting Immortal was immensely proud of herself, hoping to elicit a gaze of admiration from Lu Yang.

“Just to be safe, let me ask in advance. When you said ‘a hundred victories in a hundred battles,’ did you mean battles against those of the same level or those of a different level?”

“Of course, it’s against those of a different level!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s golden core is too strong, so what she said shall go in one ear and out the other.

Lu Yang spent three full days at the scripture library. He had read so much that his eyes became dry and his mind foggy. Luckily, the eyedrops Yun Zhi provided came in handy. After two drops, his eyes and mind cleared up.

“Forming a golden core is really something that requires careful consideration.” Lu Yang massaged his forehead in frustration. He had looked at too many methods that decision paralysis had struck him.

“I should go out for a walk.” He felt like he had become stiff all over.

After greeting Zhou Lulu, who was guarding the entrance, he left the scripture library. Facing the sun, Lu Yang stretched lazily in front of the scripture library, twisting his body to loosen up the stiffness.

“Senior Brother Lu, so you were here? I’ve finally found you.” A voice tinged with surprise rang in his ears.

“Oh, it’s you, Haoran.” Lu Yang had just met Li Haoran a few days ago.

“Look, I told you he’d be here.” The indolent Meng Jingzhou appeared from behind Li Haoran.

“Is anything the matter?”

Li Haoran became a bit awkward. This is so embarrassing to say, but I must say it. “I received a letter from my parents yesterday, saying that my fiancée has returned, and they want me to meet her. I haven’t met her before, so I’m a bit nervous. I was hoping to find someone to accompany me back home.

“I originally wanted to look for you, Senior Brother Meng, and Senior Brother Man, but Senior Brother Man is working hard on learning spells and can’t leave for the time being. I’ve only managed to find Senior Brother Meng.

“Senior Brother Lu, do you have time?”

Lu Yang pondered for a bit. I don’t have much to do now. There’s no harm in accompanying Li Haoran back home. Perhaps a change of environment may even give me some inspiration for forming my golden core.

“Sure, when do we set off?”

“Is tomorrow morning possible?”

“That works.”

Chapter 213: Artistic Embellishments

Early the next morning, the three of them arrived at the meeting place they had agreed upon.

Li Haoran came the earliest and looked a bit nervous.

With the old horse around, Lu Yang didn’t need to worry about riding the flying vessel.

“Who would have thought that you fellow have been keeping a low profile all this time? You even have a fiancée, huh?” Meng Jingzhou teased Li Haoran, winking at him.

As the eldest son of the Meng Family’s main branch, even before Meng Jingzhou was born, nobles from the imperial city had already come knocking, hoping to establish a connection with the Meng Family through him. After Meng Jingzhou was born, marriage proposals came in such droves that the doorstep was nearly trampled to pieces.[1]

“If it weren’t for cultivating, I would be living it up in the imperial city.” Meng Jingzhou sounded somewhat melancholic.

Li Haoran comforted him, “As the saying goes: when one gains something, they often lose something else. You might have lost the chance to become a hedonistic young master in the imperial city, but what you have gained in return is a Pure Yang Spirit Root, something countless people can only dream of.”

Lu Yang also chimed in, “That’s right, look on the bright side. Cherish the opportunity you still have to interact with female cultivators. Once you form your Single’s Golden Core, the golden core will automatically repel the surrounding women. You wouldn’t even get a chance to speak to them then.”

Meng Jingzhou shot back in a rage, “You scoundrel, don’t mess with my Dao Heart! I have never heard that the Single’s Golden Core has such a function!”

Lu Yang stated calmly, “This is an ancient secret. I don’t share this with just anyone!”

Meng Jingzhou eyed Lu Yang suspiciously, recalling that there was an extremely terrifying real immortal inside him. With such a powerful backer, it’s not surprising for him to know some ancient secrets.

“Wait a minute, that doesn’t seem right. The Single’s Spirit Root first appeared in the Great Yu Dynasty. There was no such thing in the ancient era! You brat, you’re just trying to trick me!” Meng Jingzhou quickly caught on. “Take my Cuckhold Turtle Fist!” [2]

The two engaged in an intense duel in the cramped space, only stopping after Li Haoran’s persuasion.

“Junior Brother Li, what’s your fiancée’s background like?” Lu Yang suddenly remembered Li Haoran’s background—his parents were ordinary rogue cultivators at the Foundation Establishment Stage with no special talents. Li Haoran’s Fire Spirit Root was pure coincidence, similar to Lu Yang.

Speaking of his own fiancée, Li Haoran was quite frustrated as he sighed. “I don’t know.”

“You don’t know?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were floored. How could one not know their fiancée’s background?

“According to my parents, when they were out adventuring, they found themselves in a life-threatening situation. By chance, an expert passed by and saved them. At that time, my mother was already three months pregnant with me. Noticing that my mother was pregnant, the expert mentioned that their encounter was fate and pointed at her belly, proposing a future marriage with the unborn baby. That was how my betrothal was arranged.

“After that, the expert left, never to be seen again. Since they could soar into the air, they were at least at the Golden Core Stage, though their exact cultivation remained unknown. My parents were totally clueless—they knew nothing of the expert’s name, title, where they came from, and where they were going.”

“...This betrothal of yours was arranged quite hastily.”

“Who said it wasn’t?” Li Haoran chuckled helplessly. “The main reason was that my parents were only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, so what could a powerful expert scheme from them? Even if I have some talent, the furthest it’d bring me would be the Golden Core Stage. But as you can see now, I have a Fire Spirit Root.”

If cultivators with a Single Spirit Root did not die prematurely, they were destined to become formidable cultivation experts. This was an extraordinary talent all ancestral clans vied for. For instance, when Lu Yang was revealed to have a Sword Spirit Root during the test, numerous families’s hearts stirred, hoping to marry their daughters to him. However, when Lu Yang became the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple and stayed on Heaven’s Gate Peak, those families never had a chance to propose.

“Could it be that the expert discerned that you had a Fire Spirit Root back then?” Meng Jingzhou was bewildered. “That doesn’t make sense either. I’ve never heard of such a spell.” If such a spell existed, the Meng Family would have long gotten ahold of it. They wouldn’t have to wait until I was four years old to test my spirit root.

“Strange.”

“Whatever, let’s not think about it anymore. When we meet your fiancée, everything will become clear.”

The three of them gave up after trying to make sense of it for half a day.

~~~

The old horse drove the carriage for the whole day, finally arriving at Li Haoran’s home.

Li Haoran’s home was in Luofeng Commandery. It was said that a pure-blooded phoenix had once passed away in a seated posture[3] here and bestowed blessings upon all beings, thus giving the commandery its name.[4]

“It's much grander than Yanjiang Commandery!” Lu Yang peeked his head out of the carriage. Taking in the majestic city walls, the busy traffic, and the subtle gazes on him every now and then, he could tell that Luofeng Commandery’s power was not to be trifled with.

“Stop. Get down from the carriage for inspection.” The guards at the city gate stopped the horse carriage.

The three of them openly took out the credentials from the Dao-Seeking Sect and allowed the guards to examine them.

“Oh, you are Daoists from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Please, go ahead.”

As soon as the guards saw that the three came from the Dao-Seeking Sect, they treated them with much deference. Despite the Dao-Seeking Sect’s off-kilter ethos, its disciples were all outstanding individuals with stellar accomplishments. Furthermore, as one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect wielded significant influence, which made the local authorities wary.

For example, the most troublesome and frightening was their enforcement rights. If the Five Great Immortal Sects found any illicit activities or collusion with the diabolic path by the local authorities, they could act first and report later. However, the Five Great Immortal Sects would usually give face to the Great Xia Dynasty, handing over the cases to them. Only in unforeseen or unavoidable circumstances would they resort to such extreme measures.

After declaring their identities as disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect, those subtle gazes on the trio disappeared. They had belonged to hidden guards watching out for potential troublemakers trying to infiltrate Luofeng Commandery.

As for trouble caused by the Dao-Seeking Sect, that was beyond the scope of their duty.

“My house is over here.” Li Haoran gave directions to the old horse.

On the way, the three had overheard a storyteller at a teahouse narrating Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“...It was said that the Taciturn Daoist Priest bore an immortal appearance. In order to experience the sufferings of the mortal world, he would often enter prisons to eat, converse, and live with prisoners, showing concern for why they had ended up in such a plight...

“Sometimes, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would learn from the prisoners about demonic activities in certain areas, and he would head there to exterminate evil.

“Today’s story begins with the Taciturn Daoist Priest receiving a certain piece of news in prison...

“...The Taciturn Daoist Priest heard from a prisoner that there was something strange with the An Family Village. Anyone who left the village would be disoriented and out of it. Despite that, those who left still wanted to return to the village...

“...The Taciturn Daoist Priest saw through the conspiracy of the village chief and unleashed his habile skills, killing the demons until they begged for mercy and vowed to never commit evil again...”

Lu Yang’s face morphed into an odd expression, finding that his master’s artistic embellishments had gone a bit overboard. “Why do I remember that the An Family Village was run by a group of flower demons that sucked people’s essence qi? It was actually a brothel disguised as a village to evade taxes. Later, the Great Xia Dynasty discovered the tax loophole and sealed the An Family Village.”

Li Haoran was floored. “That was the truth? But if the sect leader could make up such a story, he must have his reason. Maybe he played an important role!”

“He was a patron, locked up for fifteen days.”

1. In the architecture of ancient Chinese estates, there is typically this doorstep or menkan where you have to step over it. It had many purposes, including protection and feng shui. Feel free to browse through the pictures of various menkan in this article. ☜

2. Although it’s supposed to refer to a turtle here, it also has the meaning of ‘cuckold.’ The term can also be appended with the character for “egg,” so you may hear people cursing someone with “turtle egg.” You might have also seen people drawing a turtle in shows for comedic effect. ☜

3. It's a term in Buddhism, and as the name suggests, one passes away in a seated position, which is deemed to be more refined. ☜

4. The name of the commandery roughly translates to “phoenix falls” or “phoenix descends.” ☜

Chapter 214: Break off the Betrothal!

Lu Yang began considering whether he should tell Yun Zhi about the stories the Taciturn Daoist Priest had made up. If I tell Big Senior Sister, Shifu will certainly be in for it. But if I don’t tell Big Senior Sister, she may assume that I’m in cahoots with Shifu.

“One is Shifu, and the other is Big Senior Sister. It’s a tough choice.” Lu Yang let out a long sigh, stuck between a rock and a hard place.

He took out a copper coin and decided to leave the result up to fate.

With a gentle flick, the copper coin made a crisp sound and spun rapidly in the air like a sphere. The trio had their eyes fixed on the coin, raising their heads up and down.

Clink.

It landed heads up.

“Looks like the heavens want Shifu to be doomed,” Lu Yang concluded.

“Senior Brother Lu, why don’t you try again?” Li Haoran urged. When he was soaking in lava, he had heard Elder Zhou Xin complain about how unreliable the Taciturn Daoist Priest was.

But no matter what, the sect leader is still the sect leader.

Lu Yang nodded. I don’t want to be a snitch either. He flicked the coin once more.

The coin landed tails up.

Li Haoran sighed in relief. Looks like the sect leader narrowly avoided disaster this time.

However, he also heard Lu Yang sighing beside him. “Looks like the heavens want Shifu to be doomed.”

“Wait a minute, Senior Brother Lu, why are you informing Big Senior Sister for both head and tail? How can we not tell this to her?”

“Of course, it’s when the coin stands on its edge.”

Noticing Li Haoran’s dazed expression, Meng Jingzhou explained, “Think about it, there are two possible outcomes when a coin lands: flat or standing, right?”

“Right.”

“So there is a 50% chance that Lu Yang doesn’t tell this to Big Senior Sister. That’s already a very high probability.”

Lu Yang gave Meng Jingzhou a look that said, “You have my approval.”

The corners of Li Haoran’s eyes twitched. “Senior Brother Lu, if you want your shifu dead, you should say so directly. Why go through all the extra steps?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou missed Man Gu. If it were Man Gu, he would have believed it right away.

While they were chatting, they arrived at Li Haoran’s old house. The old horse stopped the carriage, and Li Haoran was the first to alight. “Senior brothers, please take a look. This is my home. Although it’s a bit old and rundown, it bears the memories of my childhood. I still remember I often climbed the tree in front of the house when I was little.”

“...Junior Brother Li, I don’t think your house can be described as ‘a bit old and rundown.’”

Li Haoran turned his head and saw that the house of the Li Family was being torn down.

“Where’s my house?!”

I have just been away for slightly over a year, and my house is already gone?

“Eh, isn’t that the Li Family’s son? I heard you’ve made a name for yourself and joined the Dao-Seeking Sect.” An old man recognized Li Haoran.

“Uncle Zhang, where’s my house?” Li Haoran hurriedly asked upon seeing a familiar face.

“Hmm? Didn’t your parents tell you? To celebrate your becoming a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, your family sold your old house and moved to Chunyuan Street.”

“...Was it really to celebrate my becoming a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect?” Li Haoran covered his face with one hand helplessly.

Following the directions from Uncle Zhang, the trio finally found Li Haoran’s real house.

Before entering, Lu Yang secretly transmitted an auditory message to Meng Jingzhou, “Did you prepare the gifts for meeting Uncle and Aunt[1]?”

“I’ve done that long ago. There is plenty of good stuff inside my identity jade tablet. What about you?”

“Before coming here, I went to the Great Mission Hall to exchange for some pills and rare natural treasures.”

Only after their exchange did they alight the carriage with a peace of mind.

Li Haoran had yet to knock on the door when they heard an unfamiliar female voice from inside.

“I will absolutely not agree to this marriage!

“Betrothal before birth? Did you get my consent?

“You want me to accept this betrothal? Don’t even think about it!”

Then they heard Li Haoran’s father’s voice. “This marriage was agreed upon a long time ago...”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances with each other upon hearing the argument inside. Looks like things aren’t going very smoothly.

With his brow furrowed, Li Haoran pushed the door open and deliberately announced in a loud voice, “Mom, Dad, I’m back!”

Upon opening the door, they saw Li Haoran’s parents standing in the courtyard looking somewhat awkward, as if things had escalated beyond their control.

The person arguing with them was a beautiful girl who looked to be around Li Haoran’s age. Standing behind the girl was a captivating female cultivator who bore some resemblance to the girl, perhaps her older sister or mother.

“Haoran, you’re back?” Li Haoran’s parents were elated to see their son return.

“Dad, Mom, let me introduce you to my two senior brothers from the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.”

“Nice to meet you, Uncle and Aunt.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou flashed a warm smile and presented the gifts they had prepared.

“You didn’t have to.”

“We bought them along the way. They’re not worth much.”

After some courteous declinations, Li Haoran’s parents accepted the gifts.

“So you are Li Haoran?” The girl looked at him with a frown. To be fair, Li Haoran does look handsome and talented, but no matter how I look at him now, I just find him unpleasant to the eye.

“Who are you?” Li Haoran shot back in an unfriendly tone.

Worried about the conflict exacerbating, Li Haoran’s parents quickly introduced the visitors. “She is Qin Yanyan, and this is her mother Su Yiren, also the expert who saved us back then.”

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy softly claimed, “This Su Yiren is quite something; she’s at the Fusion Stage.”

There was a plethora of talented individuals on the Central Continent, many of whom were Fusion cultivators Lu Yang had never heard of before. Even Meng Jingzhou, who hailed from the Meng Family, couldn’t claim to know every Fusion cultivator.

“Fusion Stage?” Lu Yang was astonished. Is Junior Brother Li worth that much? A Fusion cultivator not only rescued his parents but also arranged a future marriage for the unborn child in the belly. Apart from Li Haoran’s Fire Spirit Root, Lu Yang couldn’t discern anything special about Li Haoran. He’s not someone who suddenly fell from a genius to trash, nor did he exhibit strange behaviors or spout cryptic lines.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy teased, “You’re also worth a lot. That little lass Yun Zhi personally arranged a marriage pact between you and Lan Ting. If that really went through, you’d have an entire team of Fusion cultivators backing you up.”

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, choosing not to bother with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s remarks.

Qin Yanyan sized Li Haoran up. “I heard you’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect and rank fifth in your cohort. That’s so disgraceful. A Fire Spirit Root, yet that’s all you got?”

Li Haoran thought about the four who ranked before him. The first has a Sword Spirit Root and is personally trained by Big Senior Sister, possessing talent in spells that rivals hers. The second has a Single’s Spirit Root and hails from the largest ancestral clan, the Meng Family. The third has a Metamorphic Celestial Physique which is even rarer than a Single Spirit Root. The fourth is the last descendant of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe and bears the entire tribe’s fortune.

It doesn’t seem that disgraceful for me to rank fifth.

Man Gu was the last of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, and legend had it that the final member of a race would embody all its luck.

If anything, it would be strange if I could surpass these four.

“Let me give you a piece of advice. Annul the betrothal, and we can part ways amicably, leaving us a chance to meet again in the jianghu without hard feelings. If you refuse...” Qin Yanyan’s lips curled into a sneer, the consequences of rejecting her unspoken but clear.

“What if I refuse?” Li Haoran challenged.

Qin Yanyan continued to sneer, though she actually hadn’t figured out how she should threaten Li Haoran if he refused.

1. It’s a polite way of referring to someone’s elders. ☜

Chapter 215: Betrothal for the Child in the Belly

“If you refuse, don’t even think of walking out of this door today!”

“This is my house.”

“Then I’ll use the power behind me to make your life difficult.”

“I’m a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Then I’ll tell the Dao-Seeking Sect that you forced an innocent girl into prostitution.”

“Slandering someone can land you in jail.”

“Then the two who came with you today will be in danger!”

“Do as you wish. One of them is the fourth disciple of our sect leader, and the other is the eldest son of the Meng Family.”

“Then I’ll...”

Li Haoran’s parents were at a loss for what to do, not expecting Qin Yanyan to be so opposed to the betrothal. Although they were elders, their cultivation was the lowest among those present.

Su Yiren pressed down on Qin Yanyan’s shoulder from behind and tried to persuade her daughter. “Yanyan, I know it’s hard for you to accept this betrothal all of a sudden. Why don’t you try getting to know Haoran? Maybe you...”

“There’s no maybe!” Qin Yanyan shook off Su Yiren’s hand, looking as furious as a little lion cub.

“Mom, did you get my consent when you arranged this betrothal?”

“You weren’t even born then.”

“Then what about after I was born? You didn’t tell me about the betrothal either. You only told me a few days ago!” Qin Yanyan recalled how her gentle and refined mother had suddenly dropped the jaw-dropping news on her.

You could’ve at least told me earlier! That way, I wouldn’t have been left grasping at straws to come up with threats.

Su Yiren was rendered speechless, and her reaction only made Qin Yanyan even more furious. “In any case, I don’t consent to this betrothal.”

Qin Yanyan pointed at Li Haoran, “I’m giving you some face here. Call it off now, and this matter will be considered over!”

A burst of fury also sparked from within Li Haoran. If you had come to us to talk things over peacefully, we wouldn’t have minded breaking off the betrothal. But such a rude and unreasonable attitude? That’s going overboard. “You think the betrothal can be annulled just because you say so?” He enunciated every word, “I'm telling you, I will never break off this betrothal in my lifetime!”

Qin Yanyan bristled with anger at his words. “Today, this betrothal shall be annulled regardless of whether you agree!

“Skylight Talisman!” She whipped out a talisman, which transformed into a beam of white light and shot toward Li Haoran.

Li Haoran donned a pair of gloves and punched the white light away.

“Come on, let’s back off and watch from a distance.” Lu Yang beckoned everyone else to stay further away.

“Shouldn’t we stop them?” Li Haoran’s parents and Su Yiren were concerned about the two people engaged in battle.

Lu Yang chuckled. “They’re burning with anger. Let them fight it out to dispel those flames.”

Su Yiren thought Lu Yang made sense and quickly reinforced the Li Family’s new estate to prevent it from being destroyed.

Li Haoran and Qin Yanyan noticed Su Yiren’s actions. With nothing holding them back now, they unleashed their full power and fought with bold and grandiose moves.

Li Haoran retrieved a spear from his storage space, the finest weapon he had refined. As the spear scraped the floor tiles, sparks flew everywhere.

Suddenly, Qin Yanyan held several talismans, hurling one at Li Haoran. “Daybreak Talisman!”

Taking a step forward, Li Hoaran pitched the spear upwards. Before the Daybreak Talisman could activate, it was sundered into two by the spear.

“Break!”

The spear roved like a swimming dragon, each strike exuding dominance. Its swings surpassed the speed of sound as it whizzed through the air. The spearhead stopped less than three inches from Qin Yanyan.

Qin Yanyan’s pupils contracted. There’s no way I can dodge this. “Vajra Talisman!” As she tilted her head sharply to the right, the edge of the spear grazed her shoulder, producing a metallic clang. Then, she bit her finger and used her blood as a medium to draw a talisman in the air, manifesting a gigantic hammer above Li Haoran’s head.

“Smash!”

Li Haoran could only lift his spear to block the attack. The heavy hammer struck with such force that his hands went numb, and the spear fell from his grip.

“Drawing talismans mid-air? What impressive talent in talismans!” When Lu Yang saw how Qin Yanyan flung her talismans around as if they didn’t cost a single spirit stone, he had assumed they were supplied by her family. However, based on the talent she has displayed, she probably drew these talismans herself.

“Let’s see how you’re going to fight without a weapon!” Qin Yanyan activated a Divine Speed Talisman. Her figure turned into a flash of lightning as she charged toward Li Haoran.

Without uttering a single word, Li Haoran threw out his fists. I’m not a cultivator who relies on weapons to fight—my true strength lies in refinement!

Qin Yanyan pulled out three Vajra Talismans to block Li Haoran’s fists. To her surprise, Li Haoran refined the barrier formed by the Vajra Talismans on the spot. Ripping through the barrier, he sent her flying with a kick.

Seizing this opportunity, Qin Yanyan grabbed Li Haoran’s ankle and slammed him onto the ground. She had temporarily strengthened her body with a Reinforcement Talisman, so even though her body would ache for a while later, she couldn’t afford to care so much now.

However, Li Haoran took advantage of the momentum to push against the ground with his hands and adjusted his position to bear the brunt of the impact. Just like a rabbit turning the tide against an eagle, he countered with a kick of his own.

However, Qin Yanyan was no ordinary talisman master. Most were adept at ranged attacks and hamstrung at close quarters, but she was an exception; she had specifically trained in close combat before.

The two began to fight hand-to-hand, their strikes landing slam-bang and showing no signs of mercy.

Suddenly, Li Haoran feigned a move and rammed his head into Qin Yanyan. The unexpected headbutt made Qin Yanyan giddy, and she collapsed to the ground with a thud.

“He reinforced his hair?!” Lu Yang was floored. This scene is uncannily familiar. It was with this shameless move that Meng Jingzhou defeated his opponent during the exchange with the Five-Elements Sect.

Meng Jingzhou was even more shocked. Tempering the entire body including the hair is Third Elder’s unique art. Plus, it has extremely harsh requirements. Where did Li Haoran learn it from? And how did he master it?

Their reactions didn’t go unnoticed. Li Haoran smiled at them and removed his wig.

Since one can refine the hair when refining the body, one can naturally refine a wig when refining weapons.

“When Senior Brother Meng beat his opponent with that move, I was greatly inspired. However, I’m not a physique cultivator and can’t refine my hair, so I could only shave it off and refine this wig. From the results today, I’d say it worked pretty well.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

You’re really ruthless to yourself, huh?

As Qin Yanyan lay on the ground and saw Li Haoran shamelessly wearing his wig, she was overcome with grief and indignation. She wanted to cry but forced her tears back. “You win. Go ahead and marry my mom. I won’t stop you two anymore! Do whatever you want! But I’m absolutely never going to call you ‘dad!’”

Li Haoran’s mind was left reeling from this bombshell that just hit him; he didn’t even have time to savor his victory.

“Marry...” Li Haoran muttered under his breath, then suddenly raised his voice. “Your mom?!”

Li Haoran turned to his parents and a blushing Su Yiren. “Mom, didn’t you say that it was a betrothal for the child in the belly?!”

His mother didn’t dare to meet his gaze. “That’s right. Back then, Su Yiren pointed at my belly and said that she wanted to marry you.”

“Are you sure that’s how a betrothal for the child in the belly works?!” [1]

“Give me some seeds.” Lu Yang snatched half of Meng Jingzhou’s stash, and the two began gnawing on them like hamsters as they watched the spectacle. [2]

Lu Yang mused aloud, “With a bride three...thousand years older, one can hug... what was it again?” [3]

1. The original idiom directly translates to “pointing to the stomach as marriage.” It means that the parents of two families agree to a future marriage between their unborn children should they turn out to be a boy and a girl respectively. To put it simply, it’s an arranged marriage decided by the parents of both parties before the children’s birth. ☜

2. ”Chi Gua,” also known as eating seeds or watermelon, is a Chinese slang which refers to enjoying a spectacle from the side. You might have seen this in Chinese manhua or dramas before. There are stickers too! ☜

3. This is adapted from a folk saying that when a bride is three years older than the groom, one can hug a block of gold. It basically implies that marrying a bride three years older is good, probably because they thought that the wife would be more mature and gentle toward the husband. In this novel’s version, Lu Yang tweaks the saying to “three thousand years older” instead of “three years older.” ☜

Chapter 216: Li Haoran Asks, “Is It Too Late to Back Out on the Betrothal Now?”

When Lu Yang learned who Li Haoran’s true fiancée was, numerous mythical tales and legends inexplicably flashed through his mind.

The Cowherd and the Weaver Girl[1], the Three Holy Mother[2] and Liu Yanchang[3], Fairy Couple[4]...[5]

Countless historical tales of May-December relationships where old cows ate tender grass can prove that the fastest way for mortals to ascend to greatness is by marrying fairy immortals—with an impressively high success rate, to boot.

Liu Yanchang was an exception, but that was due to problems with the Three Holy Mother’s elder brother, Yang Jian, or the system of the Heavenly Court. However, Su Yiren doesn’t look like she has an elder brother at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, and there were no Heavenly Court laws in ancient times.

Therefore, the conclusion is crystal clear.

“Junior Brother Li, you’re set to enjoy life. You’ve saved yourself decades of detours and hardships. Others will be so green with envy.” Lu Yang clicked his tongue in amazement. We didn’t come here in vain.

Absolutely worth it.

“By the way, why did Junior Brother Li call us here again?” Lu Yang had forgotten their original purpose for coming.

Meng Jingzhou cracked a handful of seeds[6] and tossed them into his mouth, savoring the aftertaste as he mulled over it. “I think he said that he was afraid that he’d be too nervous when he meets his fiancée, so he wanted us to back him up.”

“Oh, Junior Brother Li doesn’t seem very nervous. He probably doesn’t need our help then.” Lu Yang glanced at Li Haoran who looked like he wanted to cry but had no tears. That has nothing to do with being nervous.

“Got any more seeds? I’ve finished mine.” All that was left in Lu Yang’s hands were seed shells.

Meng Jingzhou whipped out a bag of seeds. “I do, but they’re raw.”

“No problem, I have fire to roast it. What flavor would you like?” Lu Yang offered.

“Something a little salty.”

“Got it.”

Lu Yang spat out his Three Flavor True Fire, controlling its heat to roast the seeds.

On the other hand, Li Haoran was still unaware that his two “reliable” senior brothers had abandoned him completely. He was too preoccupied to care about this now as he listened to how his mother had “sold him off.”

“When Su Yiren rescued your father and me back then, she noticed that I was pregnant and asked if we could arrange a betrothal between you and her. At that time, I thought that she was a pretty lady with high cultivation, which meant you would be marrying up. Su Yiren was willing, and so were we.”

“Hold on, Mom, didn’t you consider the age difference?” Li Haoran’s mouth was agape. In all my life, I’ve never heard of anyone arranging their marriage like this.

Li Haoran’s mother glared at him with an expression that said, “How have I taught you since you were a kid? Don’t be constrained by worldly views and norms. Is age a problem for cultivators? Of course not.”

“Look at the formidable Fusion couples nowadays. Do age gaps of a few hundred or thousand years even matter?” Li Haoran’s mother began counting on her fingers, enumerating anecdotes of couples with harmonious relationships despite their large age gaps. “There are also those in the Transcendent Tribulation Stage where the age difference is even greater.”

Li Haoran massaged his forehead in agony. So that’s why you told me all these theories when I was young.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded profusely as they listened by the side. Li Haoran’s mother does have a point. In the cultivation world, age gap is indeed not an issue in the face of love. Moreover, there are also no concerns about the younger person waiting for the older one to die off so that they can inherit their wealth. After all, who knew who would live longer?

Lu Yang once heard about a renowned Fusion figure whose time was nearly up. He wanted to pursue a romance in his twilight years, and multiple women married him with ulterior motives, yet after several wives passed from old age, this senior was still well alive.

If we take a step back, is the age gap between Su Yiren and Li Haoran really three thousand years? Not necessarily. Perhaps Su Yiren is very talented and has already reached the Fusion Stage.

Lu Yang had a perfect example at hand. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy became an immortal at just the age of sixteen, while I’m still at the Foundation Establishment Stage despite being at the same age—utterly embarrassing.

Hence, we can derive that as long as one party misrepresents their age, the age gap between both parties won’t be that large.

Li Haoran’s mother continued, “Back then, your father and I had no idea how high Su Yiren’s cultivation was. We figured she’d be at the Golden Core or the Nascent Soul stage. Either way, it was definitely above us.

“Later, when we tested your spirit root, we discovered that you had a rare Fire Spirit Root, which implied that you have a bright future ahead of you. Your cultivation would definitely be above the Nascent Soul Stage, so even if you marry Su Yiren, she wouldn’t lose out.”

Li Haoran’s parents had never entertained the thought of reneging on the betrothal despite Li Haoran’s remarkable talent. Su Yiren had saved their lives, and they had already fixed the betrothal early on. How could they back out?

Li Haoran’s mother added, “Originally, your father and I planned to exhort you that you could also help Su Yiren once your cultivation was high enough. It was only a few days ago when Su Yiren came with her daughter did we realize that she was at the Fusion Stage. That completely caught us off guard. You better buck up with your cultivation, or else you’ll be unworthy of her.

“It’s just that Yanyan reacted a little strongly and opposed the marriage, even suggesting multiple times that we break off the betrothal. You know how things went from there.”

Li Haoran, “...”

No wonder Qin Yanyan reacted so strongly. After living for a decade, if your mother suddenly tells you that she wants to get married and you’ll gain an extra father, who could handle that?

Putting himself in her shoes, Li Haoran reckoned that he would have reacted the same way. He told Qin Yanyan earnestly, “I think you make a point. Given the advocacy for freedom of love nowadays, something like a betrothal that goes against one’s will should be annulled.”

Su Yiren silently took out a recording orb, which played the bold declarations Li Haoran had shouted amidst his battle with Qin Yanyan.

“I'm telling you, I will never break off this betrothal in my lifetime!

“I'm telling you, I will never break off this betrothal in my lifetime!

“I'm telling you, I will never break off this betrothal in my lifetime!”

Despite not saying a single word, Su Yiren’s silence spoke more than a thousand words.

“Stop stop stop, don’t play it anymore!” Li Haoran implored. He wished he could crawl into a hole and hide himself. Why can’t I master Senior Brother Lu’s Shrinking Earth?

Had I known it would turn out like this, I wouldn’t have come home. Isn’t obediently staying in the Dao-Seeking Sect and refining artifacts much better? If I eat soft rice and live off a woman at such a young age, how would my peers see me?!

Li Haoran glanced at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, who were casually snacking on seeds. They evidently had no intention of helping him out. He continued to stare at them. Feeling uncomfortable under his gaze, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had no choice but to step forward and uphold justice.

“The main issue here lies with Senior Su. Senior Su, why did you choose to arrange this betrothal with Junior Brother Li?”

All eyes in the room were now on Su Yiren, making her face turn red with embarrassment. She was a shy person; the more people there were, the less she wanted to speak. However, now that things have come to this, she could only step in to clarify the situation. Trying to be as concise as possible, she provided an explanation.

“Actually, Li Haoran is the reincarnation of my husband.

“Yanyan, Li Haoran is really the reincarnation of your father.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

It’s over. Why is this getting even more complicated? Is it too late to back out now?

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had perked up. I definitely get to encounter many interesting and fun things by following Lu Yang.

1. This is a famous Chinese tale of two lovers, a goddess and a mortal, separated by the Milky Way. The Qixi Festival (7th day of the 7th month of the lunar calendar), also known as the Chinese Valentine’s Day, is when the Cowherd and Weaver Girl meet annually. ☜

2. Sanshengmu is a goddess presiding over love and marriage. ☜

3. This love story is originally from a xiqu or Chinese opera called Baoliandeng or “Precious Lotus Lantern.” The romance is between the Three Holy Mother and Liu Yanchang, also a goddess and a mortal respectively. ☜

4. ”Fairy Couple” is the English name of a Chinese drama adapted from the mythological novel Legend of the Seven Immortal Fairies. The story is about seven immortal fairies who descended to the mortal realm and met a man named Dong Yong, eventually staying behind to accompany him. ☜

5. In short, the stories listed here are about goddesses or immortal fairies starting a romance with a mortal man. ☜

6. This is what I mentioned about “eating seeds” in the previous chapter. Basically, they’re enjoying the show. ☜

Chapter 217: Qin Haoran

Everyone had already left the courtyard, led by Li Haoran’s parents to the guest reception hall. As Qin Yanyan was the most junior among those present, she served everyone some snacks and tea.

Although Qin Yanyan was similar in age to Li Haoran, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou, she lost to them in terms of seniority.

“Li Haoran’s previous incarnation was called Qin Haoran. He was my husband and a cultivator at the Apex Fusion Stage.” Su Yiren mentioned a name no one had heard of before.

Everyone reacted differently.

Li Haoran’s parents didn’t expect their son to have such an impressive background.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were eager to listen in on gossip but also wary of getting implicated in troublesome matters.

Qin Yanyan didn’t acknowledge Li Haoran’s identity, but she was still interested in hearing her mother talk about her father, who was seldom mentioned.

Li Haoran was expressionless—he had given up on resisting; he simply wanted to see how things would unfold.

Perhaps the matters had been suppressed in her heart for so long, or perhaps she was lost in her own memories, but whatever the reason, the more Su Yiren spoke about it, the more eloquent she became. “I met Qin Haoran five hundred years ago. At that time, I was living in isolation in the mountains as a secluded cultivator. I hardly left the mountain except to pay taxes once every ten years.

“One day, when I was meditating in the forest, a person covered in blood broke through the barrier I had set up and crashed into the ground. When he saw me approaching, he instinctively tried to activate his powers to defend himself, but he was too badly wounded to do so, and he soon fell unconscious.

“Finding him very pitiful, I saved him. He only woke up after a month. After he came to, he was initially very on guard, but after learning that I had taken care of him for a month, he relaxed and thanked me for saving his life.”

Su Yiren involuntarily skipped over some details—such as how Qin Haoran’s injuries were internal, yet she had completely wrapped him up in white cloth and even put him in a cast, making Qin Haoran look like a mummy that had hidden inside a terracotta soldier. If not for Su Yiren’s “care,” Qin Haoran could probably have woken up half a month earlier. All these are minor details, so it’s fine even if I don’t bring them up.

“He said his name was Qin Haoran and that he was a Fusion cultivator. A month ago, his enemies were pursuing him. Although he successfully killed them off, he sustained extremely grave injuries. He also apologized for destroying the barrier I had set up.

“I could discern that he was telling the truth. Even though he had just awakened and could mobilize only a small portion of his powers, he was too battered, and his meridians were all broken. He was a complete mess.

“Initially, he wanted to leave, but I was worried that he might encounter some danger if he left just like that, so I told him he could stay. And thus, he remained in the mountains to recuperate. Over time, we developed feelings for each other and married. Our marriage was very low-key. We only invited some mountain demon spirits and a few close friends.

“After he recovered, he became busy every day. I asked him what he was doing and whether he needed my help. He said he was doing something very dangerous and that it would be safer for me to stay in the dark. Out of trust, I didn’t press further.

“For the next five hundred years, Haoran slowly advanced to the Apex Fusion Stage and was only a step away from the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. He told me he used to be abstemious, thinking that it was the best way to cultivate. However, ever since he met me and married me, he realized that his previous mindset was wrong.

“During this time we were together, his rigid bottleneck loosened, and his cultivation progressed repeatedly. I asked him why my cultivation hadn’t improved, and he answered that it could be that my cultivation talent was inadequate.

“It’s extremely hard for high-level cultivators to have children. We worked hard for five hundred years before I became pregnant with Yanyan. Later, he stated that he had touched the threshold of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage but was lacking just one heavenly tribulation. He wanted to fight for a future for us, mother and daughter.

“The risk of the tribulation was too high, and I tried to persuade him otherwise. However, he explained that his identity was too special. If he didn’t reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he would have to remain in hiding for the rest of his life. Only by achieving the Transcendent Tribulation Stage could he overcome this situation.

“Unfortunately, the heavenly tribulation was too terrifying. Regardless of his many preparations, he still couldn’t withstand the last lightning tribulation and plummeted from the sky. I bawled my eyes out as I caught him, desperately stuffing all kinds of top-grade pills into his mouth. He said he knew best about his condition and had no chance of surviving.

“That was when he told me not to worry. He had practiced a type of cultivation technique that allowed him to reincarnate endlessly, with his talent in each lifetime being better than the previous. Qin Haoran was his eighth incarnation. Originally, he planned to tell the matter of his reincarnation to his subordinates so they could help look out for his next incarnation and ensure that he grew up safely. However, he later felt that he couldn’t trust them and decided to ask me to look after his next incarnation instead.

“He imparted to me the secret method to find his next incarnation. Following the secret method, I found Aunt, who was pregnant at the time. When Uncle and Aunt ran into danger, I rescued them. Afterward, I arranged a betrothal with Haoran, who was still in her belly, hoping to rekindle our past relationship.”

Li Haoran was bewildered. “Didn’t you suspect that it was a lie made up by Qin Haoran before he died?”

Su Yiren shook her head gently. “I did have some doubts, but your talent can’t be faked. When you tested your spirit root at the age of six, I was hiding in the shadows and saw with my own eyes that you had a Fire Spirit Root. No matter how powerful Haoran was, he couldn’t have randomly pointed someone out and asserted that he had a Single Spirit Root.”

“But what if Qin Haoran had a way to predict someone else’s talent?” Li Haoran was still unwilling to give up.

Su Yiren smiled. “I know you still don’t fully believe what I’ve said. Time will prove everything. Haoran once told me that as the cultivation of his next incarnation increases, he will gradually acquire memory fragments of his past lives. That said, you don’t have to worry about these memory fragments affecting your personality. You will still be you.”

When it came to profound topics like reincarnation, Lu Yang reckoned it was time to consult an immortal well-versed in ancient secrets. “Immortal Fairy, does reincarnation truly exist?”

“Theories of reincarnation had already existed in an era far older than ancient times. At that time, there were countless prodigies, and people often said, ‘This child has extraordinary talent; they might be the reincarnation of so-and-so.’ Some even claimed that the five of us could become immortals because we were also reincarnations of so-and-so.

“After the five of us became immortals, we worked together to deduce the mysteries of the world and discovered that reincarnation did not exist. All those previous rumors were simply baseless fantasies of the people.”

“Is that to say that Qin Haoran was really lying?” Lu Yang was dumbfounded. A few moments ago, I really thought that Li Haoran was Qin Haoran’s reincarnation.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “I only said that reincarnation didn’t exist in the ancient era. That doesn’t necessarily mean that it doesn’t exist now.”

“What do you mean?” Lu Yang was even more befuddled.

“You have to know that the emergence of a Dao Fruit signifies the creation of a new rule in the world. During the time I was dead, what if someone had formed a ‘Reincarnation’ Dao Fruit?

“In that case, wouldn’t the notion of reincarnation become a reality?”

Chapter 218: Secrets of Dao Fruits

Lu Yang’s heart thumped wildly. When he experienced “Buyi Town’s Rules,” he had heard the Taciturn Daoist Priest mention the concept of “rules.” At the Fusion Stage, one could begin to grasp the rudiments of rules. When one progressed to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they could control rules on a broader scale. As for immortals, they could command the rules of the entire world.

But I’ve never imagined that it could go so far as creating something like a “Reincarnation” rule. If an immortal really created such a rule, could they create other rules? All these things that seem ordinary now...how many of them didn’t exist in ancient times and only came into being later?

What was the Ancient Nameless One’s purpose in refining the stars into a continent? Could it also be a manifestation of some rule or perhaps an attempt at creating one?

Lu Yang gazed up at the dazzling sun in the sky. The sun is the moon. This was also something I never thought would be possible in my past life. The sun, a star which people view as the source of life and power, may also be the embodiment of some rule.

Lu Yang bombarded the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with all these questions, but the latter was clearly overwhelmed by their sheer complexity and became dizzy. “In any case, based on everything I’ve observed since my resurrection, there’s not much difference between now and the ancient era. At most, the refinement of the stars into a continent is one, and the sun is another.

“Since you’ve brought up the topic of Dao Fruits, I might as well explain a little. However, the Dao Fruit of immortals is something far too distant for the current you. Knowing too much now may hinder your future cultivation, so I can only share a bit. If it were that little lass Yun Zhi, I could tell her much more about Dao Fruits...oh, though it doesn’t seem like she needs me to impart it to her.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy extended two fingers and began counting as she elucidated the concept of Dao Fruits to Lu Yang. “Dao Fruits can be divided into two categories based on the rules they govern.

“The first type includes the Epoch Immortal’s Epoch Dao Fruit, which controls the rules of time. Time rules are an objective existence and have always been present. The Epoch Dao Fruit’s role is to grasp these preexisting rules and modify them at will. Only the Epoch Immortal knows the extent to which these alterations can be made.

“The second type includes my Everlasting Dao Fruit, which governs the ‘Everlasting’ Rule, a rule I have created. It has never existed before, and it only applies to me...oh, wait...Bu Yaolian is also considered. That means that the Everlasting Rule only works on me and Bu Yaolian, though its effects on him are far weaker than on me.

“Bu Yaolian’s Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit can only allow him to appear on any statue at will. It’s the most fundamental form of the Everlasting Rule and can be used for escaping. If he dies, he can’t be revived.

“But I’m different.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy broke into a wide smile, exuding immense confidence. “As long as someone calls out my name, regardless of the time, place, and language, I can be resurrected!

“This ability of mine was something the other four immortals were terribly envious of!
