Unfortunately for them, their abilities were lacking, and they couldn’t form the Everlasting Dao Fruit.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was very pleased about herself. There was naturally a reason she proclaimed herself as the leader of the five ancient immortals.

Lu Yang wondered if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had eaten a meal she cooked, achieved enlightenment on the brink of death, comprehended the true meaning of ‘Everlasting,’ and formed the Everlasting Dao Fruit. Afterward, she probably erased all unpleasant memories.

“And then there’s the Heaven Mandate Immortal, whose Dao Fruit was also a rule created out of nowhere, called the ‘Tribulation Mandate’ Rule.”

“Tribulation Mandate Rule?” Lu Yang asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy elaborated, “It is most commonly manifested as the lightning tribulation during breakthroughs. Progressing from Nascent Soul to Divine Transfiguration or from Divine Transfiguration to Void Refinement requires passing a lightning tribulation. This is something unique to your era. Back in the ancient era, cultivators didn’t need to undergo lightning tribulations.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal believed that people were cultivating solely to seek power and speed, neglecting their state of mind and losing sight of the original meaning of cultivation. Hence, he formed a Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit to add a trial for cultivators.

“Facts have proven that the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s decision was correct. With the introduction of lightning tribulation, cultivators began to value their mental state and diligently prepared to handle the lightning tribulation. Cases of falling to qi deviation became much less frequent. The Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit is a prime example of extending a rule and imposing an additional law on everyone.

“So now you see? If someone had become an immortal after I died and formed a ‘Reincarnation’ Dao Fruit, it would be akin to what the Heaven Mandate Immortal and I did—creating a rule out of nowhere. The only question is whether this ‘Reincarnation Rule’ is applied to specific individuals or everyone.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy expounded further, “If it applies to specific individuals, it would generally imply that the wielder of the Incipient Reincarnation Dao Fruit can reincarnate endlessly, achieving an alternative form of eternal life.

“If it applies to everyone, that would indicate that everyone has a past life, including you, Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and Tao Yaoye. But I think that’s not very likely.”

“Why is that?” Lu Yang followed up.

“Think about it. If everyone reincarnates, wouldn’t that mean the total number of souls in the world is fixed?”

Lu Yang nodded.

“Then have you ever considered how souls appeared in the ancient era, in other words, when the Reincarnation Rule still didn’t exist?”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. I’ve indeed never thought about something like this before.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “In the ancient era, as a fetus grew in the womb, it would automatically absorb the essence qi of heaven and earth, which would gather and form a soul. This essence qi is formless, intangible, imperceptible, and undetectable.

“The origin of souls has always been a mystery. After the five of us became immortals, we joined forces to deduce the truth and discovered a previously unknown substance called essence qi, which is the source of souls.

“The birth of souls can be regarded as a type of rule. Let’s call it the Soul Rule for now.

“If the Reincarnation Rule applies to everyone, it will inevitably clash with the Soul Rule. Creating a rule that conflicts with existing rules is a major taboo when forming a Dao Fruit. As long as the immortal wielding the Reincarnation Dao Fruit is not a fool, such a situation wouldn’t occur.”

Listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation, a question suddenly came to Lu Yang’s mind. “Immortal Fairy, can your Everlasting Rule apply to everyone?” If the Everlasting Rule can be extended to everyone, it would suggest that everyone can achieve eternal life—this is an irresistible temptation for the world.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gainsaid Lu Yang’s proposition. “I bore such an idea when I first formed the Everlasting Dao Fruit. At that time, I thought about how everyone was fighting for resources and struggling desperately to elevate their cultivation realms. Wasn’t it all for the sake of becoming an immortal and gaining eternal life?

“If I could let everyone live forever, wouldn’t the world be at peace?

“After I shared this idea with the other immortals, they reacted very strongly and came together to stop me, insisting that I mustn’t entertain such thoughts.”

Chapter 219: Second-In-Command of the Everlasting Lineage

“They stopped me for two reasons.

“The first reason was that people occupy resources not just to live but to live better.

“If everyone never dies and occupies a vast amount of resources, life will become very difficult for newborns. They would either have to fight and scheme against the old monsters or beseech them to spare a paltry amount of resources. As time goes on, each new generation will live more miserably. They’re born unable to enjoy a comfortable life but to suffer hardships. Eventually, the world will become a spiritless place.

“The second reason was that the lifespans of living beings are limited, which can also be viewed as a type of rule. If everyone gets to live forever, it will conflict with the ‘Lifespan Rule,’ shaking the foundation of the Everlasting Dao Fruit.

“I thought that while they weren’t as smart as me, these two points made quite a bit of sense, so I accepted them.

“That said, you don’t have to worry, Lu Yang. Although I can’t let everyone attain eternal life, I can give you an Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit. Granting you immortality is still possible.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy displayed her loyalty to friends. “So, what do you think? How about joining my Everlasting Lineage? Stick with me, and I’ll ensure that you get everything you want, be it riches or power!

“From this day forth, you’ll be the second-in-command of my Everlasting Lineage!”

“Before that, may I ask how many people there are in your Everlasting Lineage?” Lu Yang was cautious.

“Three people: me, you, and Bu Yaolian. Your status will be higher than Bu Yaolian since you’ll never die. Hehe, now you understand how precious this position is, right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinned foolishly.

The five ancient immortals had their trusted aides and disciples. While they were few, it was never the case that an immortal's lineage comprised only a single individual.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an exception. In reality, she was the only member of her lineage. Bu Yaolian was bamboozled by someone and forced to join the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s side. As for Lu Yang, he had just been dragged in by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Lu Yang fell silent for a few seconds, then shook his head firmly. “I will rely on my own efforts.”

“Tch, how boring.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, a little disappointed by Lu Yang’s decision. She really wanted to give Lu Yang an Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit and have him join her.

In the ancient era, countless people wanted to be accepted into the Everlasting Lineage, but I rejected all of them. As for those with ulterior motives, I didn’t even bother with them. From the ancient era until now, Lu Yang is the cultivator most to my liking. This is my first time inviting someone.

Unfortunately, I was rejected.

“Immortal Fairy, can you tell if Li Haoran has the Reincarnation Dao Fruit or the Incipient Reincarnation Dao Fruit?” This was Lu Yang’s priority at the moment.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “I can’t tell. This falls outside my area of expertise.”

“Alright then.”

~~~

Although the exchange between Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy might have seemed like it took a long time, time flowed much faster in the mental space than in the real world.

In reality, Li Haoran still staunchly believed that he had nothing to do with Qin Haoran. Just think about it. What would happen if I admit that I’m Qin Haoran’s reincarnation?

I’d gain a gorgeous, fairy-like wife at the Fusion Stage.

I’d gain a lively and adorable daughter.

I’d gain a constant flow of resources—spirit stones, pills, weapons, and natural treasures will no longer be a problem.

I’d gain a Fusion protector.

...It seems like admitting that I’m Qin Haoran’s reincarnation won’t be such a big deal after all?

No, no, I can’t think like that. I must consider the drawbacks too. Li Haoran contemplated for a long while.

It doesn’t seem like there are any real drawbacks.

“An alluring woman will disrupt my Dao heart! My goal is to become a cultivation genius like Senior Brother Lu, relying on talent and skill and cultivating to the highest realm without external help!”

Look at Senior Brother Lu. He’s roughly the same age as me, yet he has already climbed to the position of acting sect leader. Meanwhile, I can only eat soft rice and live off a woman.

“Forget it, we’ve been at this all day. Let’s rest for now.” Li Haoran’s parents reckoned they wouldn’t be coming to a resolution anytime soon, so they decided to put the matter aside for the time being.

“There are many guest rooms at home. Little Lu and Little Meng, since you came all the way from the Dao-Seeking Sect, do stay and enjoy a few more days in Luofeng Commandery. As for Yiren and Yanyan, you don’t have to stay at an inn. Stay here with us for now.”

Needless to say, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t refuse the kind gesture. After much persuasion from Su Yiren, Qin Yanyan also agreed to stay.

After a tiring afternoon, it was already time for dinner. If not for Qin Haoran’s matter, everyone would have gotten along quite well.

“Ah, we’ve been talking so long that I forgot to prepare dinner!” Li Haoran’s mother began to panic a little.

Lu Yang stopped her. “Just leave the cooking to us. Meng Jingzhou and I are known for our skills in the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Li Haoran’s mother was still a bit hesitant. Li Haoran was aware of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s abilities, so he convinced his mother.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou skillfully whipped out their tools from their identity jade tablets: barbeque grill, brushes, fans, skewers, meat, seasonings...and most important of all—the Automatic Skewering Array. This was a product of the latest research by Chefs Liu and Gao. Rising to the call of the Everlasting Immortal, they worked hard to expand the barbeque shop beyond the Dao-Seeking Sect, opening branches across the entire continent.

And what was the most important for a chain store? Of course, it was standardization and uniformity. Their starting point was the Automatic Skewering Array.

Qin Yanyan couldn’t stop her mouth from twitching as she watched by the side. I’ve long heard that the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect are multi-talented, and I thought that referred to their manifold cultivation skills.

But why is barbeque also considered one of them?

Moreover, according to Li Haoran’s introductions earlier, one of them is the personal disciple of the sect leader, and the other is the eldest son of the Meng Family. Both have exceptional status, yet they’re so down-to-earth and in touch with the common folks?

“True Fire?!” Qin Yanyan exclaimed in surprise when she saw Lu Yang spitting out True Fire. What’s True Fire? That’s a flame even Golden Core cultivators find challenging to control, its difficulty akin to reaching the sky.

Li Haoran snorted in contempt. “It’s not just any true fire. This is the very highly-ranked Three Esse True Fire! Do you know who Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng are? They’re the first and second in our cohort!”

Qin Yanyan widened her eyes. When she heard that Li Haoran was ranked fifth in his cohort, she assumed that it was because his abilities were lacking. However, after exchanging blows with him, she had to admit that she wouldn’t have been able to defeat Li Haoran even without his wig.

At that time, I was already wondering. If Li Haoran only ranks fifth despite such abilities, what kind of monsters are the top four?

Now I know.

Li Haoran’s mother was also surprised. No wonder I find Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou so pleasing to the eye.

“Haoran, look at how they cultivate! Lu Yang must be getting up every day before the sky turns bright to practice. Now, look at you, always slacking off on your studies and not cultivating properly. When I’m not around, you must be sleeping until the sun shines on your butt. If you just put in half the effort Lu Yang does...”

Li Haoran’s face darkened. Had I known, I wouldn’t have brought Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng along.

Besides, what did you just say? They are diligent in their cultivation my ass! We are all at the same age and know one another well. Our schedules are not that different, okay?

Chapter 220: Overcast and Clear Skies

As the founders of “One More Time” Barbeque Shop, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s skills would naturally be no letdown. This was already evident back in Yanjiang Commandery. Now that Lu Yang had mastered the Three Flavored True Fire, his abilities had risen to a new level.

Among the Foundation Establishment cultivators, Lu Yang was confident that no one could rival him—in terms of barbeque skills.

As Lu Yang shook the skewers, the cumin and chili powder rolled between the pieces of meat. Seared by the fire, the flavors were completely released, making even someone like Qin Yanyan, who preferred a lighter palate, involuntarily swallow her saliva.

“Come, it’s ready!” Lu Yang placed two large handfuls of skewers onto the barbeque grill with a loud and hefty thud.

Meng Jingzhou wasn’t idle either. He kept flipping the roasted potato slices, leeks, and tofu, each emitting a tantalizing aroma that was no less enticing than Lu Yang’s.

“Delicious!” Li Haoran’s parents were impressed upon digging into a few skewers. As expected of model students. Not only do they have high cultivation, but their culinary skills are also amazing. Li Haoran can’t compare to them at all.

“I’ll have a skewer too!” Li Haoran had long heard of the legends of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s barbeque, but he didn’t have the chance to try them yet.

These are the barbeque skewers so delicious that they brought down the entire Everlasting Creed.

“Delicious!” Li Haoran’s eyes lit up. This is the best barbeque skewer I’ve ever tasted.

Qin Yanyan and Su Yiren nibbled reservedly at the beginning, but as the atmosphere became livelier, they loosened up and enjoyed their meal heartily.

Watching everyone eat to their heart’s content, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was drooling with envy. In her soul form, she had no sense of taste and couldn’t eat. “Lu Yang, let me use your body. I want to eat a couple of skewers too,” she discussed with Lu Yang.

Lu Yang didn’t mind and generously gave control of his body to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The latter happily took over and ate with gusto, not showing any self-restraint.

“Haha, Senior Brother Lu, you’ve loosened up too!” Li Haoran laughed. Senior Brother Lu was eating in a more elegant manner moments ago, but he’s now like a different person, wolfing down the skewers and downing the bamboo juice in large gulps.

There were many red-leaf bamboo forests in the mountains near Luofeng Commandery, and their bamboo juice was clear and sweet. Many tourists here would savor its refreshing fragrance.

Lu Yang sighed. You’re an immortal fairy, you know? Can’t you show a bit more restraint?

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others also advised me to speak as little as possible in front of others. They even said that after much effort, they had finally improved the external world’s impression of immortals, and they warned me not to ruin it.

“But there are no outsiders here, are there?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t consider Lu Yang an outsider.

Lu Yang retorted in rage, “But the problem is that you’re using my body!”

“Aiya, why draw such a clear line between what’s yours and mine?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy demonstrated her magnanimity. “When I find my inheritance in the future, I’ll share half of it with you.”

Lu Yang remembered that when he first met the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, she had claimed that she’d buried immortal treasures on the North Star, all of which were her prized possessions.

Based on my understanding of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, there’s probably nothing good in there.

“If worse comes to worst, I’ll impart you a few immortal-level culinary skills.” The Everlasting treated the second-in-command of her Everlasting Lineage as her successor.

Lu Yang rolled his eyes and didn’t respond to her.

Casting aside this small exchange that only the two were privy to, everyone was content with the meal.

Li Haoran’s parents had arranged the respective rooms for their guests.

After Lu Yang washed up, he took out a half-human-sized pillow from his identity jade tablet. It was Lu Yang’s bolster; he liked to hug something while sleeping. With over a decade of sleep experience, Lu Yang could sleep well anywhere, never picky about his sleeping location.

~~~

Early the next morning, Lu Yang woke up to find that he had kicked his bolster to the foot of the bed, which made it look rather forlorn.

“This little lass Su Yiren is thoughtful,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remarked.

“What do you mean?”

“While you were sleeping, she set up an array in the courtyard. It’s not much use to you, but for Li Haoran’s parents, it can allow them to subconsciously cultivate, infusing them with spirit energy to enhance their cultivation. However, this will take a very long time to show any results, so Li Haoran’s parents won’t notice it now.”

Walking out of his room, Lu Yang stretched lazily. The weather is not bad; an overcast day. Nice and cool.

Compared to sunny days and clear skies, Lu Yang preferred cloudy days and overcast skies.

He saw Li Haoran practicing his punches and meditating in the courtyard.

“Junior Brother Li is so hardworking even at home?” Lu Yang was astounded. I thought I’d woken up early enough. I didn’t expect Li Haoran to have gotten up even earlier, and he’s already cultivating.

Though I don’t remember him being this diligent when we were at the Dao-Seeking Sect?

Li Haoran wore a solemn expression as he transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang. “Senior Brother Lu, that’s because you don’t know. Don’t be fooled by how delighted my parents were when I came home yesterday. Based on my experience, after a night’s sleep, the sense of novelty would have worn off for them by the next day. That’s when they’ll lecture me and upbraid me for doing nothing but eating and sleeping at home and living a very decadent life.

“Rather than suffering from their tirade, I might as well take action first and pretend to be industrious. Anyway, I’ll just do this for a bit in the morning, then go out to play later in the day. They won’t bother me then.”

Lu Yang felt like he had seen the light. I’ve never realized that there’s so much knowledge and depth to this.

What Li Haoran didn’t mention was that if Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou hadn’t come, his parents would have spoiled him for a couple more days. Now that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou are here, the time they’ll pamper me will be cut short drastically!

“Haoran, you’re up so early?” Li Haoran’s mother noticed that Li Haoran was already cultivating early in the morning, with Lu Yang standing nearby with a wide smile.

It must be Lu Yang getting Haoran to join him in cultivating.

Li Haoran, “...”

He really wanted to say, “Mom, me ranking fifth in this cohort of the Dao-Seeking Sect is genuinely no small feat.”

This was not false. With Li Haoran’s talent, he could have been the undisputed first place in any first-class or ultra first-class sects. Even in the past few cohorts of the Dao-Seeking Sect, he could have also ranked in the top three.

Unfortunately, there are too many monsters in this particular cohort.

During breakfast, Su Yiren ate silently, not bringing up the array she had set up in the courtyard last night. It seemed like she didn’t want others to know about it. If not for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang wouldn’t have known either.

Li Haoran beckoned to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “Come, I’ll take you around the commandery!” After some thought, he also invited Qin Yanyan and Su Yiren.

“I only asked you along because you’re guests. Don’t overthink it,” Li Haoran said to Su Yiren.

Even so, Su Yiren smiled very brightly.

The group got ready and was about to set off when the overcast weather grew even more gloomy. The layers of clouds thickened, and the faint rumble of thunder could be heard in the distance.

“It’s going to rain.” Li Haoran looked up at the sky, a bit disappointed. Luofeng Commandery had much rainfall, and judging by how dark the sky was, a downpour seemed inevitable. “Looks like we won’t be able to go out today.”

Hearing his words, Su Yiren struck toward the sky with her palm. The oppressive tenebrous clouds instantly dissipated, replaced by a bright clear sky.

She smiled gently as if nothing had just happened. “It’s sunny now. Let’s head out.”

Li Haoran, “...”

Chapter 221: Phoenix Blood Stone

On the streets, a group of men and women drew the attention of passers-by. The two women, one mature and the other younger, were particularly striking. Each radiated the unique charm of her age, as if embodying the peak of their respective stages of life, stirring the imaginations of those around them.

The one who drew the most envy was the man walking between the other two women. Despite his nondescript appearance and mere Foundation Establishment cultivation, the older beauty was clinging to his arm.

Li Haoran kept his face devoid of expression. Don’t be fooled by how weak and delicate Su Yiren appears. She’s a bona fide Fusion cultivator. If she wants to cling to me, there’s no way I can break free.

He calmly turned his head to meet Su Yiren’s gaze. “I know you’re excited about strolling the streets with me, but please control your strength. This is the third time you’ve broken my arm.” Li Haoran swayed his arm a little to signify the severity of his injury.

Su Yiren hastily retrieved a healing pill from her storage ring and began setting his bones back in place.

At Su Yiren’s cultivation realm, she shouldn’t have lost control of her strength; Li Haoran could only attribute it to her being overly thrilled to be with him.

“Your bones broke, yet you didn’t even make a sound?” Qin Yanyan stared at Li Haoran in shock. Does this man not feel pain?

Li Haoran chuckled dryly. “Ever since I spent a year soaking in lava, I haven’t known what pain is.” Reminded of the time his master had thrown him into lava upon joining the sect, Li Haoran felt that he had survived due to pure luck.

“La-lava? Soak? A year?” Qin Yanyan’s eyes widened. Are you still human?

Li Haoran replied in a wistful tone. “Back when I first entered the lava, I screamed my lungs out because the pain was too unbearable for any human. By the end, my voice was hoarse, but it still hurt.

“My shifu didn’t allow anyone to help me and demanded that I endure it by myself. At that time, Senior Sister Zhou Lulu couldn’t bear to see me suffer and secretly snuck me a cup of water infused with rare natural treasures, saying that it could alleviate my situation.”

Upon trying to imagine what it was like soaking in lava, Qin Yanyan shuddered. She couldn’t help but ask, “Did it help you adapt to the lava faster?”

“It was century-old arhat fruit[1] water. She noticed that I had gone hoarse from yelling, so she brought it to soothe my throat.

Qin Yanyan, “...”

Ever since Lu Yang learned that Fifth Elder Zhou Xin had made Li Haoran soak in lava for a year, he no longer felt that Yun Zhi giving him a boiling water bath was any big deal.

That said, if Li Haoran hadn’t had a Fire Spirit Root, Fifth Elder wouldn’t have dared to toss him inside the lava. This was a training method unique to those with a Fire Spirit Root.

Each Single Spirit Root of the five elements had its exclusive cultivation method. For example, those with a Fire Spirit Root would soak in lava or get burned by fire, allowing them to comprehend spells or abilities related to fire. In Li Haoran’s case, he comprehended the art of refining artifacts.

Those with an Earth Spirit Root would be buried in the earth, enabling them to comprehend the Earth Escape Technique.

Those with a Water Spirit Root would comprehend the Water Control Technique.

However, there were also exceptions.

For instance, Lu Yang heard that Dai Bufan possessed a Water Spirit Root. First Elder had hurled him into a pool to prevent him from breathing, hoping that he would comprehend the Water Control Technique or water-breathing spells through this life-and-death situation. Unfortunately, things didn’t go according to one’s wishes. Dai Bufan comprehended a spatial spell and drank all the water from the pool.

“Good niece, see anything you like? Your uncle will buy it for you,” Meng Jingzhou teased Qin Yanyan. I might not have much of anything else, but I certainly have much money.

When Qin Yanyan heard Meng Jingzhou calling herself “niece,” she stomped her feet furiously but couldn’t do anything about it.

“What is this?” Qin Yanyan tried to shift the topic and randomly pointed to stones peddled at the roadside.

The stones were blood-red, bright, and lustrous as if they were naturally formed, refracting mesmerizing rays under the sun.

“Oh, this? They’re Phoenix Blood Stones, a specialty of Luofeng Commandery.”

“Phoenix Blood Stone?” Everyone present, except Su Yiren, had never heard of such a stone.

Li Haoran explained, “You probably have heard of the history of Luofeng Commandery. It is said that a long long time ago, there was a pure-blooded phoenix that freely soared through the heavens and earth. However, it grew too old and could no longer fly, so it found a place to rest. It planned to sleep for a while, but it never woke up.

“The bones and flesh of the old phoenix transformed into the hills of the land.” Li Haoran pointed to the almost imperceptible mountain range that surrounded Luofeng[2] Commandery in the distance. “Look at those mountains. Don’t they look like a phoenix?

“The old phoenix’s feathers morphed into the trees, which is why there are many red-colored vegetation on the hills. Its blood also stained the stones red, and those are the Phoenix Blood Stones we see now.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Is this a phoenix or Pangu? [3]

“When I heard this story as a child, I thought it was just a legend. It wasn’t until I came to the Dao-Seeking Sect and my shifu taught me about refining artifacts that I realized that the Phoenix Blood Stones from my hometown were truly stained with the blood of the phoenix and that these stones were excellent materials for forging artifacts.”

“Phoenix, huh...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed to be reminded of something upon hearing the term again after a long time. “Back then, it wasn’t just Qilin but also the Dragon and Phoenix tribes that had individuals who could become immortals. At that time, two demon prodigies meticulously groomed by the Dragon and Phoenix tribes demonstrated unparalleled talent. Moreover, with the support of the two big clans, their chances of becoming immortals were very high.

“In contrast, Qilin was said to be the favored child of heaven and earth, but he had no actual foundation and was left to his own devices. Most demon tribes didn’t have any high hopes for him.

“Qilin once faced many formidable enemies, but none were his match. Defeating numerous opponents that should have been impossible for him, he rapidly rose within the demon race. The ideology of his Dao Fruit was very similar to that of the prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes. If he wanted to ascend to an immortal, a deadly battle would be inevitable.

“As Qilin carried great fortune, he took on two opponents at once and defeated the two prodigies, successfully proving himself and attaining a Dao Fruit. That was how he became the Qilin Immortal.”

Lu Yang asked, “Did the Qilin Immortal kill those two prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes?” Despite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s impassive tone, he could sense the underlying cruelty in it. Indeed, becoming an immortal is no playing house. The winner takes all, while the vanquished loses everything, including their lives.

“No, they got married.”

“Huh?”

“Demons admire the strong. After the prodigies lost to the Qilin Immortal, they fell in love with him. In the end, the three got married. I originally wanted to attend the Qilin Immortal’s wedding, but he said that I was too pretty and that my presence would overshadow them, so he didn’t let me go.

“What a pity. I was even planning to show off a little at the Qilin Immortal’s wedding.”

Lu Yang asked warily, “What were you planning to do?”

“Prepare the banquet, of course! Let me tell you, the Qilin Immortal and the other immortals can’t even tell grains apart. I’m the only one who could cook,” the Everlasting Immortal commented with disdain, finding the other immortals too disgraceful.

Lu Yang thought, It makes sense that the Qilin Immortal didn’t invite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He’d definitely invite lots of guests to the wedding. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were to be in charge of meal preparation, there might not be sufficient antidote for everyone.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Later, I thought that since it was a friend’s wedding after all, it wouldn’t be proper not to send a gift, so I gave them an immortal fruit that I had blessed. I even thoughtfully included a heartfelt message which wrote ‘For the Most Beautiful Demon.’

“I heard that this gift caused quite a commotion. That was probably because they had never seen such a precious gift before.”

Lu Yang fell silent for a few seconds before questioning, “How many immortal fruits did you give them?”

“One.”

Lu Yang let out a long sigh. “You really wish for the whole world to be in chaos, huh?”

“Ah? Why?”

1. Often referred to as “monk fruit,” “luohan fruit” or “luohan-guo,” it is commonly used in Traditional Chinese Medicine. It has plenty of health benefits, but it’s most well-known for its throat-soothing properties. ☜

2. Just a reminder that “Luofeng” means something like “descending phoenix” and sounds like a place where a phoenix chose to settle. ☜

3. This was explained in the thoughts section under an earlier chapter (Chapter 16), but basically, Pangu is the “first god” in Chinese creation myths, and various parts of his body formed the land. ☜

Chapter 222: Evil Ancient Mastermind Huang Doudou

“Immortal Fairy, why didn’t you give at least two immortal fruits then?” Lu Yang could roughly imagine the uproar caused by the immortal fruit.

The more time he spent with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the less he couldn’t figure out the reason she was killed—there were too many reasons that Lu Yang didn’t know which to choose.

“I already said, it’s for the ‘most beautiful’ demon. ‘Most’ can only apply to one individual, don’t you know that?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy earnestly taught Lu Yang some basic grammar.

Lu Yang remained silent for a long time before replying, “...You make a point.”

“Right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips, pleased with herself.

“So who did you give the immortal fruit to?”

“After the incident, I heard from the Epoch Immortal about what happened at the wedding. The prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes respectively quarrelled over who should own the immortal fruit, and they wanted to decide through a duel.

“Speaking of which, the Qilin Immortal was really stingy. He had an immortal fruit too. Couldn’t he have just given one to each of his wives? Why did they still fight?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. Compared to the Qilin Immortal, I’m much more generous. I could offer an immortal fruit as a gift.

“What happened afterward?”

“Later, the Qilin Immortal said that a duel at the wedding would be inappropriate, so he suggested another form of competition. Since there happened to be three immortal guests present, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, Nine-Layers Immortal, and Epoch Immortal could act as judges, while he would not participate to avoid a tie.

“Look, if the Qilin Immortal had invited me, couldn’t the five of us immortals be the judges? Besides, you know me. I’m fair and impartial. I could also have been the only judge.

“If they were worried about me being too beautiful and stealing the limelight of the two prodigies, I could’ve worn a veil!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was very confident about her appearance. I’m the first among the top ten beauties of the ancient era after all.

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Immortal Fairy, please use your head more. It’s obvious that the Qilin Immortal didn’t want to be a judge so he deliberately removed himself from the equation.

“What did the prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes compete in?”

“Culinary skills.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proceeded to shake her head regretfully. “The Qilin Immortal and others didn’t know that I had imparted the two prodigies their culinary skills. Although I bore no formal title as shifu, they were still my students. Unfortunately, they didn’t learn well and only picked up about one-tenth of my skills. Despite that, they were still unmatched among those at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“During the competition, since they were both taught by the same shifu, neither could outdo the other. Thus, it was naturally difficult to judge who was better.

“The Epoch Immortal told me that when the three of them tasted the meals prepared by the two prodigies, the food was so stunning it could stun the heavens, and they felt like the food encompassed the power of time, making them rapidly reflect on their entire lives.

“I humbly mentioned that I was the one who taught them, but they only managed to learn a fraction of my skills.

“Then, the Epoch Immortal was silent for a while before saying that they had beaten the Qilin Immortal too early and that he was not the true culprit. I asked him what he meant by that, but he didn’t answer me.”

In his mind, Lu Yang cupped his fists to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to show his respect.

If others heard this story and didn’t know the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it wouldn’t be their fault if they assumed that she was the ‘Evil Mastermind of the Ancient Era’. Without being present and with just a single immortal fruit, she caused the prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes to break out in a fight, caused the four ancient immortals to turn against one another, and caused the Qilin Immortal to be viewed as heartless and unloyal. She even secretly imparted her skills to the two prodigies, waiting for the perfect chance to strike.

Such wisdom could only be described as unfathomable. Anyone facing such a scheming old monster would only shudder in fear.

However, Lu Yang knew the Everlasting Immortal Fairy very well, so he decided to opt for another expression to describe the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s wisdom—the foolish appears to be wise.[1]

~~~

“You should know that the Dragon and Phoenix tribes are the proudest among the demons. Their blood is incredibly valuable, and it’s almost as hard as reaching the heavens for humans to obtain them. That’s why the Phoenix Blood Stones are so precious. Not only are they a specialty of Luofeng Commandery, but they also serve as a cornerstone industry of our economy. We gain an immense number of spirit stones from selling Phoenix Blood Stones every year!

“Phoenix Blood Stones are great materials for refining artifacts, and they can also be used as ornaments, granting marvelous effects when one wears them for a long time. I heard from my dad that the mining of Phoenix Blood Stones has a history of four thousand years, and the ore veins are still not exhausted. There’s still a steady supply of Phoenix Blood Stones.”

As Li Haoran introduced his hometown’s economy, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou kept nodding, as if they were officials here to inspect the place.

“How many spirit stones does this Phoenix Blood Stone cost?” Meng Jingzhou picked one Phoenix Blood Stone from the shop. Finding the item rare, he figured he’d buy a few to play with.

“Three hundred spirit stones.”

“What about this one?”

“Four hundred fifty spirit stones.”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head. Such cheap Phoenix Blood Stones are beneath my status.

“Bring out your best Phoenix Blood Stones. Money is not a problem.” Meng Jingzhou put on the airs of a young master.

The shopkeeper’s eyes lit up. This is a big customer!

Looking around, he saw that Meng Jingzhou and company were the only people in the shop, so he led them to the backyard. He carefully took an exquisite wooden box off the shelf and opened it. Resting inside was a bright red stone the size of an egg. Its garishly red hue looked as if it was stained by the blood of the old phoenix that died in the legends.

Even Qin Yanyan could sense that this was an extraordinary piece of Phoenix Blood Stone.

The shopkeeper whispered, “A few days ago, the mine collapsed. This is the last Phoenix Blood Stone transported out from the mine. I went through a lot to get my hands on it. The fixed price is five hundred thousand spirit stones; no more, no less.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. That’s more like it. “I’ll take ten.” The difference between five hundred thousand and five million spirit stones was not worth mentioning for the eldest son of the Meng Family.

The shopkeeper looked a little distressed. “Dear customer, it’s not that I don’t want to sell more. It’s just that I only have this one piece of Phoenix Blood Stone.”

“Alright then, I’ll just take this one.”

The shopkeeper was elated. In fact, he had set the price a bit high to leave room for bargaining. He didn’t expect Meng Jingzhou to buy it outright. He even gifted Meng Jingzhou a few other decent Blood Phoenix Stones, though they were far inferior to the one Meng Jingzhou had purchased.

Although Meng Jingzhou knew that he could have haggled, he always found it too troublesome. He simply asked the shopkeeper to make a hole in the Phoenix Blood Stone and thread it with a string. Wearing it around his neck, Meng Jingzhou felt quite satisfied with himself.

However, since everyone had come out to shop together, he figured he couldn’t buy the Phoenix Blood Stone only for himself. He browsed several more shops, hoping to purchase Phoenix Blood Stones of a similar quality for everyone else. Unfortunately, none of the stones matched up to his one. Many shopkeepers asked Meng Jingzhou where he had procured his, but he didn’t tell them.

“Why is it so hard to spend money?”

Li Haoran advised, “Forget it, Senior Brother Meng. The phoenix power contained in these Phoenix Blood Stones isn’t of much use to us. Even when it comes to crafting artifacts, I currently don’t have the skills to refine a Phoenix Blood Stone of such high quality. Buying them would be pointless.”

“Fine then.” Meng Jingzhou had no choice but to give up. “By the way, what are the effects of wearing a Phoenix Blood Stone for a long time?” Meng Jingzhou pointed to the one hung in front of his chest.

“It boosts one’s yang virility.”

1. There are two versions of this idiom. One mentions that the wise appears to be foolish (大智若愚), and the second one was derived from the first version, and it’s also the one used in this novel (大愚若智). The meaning becomes the opposite just by switching the second and fourth characters. ☜

Chapter 223: That Thing

The Meng Family, one of the most prestigious clans of the Central Continent, had a history that spanned a hundred thousand years and was known for their refined upbringing. As the eldest son of the main branch, Meng Jingzhou carried himself with poise; he naturally wouldn’t be displeased with Li Haoran because of trivial matters.

Meng Jingzhou looked at Li Haoran and said dispiritedly, “Next time, can you tell me earlier when something is for...boosting one’s yang virility?”

Li Haoran responded with an “oh.” He then recalled something and added, “Shifu told me that soaking in lava long-term can also boost one’s yang. This was one of my main motivations for persevering through it. The results have proven itself to be rather effective.”

“...Can we move on from this yang-boosting topic?”

“Alright.”

~~~

By the time Lu Yang’s group returned to the Li estate, Li Haoran’s parents had already prepared a sumptuous dinner for everyone. After all, she couldn’t let their guests, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, cook every day.

Meng Jingzhou had purchased a heap of items. Essentially, he would buy anything he had never seen before. Their utility was secondary—the most important factor was novelty.

Of course, he didn’t buy items that challenged his intelligence. One example was a product that claimed to be four thousand years old, dating back to the same era as the old phoenix. It was said to have witnessed the entire process of the old phoenix’s fall; the product was “pure natural spirit qi.”

Lu Yang purchased a phoenix accessory with exquisite craftsmanship and tied it together with his identity jade pendant at his waist.

Qin Yanyan bought a crate of bamboo juice, having enjoyed Luofeng Commandery’s specialty drink last night while eating barbeque.

Su Yiren got nothing. As a Fusion cultivator, there was nothing worth her interest in Luofeng Commandery, unless it was the corpse of the old phoenix.

“Mom, I didn’t know you have such skills.” Li Haoran’s mouth was agape at the lavish spread on the table. In my memory, Mom has never been able to make so many delicious dishes.

Li Haoran’s mother smiled. “I just learned them. While you were away, I had nothing much to do, so I figured I might as well pick up something new.”

Li Haoran’s father interjected, “What your mom just learned is how to buy dishes from the Old Restaurant.”

Li Haoran’s mother glowered at her husband.

Li Haoran, “...”

The Old Restaurant needed no further elaboration; their dishes were naturally brilliant. Although it was rare for Lu Yang to see century-old establishments in his past life, they were commonplace across the Central Continent.

However, shops merely a hundred years old were not qualified as “old.” To earn the title, a shop must have a history of at least five hundred years.

The Old Restaurant was a thousand-year-old establishment, having seen countless batches of staff come and go. Yet, its owner had never changed, preserving their original recipes and flavors. The oldest thing in the Old Restaurant was neither their recipe nor the furniture but the owner himself.

“What? you’re saying that the food tasted different when you ate here as a child?” If someone were to hurl such a remark, the Old Restaurant could respond, “Well, I was the one who cooked the food you ate back then!”

After dinner, Lu Yang consulted Su Yiren on forming a golden core.

“Form a golden core?” Su Yiren didn’t expect Lu Yang to ask her something like this. Didn’t Haoran say that he’s the fourth disciple of the sect leader? Why not ask the sect leader directly? As a fellow Fusion cultivator, the sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect definitely has more substance than I do.

Lu Yang had to choose his words wisely. I can’t possibly say that my shifu is a whimsical and eccentric dude who goes out every day to tell stories and hardly taught me anything. “Shifu’s heart is preoccupied with the world and has no time to spare for me.”

“I see.” Su Yiren nodded, believing Lu Yang’s explanation.

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes at the side.

Since Meng Jingzhou and Li Haoran were also around, they listened to Su Yiren’s elucidation of golden core formation.

“In my opinion, the most integral aspect of forming a golden core is one’s fortuitous opportunities. My talent is quotidian, and my greatest aspiration was to form a second-grade golden core. This is already the best outcome I can hope for.

“In order to form a second-grade golden core, I tried everything I could to comprehend: venturing deep into the mountain forest to battle demon beasts, sitting on a boulder and allowing the waterfall to wash down on me, and observing the myriad facets of the mortal realm to comprehend the mundane atmosphere... However, everything failed.

“One day, after I finished my cultivation practice, I lay at the edge of the cliff, gazing up at the starry sky, feeling infinitesimal in this world. It was then that an inexplicable comprehension surged into me. I seized this opportunity to gather qi and condense it into a golden core. The result was a first-grade golden core that was full and lustrous.

“When I stopped pursuing it deliberately instead, I achieved enlightenment. I’ve discussed my insights with several fellow Daoists, and there were two who had similar experiences.”

Lu Yang felt inspired and expressed his gratitude to Su Yiren.

~~~

In the middle of the night, Lu Yang opened his eyes, uncertain of the exact hour.

“You’re awake? I was just about to call you.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not surprised that Lu Yang had woken up.

Lu Yang frowned. In his sleep, he had sensed someone secretly sneaking into Li Haoran’s house.

What is their objective?

“Two people, both at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy informed him.

Lu Yang was baffled. Li Haoran’s parents are only at the Foundation Establishment Stage; they’re not rich either. What’s there in Li Haoran’s house that could possibly attract Golden Core cultivators?

Could it be the Phoenix Blood Stone that Meng Jingzhou had bought?

Lu Yang was not worried about potential danger. Even if Su Yiren didn’t take action, he was confident that he and Meng Jingzhou could handle these two uninvited guests with ease.

“Sir Lu, Sir Meng, you’re awake?” Su Yiren’s voice echoed in Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s minds.

Li Haoran and Qin Yanyan were still inexperienced and didn’t possess the same vigilance as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Just woke up,” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou replied. “Senior Su, what’s the situation now?”

Su Yiren shook her head. “I don’t know much. All I can make out is that two Intermediate Golden Core cultivators have infiltrated the house. They’re acting suspiciously, and I’m not sure what they’re after. My instinct tells me that there’s someone behind them. I want to capture them, but I’m afraid I might alert them.”

“That’s not an issue. Senior Su, you just have to bring up the rear.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickly hatched a plan.

Under Su Yiren’s curious gaze, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou changed into their night stealth attire with much familiarity and sneakily exited the house.

The two Golden Core cultivators seemed to be searching for something, but they dared not use their spiritual consciousness for fear of being detected. They heard that there was a genius in this house who was a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Unless necessary, they mustn’t let the Dao-Seeking Sect find out about their matters.

They assumed that they were very secretive, but in reality, they had already attracted many watchful gazes. Suddenly, they sensed danger approaching. Swiftly dodging, they naturally evaded Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s attacks.

“Didn’t expect you to dodge this attack. Not too bad.” Lu Yang sneered as he transmitted an auditory message through his spiritual consciousness.

“Who are you?! What are you doing in the Li Family?” the two Golden Core cultivators responded.

“Heh, you’re asking the obvious. Since we have bumped into each other in the Li Estate, what else could it be? We’re here to find that thing, of course!” Meng Jingzhou laughed nonchalantly, as if he was mocking the two for asking a dumb question. “As for who we are, who else do you think could know about this?”

The two Golden Core cultivators widened their eyes. “How did you know?!”

“The wind will eventually penetrate all walls; nothing can stay a secret forever. No matter how you hide it, we’ll still find out what needs to be known.” Lu Yang chuckled. “Did you think you were the only ones who paid attention to that thing?”

“Damn it! How did the Mo Family learn about the Phoenix Blood Stone?!” The two Golden Core cultivators quickly deduced Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s “identities.”

They must be from the Mo Family, our opponents!

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances with each other. This is indeed caused by the Blood Phoenix Stone we brought back.

Realizing that their cover was blown, the two Golden Core cultivators quickly dealt a few moves before seizing a chance to escape. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou pursued them with all their might, only to be discomfited by their inability to keep up.

Noticing that they had shaken their pursuers off, the two Golden Core cultivators rushed back to report the situation.

“Senior Su, if we follow them, we’ll be able to find out who’s behind this,” Lu Yang said as he hastened his pace to tail the two cultivators secretly.

Su Yiren wore a rather odd expression. Why do the two of you seem so experienced in such matters?

Chapter 224: This Bit of Spirit Stones Might Not Be Enough

The two Golden Core cultivators weaved in and out of the buildings in Luofeng Commandery, clearly having committed the paths to memory. At night, Luofeng Commandery would dispatch cultivators to patrol the streets, but these two ingeniously avoided the patrol routes.

Just then, Li Haoran was woken up by Su Yiren. Listening to the brief summary of events from his fiancée, an odd expression crept onto his visage.

“Senior Brother Meng has finally become a target after flaunting his wealth?”

“What do you mean flaunting my wealth? Why am I not allowed to tell others that I have money?” Meng Jingzhou glared at him. As the young master of the Meng Family, who dared target my things when I was in the imperial city?

Su Yiren led the three in secretly tailing the two Golden Core cultivators. While navigating the rooftops, Lu Yang noticed from the corner of his eye that other silhouettes were doing the same in the distance.

“Is Luofeng Commandery always so lively at night?” He initially wanted to head in their direction to investigate, but he saw that the two Golden Core cultivators had vaulted over a high wall and entered the courtyard of a residence, so he could only focus on the task at hand for now.

“I remember that this place is...the Commandery Governor Estate?” Li Haoran was a bit hesitant, uncertain if he had remembered wrongly. A Phoenix Blood Stone worth five hundred thousand spirit stones is indeed precious, but it’s not enough to tempt a commandery governor.

Unless there’s more to the Phoenix Blood Stone Senior Brother Meng had bought.

As an array enveloped the high-walled courtyard, recklessly entering without the appropriate method would alert those inside.

Su Yiren ignored the array and successfully led the trio inside.

~~~

“Patriarch, we have returned.” The two Golden Core cultivators respectfully greeted a middle-aged man who stood with his hands behind his back.

Since Li Haoran had never met the commandery governor before, he couldn’t ascertain if this middle-aged man was the commandery governor or someone like a steward.

The middle-aged man gave a soft affirmative. “Did you get that thing?”

The two cultivators were quite ashamed. “We encountered an unexpected situation. Worried that we might make too much commotion, we didn’t continue to steal that thing.”

“Unexpected situation?”

“Yes, we encountered others trying to steal the same thing at Li Haoran’s house. Although they didn’t reveal their identities, I suspect they were sent by the Mo Family.”

“What happened? Explain in detail.”

The two recounted the situation with all the details, but to their surprise, the patriarch was incensed. “Hmph, you were tricked! The people you encountered were not from the Mo Family but disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect!

“If I’m not wrong, they’re currently eavesdropping from the rooftop!

“I’ve already said so much, so you might as well come out. We can have an open discussion.”

Li Haoran’s heart skipped a beat. Just as he was about to reveal himself, Lu Yang pulled him back. Lu Yang shook his head and remained quiet.

The patriarch waited for a long time, but no one appeared. “Looks like those people are indeed from the Mo Family. As I thought, the Mo Family has also learned about the existence of that thing.”

It was just a casual bluff that he had thrown out earlier.

He had heard from his subordinates yesterday that three Foundation Establishment disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect had come to Luofeng Commandery, with a local among them. However, he didn’t take it to heart.

Unexpectedly, his subordinates reported to him this afternoon that one of the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples had purchased an extremely rare Phoenix Blood Stone and was searching other shops for similar ones. When he heard the description of the Phoenix Blood Stone, his heart almost stopped beating for a moment; he suspected that it was the problematic Phoenix Blood Stone.

He couldn’t let this fall into the hands of the Dao-Seeking Sect. It would be disastrous if they discovered something was wrong. Thus, he dispatched two subordinates to steal the Phoenix Blood Stone, but that was when they ran into the Mo Family.

The Mo Family was the largest family in Luofeng Commandery and were at odds with him; they had been eagerly waiting for a hold on him to bring him—the commandery governor—down.

“Tsk, I wonder how that thing ended up outside. Have you asked the shopowner?”

“He’s no longer around. According to the shop assistants, the shopowner earned a hefty sum of money and took his wife and children out on a trip. They won’t be back for a while, and only a few assistants are left to look after the shop.”

“So envious.”

“Ah, what did you just say, Patriarch?”

“Nothing.”

The commandery governor thought, Once this job is done, I also want to take my wife and children to travel to other places.

“How’s the situation at the mines? When will the job be completed? We can’t keep using the excuse of the mine’s collapse to stop the miners from going in.” The excuse of the mine collapsing could only delay things for a while. After all, in the cultivation world, a few high-level cultivators could easily create a new tunnel to the mine.

The commandery governor himself was one example. In just half a day, he could break open a new tunnel to the mine. For now, he had announced to the public that something had gone wrong during his cultivation, and that he wouldn’t be able to act for half a month.

“They said they still need three more days.”

“Get them to speed up! But make sure it’s kept secret. No outsiders must know of this. This matter doesn’t only affect us but the whole of the Phoenix Tribe’s interests!”

“Yes!”

Lu Yang and the other three were taken aback. From what the commandery governor just said, it sounds like he’s colluding with the Phoenix Tribe?

With the imminent arrival of the Great Era, the overt and covert struggles of various factions on the Central Continent had intensified, including the conflict between the Central Continent and the demon tribes. Some demons wanted to start a war with the Great Xia Dynasty, while others hoped to ease the relationship with the Great Xia Dynasty and face the crisis of the Great Era together. As such, the demon tribes were divided into the pro-war and pro-peace factions.

“I wonder which faction the Dragon and Phoenix tribes belong to.” Lu Yang had heard that the demon tribes had dispatched many spies to infiltrate the Central Continent with the intention of secretly causing trouble.

“Also, do you know what to do with them after this is completed?” The commandery governor wore an expression of reluctance, as though he had no other choice.

The two Golden Core cultivators froze, but killing intent soon appeared in their eyes. “Are you saying that...these few days will count as overtime and that we should pay them triple the usual wages?”

“Yes.” The commandery governor turned around. When he saw the gazes of the two cultivators, he froze for a moment.

“Why are you looking at me like that?”

The two Golden Core cultivators spoke with a trace of bitterness. “Patriarch, you’ve never said anything about paying us overtime for night shifts, just like tonight.” Even if Golden Core cultivators don’t need to sleep, you can’t let us work successive day and night shifts without resting, right?

My wife is still waiting for me in bed.

Why do others get paid for overtime, but we have to work for free?

“...I’ll also give you overtime pay.”

“Patriarch, what should we do about that Phoenix Blood Stone?”

“Hmph, since we can’t do it secretly, we’ll do it openly. The two of you will pretend to be merchants tomorrow. Say that the Phoenix Blood Stone is rare and offer a handsome sum to buy it!”

“And how much is that?”

“One million spirit stones!” The commandery governor was convinced that the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect wouldn’t be able to resist. This is an easy profit of five hundred thousand spirit stones!

The two Golden Core cultivators revealed a hesitant expression.

“What is it? If you have something to say, just say it.”

“Patriarch, that Dao-Seeking Sect disciple might not lack this bit of spirit stone.”

“Then make that one million five hundred thousand spirit stones!” The commandery governor was fired up. I don’t believe one million spirit stones still isn’t enough to make the other party give up.

“That might still not be enough.”

“Two million!”

“Still not enough.”

The commandery governor flew into a rage. “Then tell me, how many spirit stones would it take for them to cede? The other party is just at the Foundation Establishment Stage. How many spirit stones could they possibly have? I refuse to believe that two million spirit stones won’t move them!”

“We heard that he is the eldest son of the Meng Family.”

“Meng Family.” “Eldest son.” These two terms combined represented tremendous power and wealth; no one dared to provoke them. As the number one ancestral clan in the Central Continent, the Meng Family’s reputation spread far and wide.

However, the commandery governor was even more irate, completely undeterred by Meng Jingzhou’s identity. “So what if he’s the eldest son of the Meng Family? If worse comes to worst, I’ll personally steal it tomorrow night!”

Chapter 225: Peer of the Same Trade

The commandery governor did not want to blow the matter out of proportion. If something can be solved with spirit stones, I’ll try my best to solve it with spirit stones.

Luofeng Commandery’s key economic sector was mining. As the commandery governor, the amount of spirit stones under his control could only be described as vast. He refused to believe that a mere Foundation Establishment disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect could match his wealth.

However, he now knew that he had overestimated himself. I’m nowhere near qualified to compare my wealth to that of the Meng Family’s eldest son.

It’s best to steal it myself; that’s much more economical and practical.

“Do you think offering ten million spirit stones would make the Meng Family’s eldest son interested?”

The two Golden Core cultivators hesitantly shook their heads. “No.”

“Fine, I’ll set my offer as ten million spirit stones.” The commandery governor tried to boost his self-confidence.

~~~

On the roof, Lu Yang turned to Meng Jingzhou. “Would you sell it for ten million spirit stones?”

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. “I’d even sell it for just five hundred thousand spirit stones. Why the hell would I hold on to a yang-boosting thing?”

“To train your willpower?”

“Get lost.”

~~~

Meanwhile, another scene unfolded at the Mo Family.

“Family Head, the ore shops under us came to report earlier today that a group of people came in with a unique Phoenix Blood Stone and asked if there were any similar stones. From the description, it sounds exactly like the Phoenix Blood Stone we’ve been searching for.”

“Oh? Are you certain?” Family Head Mo’s eyes lit up, not expecting that they had finally found the Phoenix Blood Stone.

As the saying goes, “Merchants cannot win against officials.”[1] Although the Mo Family is wealthy and influential, we’re still no match for the commandery governor. If we can get our hands on this Phoenix Blood Stone, it’ll be considered having leverage over the commandery governor, and we won’t have to fear him anymore.

His subordinate stated, “I plan to act tonight and steal the Phoenix Blood Stone.”

“Tonight? Let me ask you, who bought the Phoenix Blood Stone, what is their identity, and how is their cultivation? What would you do if they are at the Divine Transfiguration Stage?”

His subordinate stammered, unable to answer. He realized he had been too eager to impress his master.

Family Head Mo snorted coldly. “We can’t be careless. Go inquire who obtained the Phoenix Blood Stone tomorrow. If nothing goes wrong, I’ll personally steal it myself tomorrow night!”

“You’re going to do it yourself?” The subordinate gasped. Does this really call for the Family Head to step in?

“Of course, this is evidence that can give us leverage over the commandery governor. It’s worth me personally handling this.” Family Head Mo revealed a sliver of excitement.

It’s about time to turn the tide in our struggle with the commandery governor.

~~~

“What exactly is so special about this stone?” Meng Jingzhou took out the Phoenix Blood Stone upon returning to Li Haoran’s home. He examined it closely but couldn’t find anything of note.

“Senior Su, can you tell if anything’s wrong with this?”

Su Yiren shook her head. “I don’t know much about the Phoenix BloodStone. Perhaps only a cultivator adept at forging artifacts can tell what’s unusual about this stone.”

Everyone turned their eyes to Li Haoran.

The corners of Li Haoran’s mouth twitched. “I think all of you are overestimating me. It’s more like it if my shifu were here instead.”

“Immortal Fairy, can you tell if anything’s wrong?” Lu Yang sought assistance from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

She frowned. “It smells of blood, and it’s very fresh. I don’t like it.”

“Smells of blood? Very fresh?” Lu Yang had a bad feeling about it. Could this Phoenix Blood Stone be a clue left behind by some deceased person?

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, is it true that a phoenix passed away in a seated posture in Luofeng Commandery?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “There was indeed one, but it did not surround this place like Li Haoran had said. It’s beneath our feet.” She pointed downward. “Beneath the entire Luofeng Commandery lies a corpse of a phoenix at the Fusion Stage.”

“What should we do?” Li Haoran asked, not expecting this turn of events. I was just making a trip back home to visit my parents, and now we have attracted the commandery governor’s attention and made him take action personally.

Luofeng Commandery was a large commandery, and its commandery governor was at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“Catch him directly?” Su Yiren had the highest cultivation among everyone present, so she had the right to speak first. Her idea was simple—capture the problematic person.

Lu Yang contemplated for a bit. “It’s not a good idea to directly act without evidence. We’re representing the Dao-Seeking Sect, so we shouldn’t misuse their law enforcement authority. Let’s have faith and wait for the commandery governor to come and steal the thing tomorrow night. We’ll first use a recording orb to record everything, then ask Senior Su to take action. That way, we can catch him red-handed!

“With all that evidence, he has to admit it even if doesn’t want to!”

“Got it,” Su Yiren agreed.

Lu Yang reminded everyone, “Also, only the few of us should know about this. Junior Brother Li, you don’t want your parents to get involved, right?”

Li Haoran nodded, his tone slightly helpless as if he had recalled something. “From what I understand about them, it’s best not to let them find out about this.”

“I’ll also keep this a secret from Yanyan,” Su Yiren assured.

Li Haoran lamented. “Fortunately, we have Senior Su here with us. Otherwise, I really wouldn’t know what to do tomorrow night.”

Meng Jingzhou chuckled. “What is there to be scared of? Don’t we have Lu Yang? He defeated a Divine Transfiguration cultivator when he was just at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage. With him around, there’s nothing to fear about the commandery governor.”

Su Yiren originally wanted to correct Li Haoran’s method of addressing her, but the information from Meng Jingzhou was too astonishing. An Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator defeating a Divine Transfiguration cultivator? What kind of one-and-only genius is this?! Was I embarrassing myself by sharing my golden core formation experience in front of an expert?

“Scram!” Lu Yang glowered at Meng Jingzhou, knowing that he was taking revenge against him for teasing him earlier.

Overwhelmed with curiosity, Su Yiren kept asking about the details of the battle where he fought above his level. As the process was too embarrassing, Lu Yang was adamant about keeping his mouth shut. He even shot warning looks at Meng Jingzhou and Li Haoran. “Don’t you dare tell her!”

When daytime arrived, everyone pretended as though nothing had happened the night before, going about eating, drinking, and having fun as they should.

Lu Yang took the time to ask around if any cultivators had recently gone missing or died. The answer he got was that there were none.

~~~

As the sunlight faded, night fell, with the darkness intensifying.

A figure blended into the night as it snuck into Li Haoran’s house.

The commandery governor was fully prepared, geared up with night stealth attire and a mask. His clothes had the function of concealing his aura and presence. Both his voice and spirit energy fluctuations were altered such that even his wife wouldn’t recognize him.

“I didn’t leave anything out, right?” It was the commandery governor’s first time doing something like this, so he felt a bit nervous. However, as soon as he thought of how his operation was worth ten million spirit stones, it eased his nerves.

Releasing his spiritual consciousness, he found the Phoenix Blood Stone placed at Meng Jingzhou’s bedside. The person in question was sound asleep, completely unaware.

Meng Jingzhou was very frustrated. He originally wanted to watch the spectacle, but it wouldn’t be reasonable for him not to sleep here. Left without a choice, he could only pretend to be asleep while listening to Lu Yang’s broadcast.

“Found it!”

The commandery governor was just about to proceed when he noticed another figure vaulting over the wall—Family Head Mo. His get-up was exactly the same as the commandery governor’s, wrapping himself up from head to toe so that no one could recognize him.

The two froze simultaneously, not expecting to run into a “peer of the same trade” here. Is this place so popular?

Wait, no...I’m the commandery governor/family head. I’m just being a thief this one time.

1. This is modified from the original version which says, “The poor cannot win against the rich, and the rich cannot win against the authorities.” ☜

Chapter 226: The Third Dark Figure

Family Head Mo had already investigated the current situation of the Phoenix Blood Stone and found it a bit tricky.

A Foundation Establishment disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, likely a nouveau riche, had bought the Phoenix Blood Stone. He had two other companions, also from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Foundation Establishment cultivators were nothing much in his eyes, but hearing the name “Dao-Seeking Sect” had completely changed things. The higher one’s cultivation was, the more secrets they knew, and the more they understood the terror of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

That’s why this matter requires me to take action personally. If a Divine Transfiguration cultivator wants to steal something, how could three Foundation Establishment disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect possibly notice?

However, he was not the only one stealing tonight.

Thief, how dare you covet the thing I have set my sights on?

“Leave now!” The commandery governor and Family Head Mo released their oppressive pressure toward the other party simultaneously. Ordinary thieves would have sat frozen on the floor in fear.

The commandery governor revealed a trace of a sneer. He surmised that the Mo Family hadn’t given up after their failure last night and had sent people here again tonight. What use is that? You can only consider yourselves unlucky to have met me!

The almost identical oppressive pressure collided silently, causing both of them to frown.

“Hmm?” The two sensed that the other party’s oppressive pressure was unusual—definitely not any small fry!

“Old Monster Mo!”

“Old Ghost Shi!”

Both parties recognized each other’s identities. What ensued was a silence that lasted more than ten seconds.

It was too easy to identify the other party—they were the only two Divine Transfiguration cultivators in the whole of Luofeng Commandery.

Both took pride in their status and despised petty thievery, so running into each other here was truly awkward.

After all, they couldn’t possibly claim that they were here to bask in the moonlight.

“What a coincidence, you’re here too.”

“Exactly, what a coincidence.”

What ensued next was again an awkward silence of more than ten seconds.

The commandery governor gained the upper hand by striking first. He transmitted an auditory message with his spiritual consciousness, his voice solemn and filled with righteousness. “I had already predicted that a thief would come here tonight, so I’ve been waiting here. As I thought, you’ve finally come, Old Monster Mo. Surrender immediately!” He pulled out an iron chain from somewhere and tried to loop it around Family Head Mo.

“Pah! You think I’m blind? Look at how you’re dressed! And you have the face to say that you’re waiting for the thief?” Family Head Mo clearly didn’t buy it. This grandson is dressed in black from top to bottom like I am. Who is he fooling?

He drew his weapon for battle. The two were worried that the matter would be exposed, so they tacitly didn’t use any of their powers and fought silently. Having been opponents for decades, they were extremely familiar with each other’s tactics. Aware that a battle wouldn’t do anything to the other party, they stopped after exchanging a few dozen moves.

“At this rate, it won’t lead to any outcome.” The commandery governor proposed, “You came here for that Phoenix Blood Stone, right? Let’s steal it based on our abilities. Whoever gets it will keep it.”

“Alright, it’s settled.” Family Head Mo agreed quickly.

The commandery governor sneered inwardly. Even if he gets the Phoenix Blood Stone, I will find a way to snatch it back. This affects my future prospects. Who’s going to honor a promise with you?

Coincidentally, Family Head Mo thought the same thing.

In the shadows, Lu Yang was capturing everything with a recording orb.

The two people had already used their spiritual consciousness to detect the location of the Phoenix Blood Stone. Just as they were about to enter Meng Jingzhou’s room together, another dark figure scaled the wall.

“Why is there another one?” The commandery governor and Family Head Mo were not the only ones befuddled. Even Lu Yang, Su Yiren, and Li Haoran, who were observing from the shadows, found it bewildering.

Lu Yang looked at Li Haoran. “Is your house so attractive?”

Li Haoran rolled his eyes and didn’t bother to respond. It’s not my house that is attractive; it’s Senior Brother Meng’s Phoenix Blood Stone that is attractive.

Lu Yang recalled the dark figure he had glimpsed while following the two Golden Core cultivators last night. Could it be the same person?

Su Yiren warned, “The third dark figure is also a Divine Transfiguration cultivator.”

Lu Yang grew cautious. Who is the third dark figure? What is their objective?

“What? There are now three Divine Transfiguration cultivators instead of two?” Meng Jingzhou couldn’t see what was going on, so his heart was itching as he listened to their conversation. How I wish I could see what’s happening outside.

~~~

The third dark figure was not surprised to see the commandery governor and Family Head Mo. He nodded and said, “Not bad, you arrived fifteen minutes ahead of schedule. Let’s go.”

The commandery governor and Family Head Mo exchanged glances with each other, realizing they couldn’t discern the third figure’s cultivation stage.

Divine Transfiguration Stage? But where would a third Divine Transfiguration cultivator come from in Luofeng Commandery?

Since the other party seemed to have mistaken them for someone else, they decided to play along and followed the dark figure.

The commandery governor asked, “Your Excellency, I heard that a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple lives here. Is it safe for us to act?”

The dark figure didn’t think anything of it. “He’s just a the Foundation Establishment disciple. What could go wrong? Everything is ready except for the one last critical thing[1]—a premier grade Phoenix Blood Stone. To think that the Phoenix Blood Stone with the best quality has landed in the hands of this Dao-Seeking Sect disciple.

“Once the job is done, the three of us will be promoted. We’re about to succeed, so why are the two of you so fidgety and hesitant? Quickly keep up!”

It turned out that the dark figure’s aim was also the Phoenix Blood Stone Meng Jingzhou had purchased.

Lu Yang grumbled, “What on earth is this Phoenix Blood Stone you bought? It specializes in attracting Divine Transfiguration cultivators.” That’s what you get for flaunting your wealth. Now everyone knows you have a premier-grade Phoenix Blood Stone in your possession.

“The hell could I have known?! If I had known, I might as well have thrown it into the garbage bin,” Meng Jingzhou also grumbled.

The three Divine Transfiguration cultivators arrived at Meng Jingzhou’s room simultaneously.

“Phoenix Blood Stone!” The commandery governor’s eyes shone as they lay upon the Phoenix Blood Stone beside Meng Jingzhou. Just as I thought, it’s that Phoenix Blood Stone that absolutely mustn’t be released into the market.

Family Head Mo noticed the commandery governor’s reactions and knew that he hadn’t guessed wrong.

The dark figure’s eyes also shone. Although he had never seen a top-grade Phoenix Blood Stone before, the quality of the one before him was enough.

“By the way, Your Excellency, what do we need this Phoenix Blood Stone for?” the commandery governor casually asked.

Perhaps it was because the goal was right before his eyes, the dark figure inadvertently relaxed his guard. “Of course, it’s to refine the phoenix beneath our feet into a corpse puppet so that we can overturn Luofeng Commandery and bolster the might of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. With all the arrangements in place, the only thing we lack is a top-grade Phoenix Blood Stone to serve as the core.”

“You’re from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?!” Family Head Mo gasped.

“What are you blabbering about? If we’re not from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, are you saying that we’re from the Everlasting Creed... Hold on, who are the two of you?!” These two people aren’t my subordinates at all!

The three thieves tensed up, prepared to strike at any moment.

“Since you’ve been discovered, I can’t let you live!” The dark figure launched a bold attack, his Apex Divine Transfiguration cultivation on full display, intent on using this opportunity to eliminate the two.

The commandery governor and Family Head Mo weren’t pushovers either. We’re all at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, yet you want to kill us in a flash? We still don’t know who will kill whom!

At the same time, the space froze, and none of the three could move, as if time had come to a standstill.

Modifying rules was an ability of Fusion cultivators—Su Yiren had made her move.

1. This is a modification of a famous expression that translates as “Everything is ready except for the east wind.” It came from the military strategist Zhuge Liang’s fire stratagem. Everything was set, and the only critical thing left in the plan was the east wind to spread the fire. ☜

Chapter 227: Su Yiren Makes Her Move

“There’s more people?!” The commandery governor, Family Head Mo, and the member of the Nine-Netherworlds Sect were stunned. They had prided themselves on being chess masters who manipulated everything in the shadows.

Why are we the ones being manipulated now? Who else is hiding in the dark?

They unleashed their respective attacks.

The commandery governor attempted to activate the chain hidden on his back, but no matter how hard he tried, the chain seemed to be nailed to his back, unable to budge an inch.

Family Head Mo’s arms were tattooed with eighteen designs of weapons, each representing a type of weapon he had forged himself. In the past, these weapons were unstoppable, but they had all fallen silent, and not a single one could be activated.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower tried to summon the shadows of monsters hiding inside him, but they cowered in fear as if they had encountered something terrifying, refusing to come out.

The three realized that the person who had just made a move was no simple figure. The ability to casually alter part of the rules... They’re at the Fusion Stage?!

Do Dao-Seeking Sect disciples always travel in such extravagance, accompanied by a Fusion expert?

The commandery governor and Family Head Mo were beset with regret. All we wanted was to steal the Phoenix Blood Stone. How did we stir up so many other problems? There’s now the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and a Fusion cultivator...

When Meng Jingzhou sensed that Su Yiren had finally made her move, he was so frightened that he sprung out of bed and ran, seeking her protection. He was the only person in the room who could still move.

Lu Yang whispered to Li Haoran, “If she wants to use force, it looks like you have no ability to resist. You should just give in to her.”[1]

“If she does that, she’ll only get my body, not my heart!” Li Haoran responded sternly, though he was secretly on tenterhooks.

That said, Su Yiren is gentle and virtuous like a caring older sister. If I really give in to her...that might not be as bad as I thought.

Su Yiren pushed open the door and looked at the three people she had immobilized. Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Li Haoran followed behind her, filled with a sense of security.

“I didn’t expect it, Commandery Governor Shi. You colluded with not just the Phoenix Tribe but also the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. You’re truly reprehensible. I have already captured everything with a recording orb!” Lu Yang immediately accused him.

“Hey hey hey, you can’t just say that.” The commandery governor’s expression changed.

“Ah, right right right, he colluded with the Phoenix Tribe and Nine-Netherworlds Creed. I can testify.” Family Head Mo jumped at the opportunity to kick the commandery governor when he was down.

“Let me introduce myself, I’m Lu Yang, a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Meng Jingzhou, disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Li Haoran, disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Su Yiren didn’t speak. Although she might be amicable in front of Li Haoran, it was a completely different case when it came to outsiders.
