“I originally wanted to see what secret this Phoenix Blood Stone holds, but I didn’t expect to reel in such a big fish.” Lu Yang removed the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower’s mask and saw that the person had no noticeable features.

“You just said that you wanted to refine the phoenix into a corpse puppet. Tell me everything, and I might spare your life.” This was no small matter. The corpse of a Fusion phoenix was right beneath their feet. Let alone refining it into a corpse puppet, even just the phoenix turning over would be a calamity for Luofeng Commandery.

The commandery governor’s expression was grim. If the Nine-Netherworlds Creed really succeeds, that would mark the end of my position as commandery governor.

The follower from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed laughed out loud. “Now that you’ve discovered me, how could you possibly still let me live?”

“Senior Su, please search his soul,” Lu Yang requested for Su Yiren to take action when he saw that the other party had no intention of confessing.

Su Yiren stepped forward and pressed her finger to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower’s forehead, her brows knitted. “He’s not human but a corpse!”

Suddenly, the eyes of the Nine-Netherworlds follower became vacant, and his body rapidly decayed until nothing but a pile of white bones was left.

This was a common tactic of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed—animate a corpse while the original body pulls the string in the background. Once discovered, they would sever the connection with the corpse, causing it to rot pronto and leave no trace behind, which made it hard for them to be captured. However, those present didn’t know much about the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“Trying to escape?” Su Yiren made another move. With her Fusion abilities, she enveloped the entire Luofeng Commandery with the rules, preventing insects from entering and birds from escaping. She was determined to ferret out the person from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Controlling a corpse is limited by a certain distance; the other party must still be in Luofeng Commandery. My cultivation is two major realms ahead; letting them escape would be downright embarrassing.

It doesn’t matter if I embarrass myself, but not in front of Li Haoran!

She spread out her spiritual consciousness and scanned every inch of Luofeng Commandery.

“Found them!” Su Yiren quickly locked onto several suspicious cultivators. They seemed to have some sort of restrictions on them; as soon as Su Yiren immobilized them, they exploded and died.

“So ruthless?”

The commandery governor’s expression darkened. “I heard that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed believes in the existence of the Nine Netherworlds. To them, death is just a cycle of reincarnation and is nothing scary. That’s why they are a bunch of criminals who have no regard for their lives and are extremely dangerous!”

With her spiritual consciousness, Su Yiren discovered that the dried-up wells in the homes of many affluent families hid arrays. They were closely interlinked, covering the entire large array, likely the one for refining the phoenix.

“Wait, something’s wrong. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed followers who exploded are not at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. The real mastermind hasn’t been found yet!” Su Yiren realized that those who had died were just the mastermind’s subordinates.

“They’re below, in the phoenix’s corpse!” Lu Yang was the first to think of it. Since the old phoenix was at the Fusion stage when it was alive, a Fusion corpse can block the spiritual consciousness of someone else at the same cultivation stage.

Su Yiren also figured it out, but she didn’t move.

“Senior Su, what’s the matter?” Lu Yang was baffled. Darting into the ground shouldn’t be anything difficult for a Fusion cultivator, right? Don’t they all have a few simple spells for that?

“Senior Su, you should quickly go down! If the Nine-Netherworlds Creed manages to refine the phoenix, Luofeng Commandery will be in danger,” Li Haoran also urged.

Su Yiren paused to consider her choice of words. “My methods...might be a bit different from what you think.”

She took a deep breath to calm herself. Now that things have come to this, I can’t pretend to be a demure young lady anymore.

Clenching her fists, she hurled a punch right toward the ground, creating a deep hole wide enough for a person. Then, she leaped in and burrowed underground.

Lu Yang and his other two companions stared with their eyes widened as they gulped. Senior Su Yiren’s methods...don’t seem to match her delicate appearance at all.

They suddenly thought of a question that had been overlooked all this time: what type of cultivation did she specialize in?

Meng Jingzhou peered at the huge hole and found it familiar. Why do her methods seem similar to that of my shifu?

The three exchanged glances as an absurd thought coalesced in their minds.

Don’t tell me that Su Yiren is...a physique cultivator?

~~~

Meanwhile, Su Yiren saw a phoenix with bright red feathers lying quietly underground as if it had just died.

Suddenly, the arrays the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had left on the ground activated in succession. The phoenix's eyes lit up with a light that resembled jasper. Phoenix True Flame erupted in the surroundings, burning the entire underground space hollow.

“Since I’ve been discovered, let’s all go down together!” The voice of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower echoed from within the phoenix, raspy and consumed with insanity.

Despite all that, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower’s heart was overwhelmed with regret. Set up the array, steal a Phoenix Blood Stone, resurrect the phoenix, and overturn Luofeng Commandery—what a perfect plan! It was supposed to be simple, easy to execute, flawless, and undetectable.

We just wanted to steal a Phoenix Blood Stone. Why is there a Fusion cultivator guarding it? Is this Phoenix Blood Stone really so valuable? Huh, tell me!

“Although I couldn’t revive the phoenix to its peak in such a hurry, it’s more than enough to overturn Luofeng Commandery!” At this point, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower couldn’t be bothered so much. “I know you’re at the Fusion Stage, but so what? Are you an array cultivator or a talisman cultivator? None of that matters anymore. Before you can completely stop the phoenix’s movements, I’ll already have ample time to destroy Luofeng Commandery several times!”

The phoenix’s shrieks reverberated in the underground cave as it was engulfed in true flame. It spread its wings, carrying boundless destructive power, as if it was just reborn from the ashes and flame.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower was about to manipulate the phoenix to soar into the sky but suddenly found that the phoenix just couldn’t take off. “What’s going on?”

He used his spiritual consciousness to probe the outside world and discovered that Su Yiren was grabbing the phoenix’s beak with one hand, preventing it from flying a single inch no matter how hard it flapped its wings.

“Fly?” A sliver of a cold smile emerged on Su Yiren’s charming face. With the hand that was gripping the phoenix’s beak, she forcefully slammed the phoenix onto the ground.

The commandery governor and Family Head Mo led Lu Yang’s trio down the tunnel and arrived just in time to witness the scene of Su Yiren flinging the phoenix—a perfect blend of beauty and violence.

Li Haoran tried his best to swallow his saliva. If we get married, can I still survive?

1. The tone and phrasing here seem very much like the trope of a delicate woman and the alpha male in Chinese novels. ☜

Chapter 228: Phoenix True Flame

In the beginning, Li Haoran was resistant to Su Yiren. He felt that he couldn’t live off a woman; he wanted to be independent just like Lu Yang.

Later, he began to see Su Yiren as beautiful, kind, gentle, and caring, exuding a maternal warmth that made him involuntarily want to act spoiled in front of her.

Now, as he watched Su Yiren’s every punch and kick brimming with such strength that the phoenix couldn’t get up from the ground, he changed his mind. I’m too small and fragile compared to the robust phoenix. For the sake of my own safety, I should stay further away from Su Yiren.

This is what they call staying true to one’s original intention.

Li Haoran’s legs trembled, nipping any thought of being a kept man in the bud.

My heart may be ready, but my body isn’t.

Clinging onto my arm on the streets only broke my bones, but if our relationship progresses further, I don’t dare to imagine the torment my body will suffer.

Lu Yang seemed to have read Li Haoran’s mind and patted his shoulder. “There are pros and cons to everything.”

It wasn’t just Li Haoran; even the commandery governor and Family Head Mo were shaken by the terrifying way Su Yiren fought. This senior looks so gentle and delicate. Why does she seem like a completely different person when she’s fighting?

They had come underground to see if there was anything they could assist with. However, they were now worried whether Su Yiren would beat them up too.

“Is this senior from the Dao-Seeking Sect a physique cultivator?” The two assumed that Su Yiren was at the rank of an elder in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Senior Su is not from the Dao-Seeking Sect; she is his fiancée.” Meng Jingzhou solemnly introduced Li Haoran, the outstanding young man from Luofeng Commandery.

The commandery governor and Family Head Mo immediately put on a solemn expression that radiated their deep veneration.

While the group above chatted jovially, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower below was in an execrable state. In order to refine the corpse of the phoenix, destroy Luofeng Commandery, and instigate the conflict between the humans and phoenixes, he had plotted for years, browsing classic texts, researching ancient books, consulting seniors, and ancient ruins. It was then that he finally discovered the method to refine the phoenix’s corpse.

The Phoenix Tribe was a pro-peace faction, maintaining a rather harmonious relationship with the human race. If he could use the matter of refining the phoenix’s corpse to stoke the flames of war, countless lives would be lost, sending more lives into the cycle of reincarnation.

I was just one step away!

Just one more step!

Why did a Fusion cultivator just have to appear from nowhere?

“It doesn’t matter even if you’re at the Fusion Stage!” the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower shouted in a deranged manner, having completely lost his mind.

Controlling such a colossal corpse was a test for both his cultivation and mental power. Normally, other followers from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed would help to share the burden, but Su Yiren had already killed all of them.

The old phoenix burst into an inferno and crackled as the space seemed to begin to warp. Even Lu Yang and the others, who were standing right at the edge, could feel the onslaught of the blistering heat waves. The commandery governor had no choice but to whip out a string of golden bells from his storage ring to shield everyone in them.

As Su Yiren stepped on the phoenix’s back, the phoenix plummeted to the ground with a crash. However, the flames showed no signs of abating. The Phoenix True Flame was capable of dissolving all things, including soil. The creation of this underground cavity was also its work. If the true flame continued to spread, the entire Luofeng Commandery would be engulfed in a sea of fire.

One had to know that the Phoenix True Flame and Golden Dragon True Flame were as famous as the Three Esse True Fire.

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched the battle from the mental space, she remembered the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy she had mentored. “It’s hard dealing with the Phoenix True Flame as ever.” The prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes naturally mastered their tribe’s signature skill, demonstrating impeccable proficiency over flames—perfect for cooking.

“Is there any way to counter it?” Lu Yang hurriedly asked. If there’s really no way about it, I’d have to summon Big Senior Sister.

“There’s an acupoint unique to phoenixes at the center of its neck. That’s the source of the Phoenix True Flame. Hit that acupoint, and it won’t spout flames anymore.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t drop the ball, providing a solution at this critical moment.

Lu Yang immediately passed on the information in an auditory message to Su Yiren. The latter turned to glance at Lu Yang in surprise, though she didn’t think much of it, simply assuming that Dao-Seeking Sect disciples were knowledgeable and had learned it from their lessons.

After all, his shifu is the sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Su Yiren aimed for the point according to Lu Yang’s direction and charged forward, while the Phoenix True Flame surged toward her as if it had gone mad. Clenching her right hand into a fist, she positioned it at her waist and delivered a punch with a burst of force. The space in front of her was completely distorted, and the Phoenix True Flame could no longer get close to her.

“Die!” Su Yiren dished out a punch with the sound of thunder, hammering the old phoenix’s neck. The Phoenix True Flame seemed to have lost its energy source and gradually dissipated.

“What on earth is going on?!” the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower exclaimed in horror, color draining from his face. The Phoenix True Flame is renowned for its ability to melt all beings and for being inextinguishable. How did it disappear just like that?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy divulged to Lu Yang that this was a secret of the Phoenix Tribe. Even few within the tribe were privy to this, much less the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s followers.

Without the True Phoenix Flame, the old phoenix was no longer a threat. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower was still desperately trying to carve a path out with blood, but a hammer-like blow from Su Yiren rendered him immobile.

Su Yiren was also fuming inside. I had pretended to be a gentle and virtuous lady for the past few days and finally made a good impression on Li Haoran. Now, it has all gone to ruin because of you!

Damn Nine-Netherworlds Creed!

Die, die, die!

Watching Su Yiren’s earth-shattering fists pummel down in succession, Li Haoran couldn’t stop his eyelids from twitching. If these were to land on me, my soul probably wouldn’t even survive.

Finally, Su Yiren unleashed a devastating punch packed with sheer force and ferocity. Its sound reverberated through the ground until the whole Luofeng Commandery could hear it, signifying the conclusion of the battle. She ripped open a hole in the phoenix’s corpse, dragged the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower out, and directly searched his soul.

Her eyebrows furrowed. During the battle earlier, this creed member had used his spiritual consciousness beyond what he could handle, leaving his mind in a complete mess, preventing her from discerning anything. In other words, this follower had gone crazy.

“Damn it, so unlucky.” Su Yiren snapped the follower’s neck, sending him straight to the Nine Netherworlds.

The aftermath of the battle in the underground space was somewhat challenging to sort out. Su Yiren temporarily used the power of rules to stabilize the space above and left the remaining matters to the Great Xia Dynasty since she was not well-versed in this aspect.

The commandery governor expressed his heartfelt gratitude, “Senior, thank you for extending your assistance. Without you, Luofeng Commandery might not have escaped this calamity.”

“Don’t be in a rush to thank me just yet. What’s the deal with this Phoenix Blood Stone? Explain yourself.”

“Senior, there’s really nothing to this Phoenix Blood Stone. I simply found it rare...” The commandery governor clearly didn’t want to tell them the truth.

Lu Yang pulled out the recording orb. “This recording orb contains evidence of the commandery governor breaking into civilian homes, stealing property, and defecting to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

“Wait a second! I can accept breaking into civilian homes and stealing property, but since when did I defect to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?”

Lu Yang played the recording. It displayed the Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower vaulting over the wall, with the commandery governor and Family Head Mo following behind him as they headed to Meng Jingzhou’s room.

The recording stopped here.

“What about everything after that? Where’s the footage of us uncovering the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s goals and preparing for battle?” The commandery governor and Family Head Mo were flung into a panic.

Lu Yang said expressionlessly, “The recording orb is broken, so it doesn’t display the rest.

“If the commandery governor is willing to offer us an explanation, I might be able to fix the recording orb.”

The commandery governor responded through gritted teeth, “The disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect truly live up to their name.”

Chapter 229: The Origins of the Phoenix Blood Stones

The only thing the commandery governor could do was gnash his teeth at Lu Yang. From the bottom of his heart, he had no desire to reveal this matter, but now that things had progressed to this, he had to divulge the truth whether he liked it or not.

Family Head Mo’s countenance was one of schadenfreude.

The commandery governor let out a heavy sigh. “Everyone, please follow me.”

The group followed the commandery governor, heading straight for the mine.

“The mine collapsing was merely a cover story we released to the public; there’s more to this than meets the eye.” With practiced ease, the commandery governor led the group to the end of the tunnel. Pressing a hidden mechanism on the wall, a stone door opened with a rumbling sound, showing a path into the depths of the mine.

This passageway was only disclosed to a select few. It was secretly protected by an array that evaded the detection of spiritual consciousness. If someone’s spiritual consciousness scanned the area, they would only see an image simulated by the array.

Family Head Mo’s expression turned serious. Just like what my investigations have yielded, there’s indeed a secret passageway.

The further they ventured inward, the stronger the stench of blood became. It was as if a massacre had just occurred ahead, with corpses piled as high as a mountain and their blood run dry.

When Lu Yang stepped out of the tunnel into an open space, the overwhelming odor of blood swept over him. Fortunately, he adapted to the bloody smell quickly and took in the scene before him.

In the center of the open area was a massive pit filled with blood-red liquid. Countless stones jutted out from the blood-red pool, their vivid hues resembling the quality of the Blood Phoenix Stone Meng Jingzhou had bought. Several people moved around the edge of the pit, occasionally pouring blood into the crimson pool.

“This...this is...”

The commandery governor explained helplessly, “This is where Phoenix Blood Stones are produced.”

“The Phoenix Blood Stones are fake?” Meng Jingzhou was dumbstruck. I spent half a million on a counterfeit?!

Li Haoran shook his head. “Wait, that’s not right. The blood in the pit is indeed phoenix blood. I’ve seen my shifu use it before for refining artifacts, though the quality of the Phoenix Blood he used was much higher than the ones here.”

“Commandery Governor, who are these people?” A young man with red eyes and red feathers on his neck walked over. His brow was knitted, displeased with the commandery governor for bringing outsiders here.

The commandery governor sighed. “I had no choice. If I didn’t bring them here, I’d be the unlucky one to suffer.”

The red-eyed youth was about to explode with rage. Bringing outsiders here means that our secret is exposed. How am I supposed to explain this to the tribe leader when I return?

“These people are from the Dao-Seeking Sect, and this is my grandson, the family head of the Mo Family.”

“Scram!”

“Dao-Seeking Sect?” The red-eyed youth scrutinized Lu Yang and the others in surprise. Myriad emotions flashed past his visage, as though he was recalling some unpleasant memories; his arrogant demeanor softened considerably.

“What’s your relationship with Yun Zhi?”

“She’s my Big Senior Sister.”

“What about Gan Tian?”

“She’s my Third Senior Sister,” Lu Yang replied. He had never met his third senior sister, for she was currently training and gaining experience in the Demon Region.

“Ah, fellow Daoists from the Dao-Seeking Sect, you’re here for an inspection? Please, this way.” The red-eyed youth’s attitude made a complete turnaround. He plastered on a wide and affable smile.

The commandery governor could feel his eyelids twitching. I’ve never seen him act so friendly toward me before. “Allow me to introduce, this is Jiang Shan from the Phoenix Tribe.”

“Senior Jiang Shan, regarding my Big Senior Sister and Third Senior Sister, may I ask how you know...”

“Aiya, calling me Senior Jiang Shan is too formal. Just call me Little Jiang.” For some reason, Jiang Shan was especially cordial toward Lu Yang. “As for Senior Yun Zhi and Senior Gan Tian, they’re exceptionally kind to the Phoenix Tribe. They even visited us for a friendly sparring session and offered some guidance for our cultivation. I was also fortunate to have received some of their advice myself.

“Of course, if possible—and I mean if—could you perhaps let your Big Senior Sister and Third Senior Sister know that they don’t have to visit the Phoenix Tribe again? The Dragon Tribe has plenty of space; they should go there instead.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Big Senior Sister, Third Senior Sister, just what exactly did you do at the Phoenix Tribe?

Su Yiren was also very curious. This doesn’t match the prideful reputation of the Phoenix Clan at all.

“I’m here to find out the truth about the Phoenix Blood Stones.” Lu Yang stated his purpose.

The commandery governor replied, “Jiang Shan doesn’t know as much as I do. Let me explain.

“This matter can be traced back to four thousand years ago. Back then, a phoenix senior passed away here, and their blood permeated the mine, giving rise to the first batch of Phoenix Blood Stones. The people accidentally discovered the stones and were ecstatic. They set up camps here, marking the beginnings of Luofeng Commandery.

“About seven hundred years later, the Blood Phoenix Stones became increasingly scarce and difficult to mine. The commandery governor at the time realized the exigency of the situation. Without the Phoenix Blood Stones, the backbone of Luofeng Commandery’s economy would collapse, and the whole commandery would fall apart. Hence, he secretly approached the Phoenix Tribe, hoping to purchase some phoenix blood to produce a new batch of Phoenix Blood Stones.

“At first, the Phoenix Tribe refused. They viewed themselves as high and mighty, unwilling to sell their blood to the commandery governor. However, when the commandery governor presented a detailed record of the revenue from selling Phoenix Blood Stones over the years and promised to share thirty percent of the profits with the Phoenix Tribe, their attitude shifted drastically.”

Everyone turned their gaze to Jiang Shan, the only member of the Phoenix Tribe present.

Jiang Shan was convinced that reason was on his side. “There are so many people in the Phoenix Tribe. All of them require spirit stones for food, clothing, and shelter. What’s wrong with earning some money through our own abilities to support our households?”

It was Lu Yang’s first time hearing someone describe selling their blood in such an unconventional yet dignified manner. He recalled Li Haoran had once said, “The Dragon and Phoenix tribes are the proudest among the demons. Their blood is incredibly valuable, and it’s almost as hard as reaching the heavens for humans to obtain them.”

Truly “as hard as reaching the heavens.”

The commandery governor shot Jiang Shan a glance. “If the Phoenix Tribe is so self-assured, why do you still demand that the Phoenix Blood Stones be artificially aged to ensure that outsiders can’t tell they’re freshly soaked?”

Jiang Shan shifted his guilty gaze furtively, avoiding eye contact with the commandery governor.

The commandery governor continued, “The Phoenix Tribe was willing to sell their phoenix blood, but they insisted on keeping it a secret. Thus, that commandery governor developed a method to expedite the aging of the Phoenix Blood Stone.

“Just like this.” He picked up a random stone from the blood pool and cast a spell. The originally vibrant Blood Phoenix Stone turned dull, as if it had weathered through several hundreds or thousands of years.

“Every few years, Luofeng Commandery would receive a batch of blood from the Phoenix Blood Tribe, soak the stones, and produce Phoenix Blood Stones. This has been going on for over three thousand years and is passed down as a secret from one commandery governor to the next.

“Later, for some reason, an accident occurred. An unaged Phoenix Blood Stone was circulated outside, and after changing hands a few times, it was purchased by the eldest young master of the Meng Family.

“If an experienced artifact-crafting master sees that Phoenix Blood Stone, they would immediately surmise that the current Phoenix Blood Stones in Luofeng Commandery are freshly produced, thereby deducing the arrangement between Luofeng Commandery and the Phoenix Tribe.

“It would reflect poorly on both the Luofeng Commandery and Phoenix Tribe if this matter is exposed. That’s why I’ve been trying to reclaim this Phoenix Blood Stone. As for this guy surnamed Mo, he has the same idea.

“However, now that all of you know the truth, there’s no longer any point in recovering it.”

Chapter 230: The Legend of Being Reborn From Fire

One couldn’t exactly say that the Phoenix Blood Stones were fake. After all, the crime scene was right here—the stones were soaked in bona fide phoenix blood.

There wouldn’t be any severe ramifications even if this matter came to light. The only downside was that it would tarnish the Phoenix Tribe’s proud image in the eyes of the world, resulting in a loss of face for the tribe.

Everyone present was cognizant of the ethos of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Although it was off-kilter, the people weren’t blabbermouths who would go around announcing whatever they just found out. Thus, the truth of the Phoenix Blood Stones would most likely only circulate within the Dao-Seeking Sect.

They redirected their gazes toward Jiang Shan, who did not object to the Dao-Seeking Sect becoming a knowing party. “Who doesn’t know about the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation? They exterminate evil, uphold justice, and keep promises. I believe that the fellow Daoists here won’t spill this matter.”

Anyway, it’s not like the Phoenix Tribe has never lost face to the Dao-Seeking Sect before. Compared to that incident, selling phoenix blood is nothing that shameful anymore.

Lu Yang and the other two nodded; this was indeed not a big deal.

Li Haoran was curious as he pointed to the yamen bailiffs working on producing the Phoenix Blood Stones nearby. “Commandery Governor, how did you ensure they wouldn’t leak the secret? Was it by raising their wages?” At least a dozen people were working here. As long as one of them spilled the beans, the matter of the Phoenix Blood Stones could no longer be kept under wraps. After all, you never know when someone might let it slip.

The commandery governor shook his head. “They definitely won’t leak the secret.”

“Why’s that?”

“You should know that wearing the Phoenix Blood Stones for an extended period can boost one’s yang virility, and that is ultimately thanks to the phoenix blood contained inside. Since wearing the Phoenix Blood Stones alone can already boost one’s yang, just imagine, what would the effect of working in an environment suffused with bloody mist be like? If someone gives the secret away, none of them will be allowed to work here again next time.”

“Alright then.”

Just then, Lu Yang couldn’t help but be reminded of an ancient legend. “By the way, I heard that a phoenix can be reborn from fire.” He remembered that the old phoenix was bathed in true fire, as if it was coming back to life.

Jiang Shan nodded earnestly, his expression filled with solemnity and admiration. “Yes, but this is also regarded as little more than a legend in the Phoenix Tribe.

“Legend says that in the ancient era, there was an old ancestor in the Phoenix Tribe who was only one cultivation stage away from obtaining an immortal’s Dao Fruit. Her every gesture exuded supreme might, and she could alter the days with a single thought. She was the strongest in the history of our Phoenix Tribe, and even in the records of the entire demon race, few could rival her.

“There was once a world-shaking decisive battle between the old ancestors from the Phoenix and Dragon tribes respectively. During that battle, even the stars in the sky turned to smithereens, the radiant sun was snuffed out, and the whole universe plunged into a deathly silence.

“No one knew the outcome of that battle. However, a Transcendent Tribulation expert from the Phoenix Tribe stood at a distance and witnessed a portion of the battle. He saw our old ancestor lying quietly in the universe, devoid of any life force and their soul stilly; she had completely died. Her body was like a small boat, rising and falling with the undulating waves.

“However, the old ancestor from the Dragon Tribe didn’t think that the battle was over. Instead, she remained vigilant by the side. Suddenly, immortal fire soared from our old ancestor’s body. Bathing in the immortal fire, she spread her wings and unleashed a piercing cry to the heavens. The immortal fire was resplendent, even more dazzling than the sun, and her cries reverberated through the universe.

“Apart from the Phoenix Tribe, many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators gazed upon this epic battle from afar. If you ever have the chance to go to other demon tribes to browse their ancient records, you’ll be able to find relevant references to this event.

“From that on, the saying of the phoenix being reborn from fire emerged. However, that was only something the old ancestor could achieve. Some of our tribe members speculate that perhaps only by reaching our old ancestors’ cultivation stage can we ignore life and death and come back to life. Therefore, the notion of being reborn from the ashes is no different from a legend for ordinary members of the Phoenix Tribe like us.”

Jiang Shan spoke humbly of himself. As a pure-blooded phoenix, he was already a rare existence within the Phoenix Tribe with his noble bloodline and prominent status. Without such status, he wouldn’t have had the chance to receive guidance from Gan Tian and been sent to Luofeng Commandery to oversee the production of the Phoenix Blood Stones.

“So the matter of rebirth from the ashes is true. I thought it was just a baseless legend.” Su Yiren felt that she had broadened her horizons. She seldom interacted with others, much less conversed with members of the Phoenix Tribe.

The others also nodded, expressing that they had learned something new. “That old phoenix ancestor must have attained a prodigious realm far beyond what ordinary Transcendent Tribulation cultivators could compare to.”

Lu Yang was more concerned about another matter. “May I ask where this old ancestor from the Phoenix Tribe is now?” Perhaps I can learn the whereabouts of the Qilin Immortal through this old phoenix ancestor.

Jiang Shan shook his head. “She has disappeared for a long time. Even the oldest elders in the tribe don’t know where she went.”

“Immortal Fairy, do you know about the phoenix being reborn from fire?” It suddenly occurred to Lu Yang that his golden finger cheat—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—was residing in his mental space.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy jolted awake from her sleep. Rubbing her eyes and yawning continuously, she could barely open her eyes and was in a daze. “What did you just ask?”

“Immortal Fairy, do you know about the phoenix being reborn from fire?” Lu Yang repeated his question.

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was still groggy from her sleep, her memory was slightly muddled. Raising her head, she thought for a long while before replying, “Yes, there’s such a thing.”

As expected of the head of the five ancient immortals; she has extensive knowledge. This is what they mean by “Having an elder in the house is like having a treasure.”[1]

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned again before continuing, “I remember that the prodigies from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes were fighting for a man back then, and I happened to be watching from the side. Tsk tsk, they were so ruthless—burning paper, yanking each other’s hair, drawing circles, cursing, and unleashing a whole range of moves.”

“Hold on, what do you mean by burning paper, pulling each other’s hair, drawing circles, and cursing?” Lu Yang thought to himself, This doesn’t sound like a fight between two Transcendent Tribulation experts.

“Oh, basically, the two of them used the respective true fire of their tribes to attack each other, burned half-immortal-tier talismans, used each other’s hair as a medium, and set up arrays to cast a Tame Head Curse[2] on the other person,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained nonchalantly.

“...Please continue.”

“In any case, they fought rather fiercely. As they kept going, their attacks grew fiercer, and it seemed that the Dragon Tribe’s prodigy had the upper hand. It wasn’t their first time in a brawl. The Dragon Tribe’s prodigy had a sixty percent chance of winning, so it was normal for her to win this time.

“Just as I thought the battle was about to end, the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy showcased a unique art she had learned from me—the Play-Dead Technique. She lay on the ground and pretended to be dead. With her signs of vitality dissipated, no one could tell that she was still alive.

“The Dragon Tribe’s prodigy had never encountered a situation like this before, so she was stuck in a tough spot. If she claimed to have won, she wouldn’t feel a sense of accomplishment, while if she said that she had lost, that would be even more ridiculous. However, she couldn’t strike a dead person since it would look bad on her if word got out.

“At that moment, a brilliant idea sparked in her mind—she would burn the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy with fire.

“The Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy screamed in pain and jumped up. Her shrieks were so loud that the whole universe could hear her.

“After that, for some reason, word spread that a phoenix was reborn from fire. I have no idea who circulated the rumor. Truly unethical.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, somewhat displeased with the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy. “She hadn’t honed the Play-Dead Technique to perfection yet. If it were me, I would’ve certainly continued to play dead.

“Fortunately, no one knows that I was the one who taught her the Play-Dead Technique. She learned it so poorly that I’m too ashamed to admit that I had taught her. So embarrassing.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Aren’t you the embarrassing one, Immortal Fairy?

1. The author actually changed one character of this saying, but based on the context, I went with the meaning of the original saying. ☜

2. As explained in an earlier chapter, you can think of it as a type of witchcraft or voodoo doll. ☜

Chapter 231: Li Haoran’s Past Life

Out of respect for the Phoenix Tribe’s old ancestor and the romanticized fantasies the people had about the phoenix, Lu Yang felt that there was no need to reveal the ancient secrets he had just learned. I’m just at the Foundation Establishment Stage, yet I’m already carrying so much on my shoulders...

Logically speaking, if a Foundation Establishment cultivator were to be privy to many ancient secrets, they should be able to make use of them to attain various fortuitous opportunities.

For example, if an ancient tribe lost its legacy, Lu Yang could flash a smile and casually utter its location, allowing the ancient race to recover its legacy. They would then be so amazed by Lu Yang that they would offer their holy maiden to be his wife.

Alternatively, he might stumble across an ancient secret domain where others fiercely fought with their lives to clear trials. Leveraging his knowledge of the underlying principles, he would effortlessly claim the final reward, leaving all the prodigies stupefied.

Otherwise, everyone might be indifferent to a seemingly unremarkable treasure at an auction. No one could discern its value, and it almost went unsold. Only Lu Yang would know that it was an ancient relic of immeasurable value, which he would then acquire at a low bid.

However, none of the above fortuitous events happened to Lu Yang. Knowing all these ancient secrets is utterly useless; I can’t even use a single one.

Lu Yang pondered, Did something go wrong?

~~~

After a long night, the matter of the Phoenix Blood Stones was concluded. The biggest gains were inadvertently foiling the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s sinister plot and Li Haoran learning that Su Yiren was a physique cultivator.

When Li Haoran's parents woke up and saw the vast pit in the courtyard, they fell into deep contemplation. Everything was fine before we went to sleep. Why did such a huge hole suddenly appear out of nowhere?

As Su Yiren was worried that the commotion at night might disturb Li Haroan’s parents and Qin Yanyan from their sleep, she had set up a soundproof array to block out the noise.

Truth be told, the commotion from Su Yiren punching the old phoenix’s corpse was quite deafening. Only those in Li Haoran’s house hadn’t heard it—everyone else in Luofeng Commandery had.

The commandery governor announced to the public that the noise had stemmed from improper control of the scale of the underground works conducted at night; he apologized for the inconvenience and sought everyone’s understanding.

I can’t possibly say that it’s because I’m an incompetent commandery governor who gave the Nine-Netherworlds Creed an opening to exploit the situation and had it not been for Su Yiren, everyone would have been doomed. If I were to really say that, I can say goodbye to my position as the commandery governor.

“A small accident occurred last night. Some evil people sneaked in, but fortunately, Senior Su intervened,” Lu Yang briefly summarized the events of the previous night, leaving out the details of the Phoenix Blood Stone, the commandery governor, the head of the Mo Family, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, and the old phoenix.

In short, nothing happened last night.

Qin Yanyan cast a glance at Lu Yang who was obviously blathering nonsense. If it required my mom to step in and create such an enormous pit, something big definitely happened last night. However, since Li Haoran’s parents were present, she simply let Lu Yang ramble on.

Li Haoran’s parents nodded despite not fully understanding. Since Lu Yang promised to fill the massive cavity, they no longer pursued the matter.

It was pitch-black in the pit. However, if someone could ignore the darkness, they would see an old phoenix lying at the bottom. According to Jiang Shan, the deceased old phoenix had voluntarily chosen to be buried here, though he wasn’t cognizant of the hidden story behind it.

“Senior Su, I think...”

“Call me Yiren.” Su Yiren finally found an opportunity to correct how Li Haoran addressed her. Her tone was gentle, reminiscent of a tender embrace in which heroes could lose themselves. No one could associate her with the physique cultivator from the night before.

Although Su Yiren was a physique cultivator, she wasn’t like Third Elder, whose muscles were packed with raw, explosive power. Her figure was well-proportioned and in line with general beauty standards, resembling a fitness expert from Lu Yang’s previous world.

“Yi-Yiren...” Li Haoran stuttered.

“Aye.” Su Yiren chuckled softly.

“I feel that we might not...”

Before the words “not compatible” could leave his mouth, Su Yiren lightly pressed her index finger against Li Haoran’s lips.

“Haoran, I know you need some time to accept this truth. Both of us are cultivators with long lifespans. Let’s try to accept each other bit by bit and gradually adapt. If we’re really not compatible and it doesn’t work out, you can propose a breakup then, alright?”

Li Haoran couldn’t say anything to reject her and nodded.

Su Yiren smiled and withdrew her hand, while Qin Yanyan stomped her foot in ire at the side.

Su Yiren’s index finger might have appeared to be pressed against Li Haoran’s lips lightly, but only Li Haoran knew how much force she had exerted—so much that he couldn’t open his mouth at all.

That said, even if Su Yiren hadn’t pressed his mouth shut, he would still have wanted to give it a try with her.

Now that Su Yiren had achieved her goal of this visit, she didn’t linger. Worried that being overly zealous might make Li Haoran uncomfortable, she decided to keep a distance and give both of them some space.

Su Yiren and Qin Yanyan stayed for the day and departed after dinner. Before setting off, she secretly set up various arrays that would benefit Li Haoran’s parents and waved at Li Haoran. “I’ll come look for you when I have time.”

The next day, Li Haoran resumed his customary performance of cultivating before his parents, practicing his fists and sitting in meditation.

However, as he cultivated, he sensed that something was off. The spirit energy in him surged wave after wave. His fingers and toes involuntarily stretched out and curled out, an indication of his spirit energy overflowing.

“I’m about to advance to the next stage? That makes sense. It’s about time for me to level up.” It wasn’t Li Haoran’s first time encountering this kind of sensation. He had experienced something similar when he was at the Qi Training Stage. Although he was now at the Basic Foundation Stage, due to spending too much time soaking in lava, he was later than Lu Yang and the other three by a month.

Among the top five of their cohort, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had just entered the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, while Tao Yaoye and Man Gu had been at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage for some time; Li Haoran’s progress was the slowest. Now, he was finally catching up to the other four.

Li Haoran transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to help with guarding his cultivation. The two had woken up a long time ago and were just lounging in bed. Upon hearing that their good friend was about to advance, they didn’t even bother washing up and quickly got out of bed, rushing to the courtyard to guard Li Haoran’s cultivation.

Sitting cross-legged, Li Haoran took a couple of deep breaths, and a small vortex formed above his head, absorbing the surrounding spirit qi. The sound of crackling surfaced from within his body. This was a method to temper the body, similar to how one would refine artifacts, reinforcing the blood vessels, meridians, acupoints, and organs. His skin flushed bright red, resembling a piece of searing hot iron. As sweat was expelled from his skin, it made sizzling sounds as the fine droplets evaporated into mist anon.

Fortunately, this state didn’t last too long. Letting out a muffled grunt, his aura waves burst forth, completing a circulation around the Macrocosmic Loop[1], successfully advancing to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.

As he did so, a bunch of foreign memories appeared in his mind, though they were strangely familiar, as if he had personally lived through them before.

“Hmm?” He opened his eyes slowly with a puzzled expression.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang asked in concern, thinking that he had faced a problem with his cultivation.

“In my past life, I think...I was the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.” Li Haoran’s tone was filled with uncertainty.

“Wut?”

1. Dazhoutian is a “circulation network” as explained in an earlier chapter. I managed to find another article if you’d like to read further. ☜

Chapter 232: Senior Brother Dai, We Have Captured the Creed Leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed

“Are you sure you were the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed in your past life?” Lu Yang sized Li Haoran up, completely unable to associate him with the leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Li Haoran hesitantly replied, “It’s highly probable. Didn’t Yiren say that as my cultivation stage rises, I would receive fragments of memories from my past life? When I just broke through to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage earlier, a scene flashed past my mind.

“There was a man dressed in black, probably my subordinate. The surroundings were pitch-black, and I couldn’t make out the environment. That subordinate held a few sheets of paper and said, ‘Creed Leader, this is the creed’s spirit stone income and expenditure report for the year. Please take a look.’ I took it, and the first line on the paper read exactly ‘Nine-Netherworlds Creed Spirit Stone Income and Expenditure.’ Before I could see the remaining contents, the scene disappeared.

“They called me ‘creed leader’ and even handed me the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s accounts. It’s clear what my past life’s identity was.”

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed was one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds. Just as how the world didn’t know the name of the Everlasting Creed’s leader, the name of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader was also unknown.

But Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou now knew—his name was Qin Haoran.

Lu Yang lowered his head as he mused, That means that Li Haoran really is the reincarnation of the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

He looked at Meng Jingzhou, who was also deep in thought. “What do you think?”

Meng Jingzhou looked up, his brows furrowed. “The Nine-Netherworlds Creed is kinda poor; they didn’t even light a lamp.”

Lu Yang didn’t know how to react to that. Ignoring Meng Jingzhou’s strange line of thinking, he analyzed, “If Junior Brother Li was the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed in his past life, then some of the things Senior Su mentioned match up.

“For example, why did no one know of Qin Haoran’s existence despite him being a cultivator at the Advanced Fusion Stage? Either he was a secluded cultivator like Senior Su or his identity was special and couldn’t be revealed.

“Another point is, why was Li Haoran hunted down in the first place? There are typically two reasons. One, he acquired an extremely precious magical treasure, and the culprit wanted to murder him to plunder his goods. Second, Qin Haoran was in an extremely high position, and the culprit wanted to usurp power.

“The possibility of the first scenario happening on the Central Continent is very low. Qin Haoran’s reaction would have been to seek help from the Great Xia Dynasty. In that case, he wouldn’t have ended up crashing into Senior Su’s place afterward.

“Therefore, the second scenario is the most likely. Back then, a rebellion had erupted within the Nine-Netherworlds Creed in a wrestle for power. Qin Haoran succumbed to the opponent and suffered grave injuries.

“He never told Senior Su about his identity and even mentioned that he was doing something very dangerous, insisting that being ignorant was the only way she could stay safe. As a creed leader of one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds, he naturally couldn’t let Senior Su know about it. If she was a knowing party, once the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s affairs were exposed, she would be unable to evade severe punishment.

“Qin Haoran even claimed that his identity was special. If he didn’t break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he would never be able to walk in the light. Should a diabolic creed’s leader reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they could indeed do many things they previously didn’t dare to.”

In reality, Lu Yang had long harbored suspicions about Li Haoran’s identity, but without the evidence, he couldn’t possibly say to Su Yiren’s face, “Your husband was from the diabolic creed; he’s a bad egg.”

Lu Yang shifted his gaze to Li Haoran and smiled. “Junior Brother Li, do you now believe that you’re Qin Haoran’s reincarnation?”

In fact, Lu Yang had also once speculated that Su Yiren fabricated some memories and inseminated them in Li Haoran’s mind. Though unlikely, the possibility wasn’t zero. However, after verifying with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he could confirm that these were Li Haoran’s memories and that no one had tampered with them.

Li Haoran dropped his head dispiritedly. With what has happened, I have to believe it whether I like it or not.

Suddenly, he thought of another problem and broke out in a cold sweat. “The Great Xia Dynasty doesn’t have a rule that holds people accountable for their past lives, right?”

Lu Yang swiftly ran through all the books he had read in his mind and stated with confidence, “No, the legal principle of the Great Xia Dynasty stipulates that once a person dies, all obligations are nullified. Since you’ve already reincarnated, the Great Xia Dynasty won’t interfere.”

Li Haoran sighed in relief.

“You three are up so early?” Li Haoran’s mother smiled brightly as she noticed the three of them cultivating in the courtyard.

Lu Yang responded with a smile. “Aunt, Haoran just broke through to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.”

Both Li Haoran’s parents were at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage. Previously, Li Haoran had only surpassed them in combat power. But now, he had also overtaken them in cultivation stage, which made his mother extremely elated.

Aware that revealing the matter of his past life would only bring his parents unnecessary worry, he refrained from sharing it with them.

“Ah, then we must celebrate properly! See, didn’t I tell you? If you spend more time playing with Little Lu and Little Meng, you will definitely improve.”

Li Haoran could only reply perfunctorily, “...Ah, yes yes yes.”

During the celebratory meal, Li Haoran informed his parents that he would be returning to the sect, catching them off guard. Li Haoran’s past life identity was a massive matter the three couldn’t handle, so they needed to return to the sect and report it as soon as possible.

“You’ve only been here for a few days and you’re already leaving? Little Lu, Little Meng, have you had enough fun?”

Lu Yang put down his chopsticks as his lips curved into a convincing smile. “Junior Brother Li has just broken through and requires the seniors of the sect to help him stabilize his cultivation, so we have to go back as quickly as possible.”

This was a lie. The Dao-Seeking Sect had always promoted independence in cultivation, and there was no need for the seniors to step in to consolidate the disciples’ cultivation. However, Lu Yang’s tone was so sincere and compelling.

Li Haoran’s parents immediately stopped exhorting the three to stay for a few more days.

~~~

Once again, the old horse pulled the carriage, taking the three of them back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Meng Jingzhou urged the old horse to speed up, and it nodded slowly and continued at a leisurely pace, though its every step covered hundreds or thousands of li.

“Junior Brother Li, your identity as the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed has great potential. Once we return to the sect, if we handle things well, we could reap lots of profit. After the job is done, how about a thirty-seventy split?”

“Such a good deal?”

“Of course, but you’ll have to suffer a bit first, Junior Brother.”

Not long after, the three arrived at the Dao-Seeking Sect and headed for the Great Mission Hall.

“Is Senior Brother Dai inside?” Lu Yang asked a senior male disciple on duty.

The male disciple looked up to see Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou smiling down at him, with a burlap sack slung over Meng Jingzhou’s shoulder.

“Senior Brother Dai is inside. He told me that if you need to look for him, you can just go right in. But what’s in this burlap sack...”

“Spoils of war.”

“Oh, go in then.” The male disciple didn’t think much of it. Anyway, it won’t be hazardous goods.

The two carried the sack as they entered Dai Bufan’s room. As usual, Dai Bufan was flipping through scrolls, searching for clues about the missions.

“What brings you two here?”

Meng Jingzhou spoke first. “Good news, Senior Brother Dai! Through our tireless efforts, we have finally captured the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Just wondering, how many contribution points would this meritorious service earn us?”

“Creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Dai Bufan eyed Meng Jingzhou suspiciously. Since Meng Jingzhou wasn’t lying, he had no guilty conscience and met Dai Bufan’s gaze.

Dai Bufan then looked at Lu Yang. Lu Yang also had no guilty conscience and dared to meet Dai Bufan’s gaze.

Dai Bufan was even more befuddled as he brooded over it. I have no idea what these two buffoons are up to. “Where is the leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?”

Meng Jingzhou loosened the burlap sack, revealing a bound Li Haoran with his mouth gagged. With an air of righteousness, Meng Jingzhou pointed at him. “It’s this scoundrel!”

Dai Bufan, “...”

Are you two taking me for an idiot?

Chapter 233: I see

When Meng Jingzhou saw that Dai Bufan was not buying it, he began to delve into his vivid story. “The two of us went out a few days ago and noticed black smoke billowing from a mountain stream. Assuming that some demons were causing trouble in the mortal realm, we rushed straight to the scene. That evil culprit claimed to be the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and possessed remarkable abilities. Fortunately, we were also no ordinary people. With a few tricks and a fierce life-and-death struggle, we finally captured him. When we removed the mask, we realized that it was Li Haoran!

“The leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, so mysterious and elusive—yet we actually caught him. We’re not asking for much. Just three acting sect leader vouchers for each of us would do.”

Dai Bufan finally pieced his words together. “...Do you even hear what you’re saying?” Despite being the most senior among the disciples and having lived nearly a thousand years, never had Dai Bufan felt his intelligence insulted like this before.

Lu Yang shrugged and squatted down to untie Li Haoran. “I told you Senior Brother Dai wouldn’t believe us.”

The promise to offer thirty percent of the contribution points to Li Haoran after the job was done could no longer be fulfilled.

“Why doesn’t he believe us? We really caught the leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.” Meng Jingzhou reflected on himself and concluded that he had only uttered the truth.

“Alright, what’s really going on?” Although Dai Bufan knew that these two were buffoons and troublemakers, he knew they wouldn’t joke about something like this. There must be a reason behind this.

Of course, if these two dare to say they’re here to cheat contribution points, I’ll truss them up and hang them at the entrance of the Great Mission Hall.

Lu Yang began, “Ahem, here’s what happened. Initially, Li Haoran was a bit nervous about meeting his fiancée and asked us to support him. Later, we discovered that his fiancée was beautiful, kind, and had a higher cultivation than Li Haoran. She was perfect in every way, though there was just one problem—she is slightly older.”

Dai Bufan sat with one leg propped over the other. He sipped some tea and casually asked, “Being slightly older is not a problem. Where is the woman from? Is she one or two years older?”

“Two thousand years older.”

Ptui! Dai Bufan spat his tea out.

He thought he had misheard it. Coughing violently, he took a long while to recover. “Say that again? Two thousand years?”

Isn’t she from the same generation as the sect leader and shifu?

Dai Bufan sized up Li Haoran several times, but he still couldn’t discern what was so charming about Li Haoran.

Lu Yang introduced, “Junior Brother Li’s fiancée is called Su Yiren, and she is a cultivator at the Fusion Stage.”

“Oh, Su Yiren? I’ve heard that she’s a beauty. She should be cultivating on Sky Pillar Mountain.” As Dai Bufan managed all the information in the Dao-Seeking Sect, he had eyes and ears throughout the Central Continent, keeping him apprised of affairs involving Fusion cultivators, something ordinary people were not acquainted with.

Lu Yang continued, “Senior Su’s husband was called Qin Haoran, and he was also a Fusion cultivator. He died during his breakthrough to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but due to the special nature of his cultivation technique, he reincarnated.”

Qin Haoran? Dai Bufan riffled through his memories of Fusion cultivators but couldn’t recall anyone by that name.

Lu Yang elaborated, “Qin Haoran reincarnated as Junior Brother Li, and Senior Su became Junior Brother Li’s fiancée so that they could rekindle their past relationship.

“Later in Luofeng Commandery, we accidentally discovered traces of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s activities. Senior Su took action and foiled their sinister plot, eventually leading us to witness the process of producing the Phoenix Blood Stones.”

“You saw Luofeng Commandery soaking the stones in phoenix blood?” Dai Bufan was not surprised.

“You knew about this, Senior Brother Dai?” Lu Yang was astounded.

Dai Bufan rolled his eyes. “You can figure that out easily. What kind of Fusion cultivator can leave behind an ore vein that can be mined for four thousand years after their death? What, does the phoenix have no flesh and only blood?

“It’s just that Phoenix Blood Stones are hard to find. They’re worried that if this matter gets exposed, the Phoenix Tribe will be incensed from the humiliation and stop selling their blood.”

Lu Yang replied, “...Fine then.

“Later on, Junior Brother Li broke through and obtained memory fragments of his past life and learned that he was once the leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

After Lu Yang finished speaking, Dai Bufan didn’t make any comment, rhythmically tapping his finger on the table. “Reincarnation, incarnation, Nine-Netherworlds Creed... The Nine-Netherworlds Creed believes that there’s a place of reincarnation called the Nine Netherworlds, and Li Haoran is the reincarnation of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader...”

“Senior Dai, is reincarnation really possible?”

Dai Bufan shook his head. “I don’t know, but there are many rumors among the common folk. For example, in the north, there’s a divine child who radiates golden light, is born with knowledge, can traverse through the sky and beneath the earth, and is viewed as the reincarnation of an immortal spirit. They are revered as a god by the locals.”

“And what was the truth?”

“A fool didn’t cultivate properly, and his nascent soul escaped.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

“In another instance, a young male prodigy with extraordinary talent appeared in a small sect. One day, an expert visited the sect and was completely stunned. This youth’s talent and appearance were extremely similar to a deceased old friend of theirs.”

“What happened next?”

“Later, the expert realized that his old friend had feigned his death just so that he could return to his youthful years and show off at a small sect.”

Li Haoran, “...”

“In any case, these rumors about reincarnation on the streets are not to be trusted. They’re either unfounded stories or false news created to generate buzz for whatever strange reasons. From what I’ve gathered, not a single one of these so-called reincarnations is true.

“The matter of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader involves many things, and reincarnation is likewise beyond my ken. It’s best to leave it to Big Senior Sister.”

“Then let’s look for Big Senior Sister...” Before Lu Yang could finish his sentence, a cold voice interrupted him.

“No need, I’m already here.” The tone was frosty like a glacier of ten thousand years.

Space warped, and a graceful figure walked out from an unknown dimension, appearing before the four of them. It was none other than Yun Zhi.

While they were speaking, Dai Bufan had already informed Yun Zhi.

“I didn’t expect Junior Brother Li to be the reincarnation of a formidable expert. Reincarnation doesn’t originally exist; it’s just a myth. If Junior Brother Li is really the reincarnation of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader, that could only be the result of a Dao Fruit.” Yun Zhi recalled her speculations on the Four Great Diabolic Creeds. “Could the Nine-Netherworlds Creed have formed the Incipient Reincarnation Dao Fruit a long time ago?

“Open your mind and don’t think about anything.”

Li Haoran quickly cleared his spirit platform until it was a blank canvas.

Yun Zhi’s eyes were exceptionally beautiful and mesmerizing; they seemed to contain the countless stars in the sky and encompass all the profound secrets of the world, drawing people into a trance as they lost themselves inside.

This pair of eyes was like immortal eyes that could see through everything in the legends and the heavenly eye from one of the Buddhist Six Mighty Abilities. Only Dai Bufan knew that this was a unique technique Yun Zhi had invented, a method only she could use.

Li Haoran felt as if Yun Zhi had incisively seen through every bit of secret about himself, including his past, growth, cultivation process, and inner thoughts; nothing could escape from those eyes of hers.

Yun Zhi withdrew her gaze, closed her eyes, and then opened them again, her eyes returning to normal.

Li Haoran heaved a sigh of relief. The pressure from Yun Zhi just now had been overwhelming.

“I see.” Yun Zhi’s voice exuded an air of unquestionable confidence, as if she had unraveled some mystery and perceived the truth.

Lu Yang hurriedly asked, “Big Senior Sister, what did you find out?”

Yun Zhi replied in a calm and impassive manner, “I found out that there are things even I can’t see.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Big Senior Sister, is everything okay with you?

Chapter 234: The Difference Between Li Haoran and Lu Yang

When Yun Zhi stated that she couldn’t discern anything either, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy sighed in relief. “Hehe, I told you, this is beyond our expertise. No one can perceive it.”

This means that my eyesight is not the problem—and that’s the fact.

“I observed Junior Brother Li’s body, but I couldn’t see anything different about him. There are no signs of a Dao Fruit.”

“So there’s nothing wrong with my body?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “No, this actually shows that there is something wrong. If your body is no different from an ordinary person’s, where did the memory fragments come from?

“The matter of Dao Fruits is connected to the principles of the world, and I, too, cannot fully understand it. Junior Brother Li’s case has to be considered at length.

“Junior Brother Li, if you obtain more memory fragments in the future, please inform the sect. The more we know, the easier it will be to analyze what exactly happened to you. Besides, this is also an opportunity to understand the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

Li Haoran nodded. I’ll definitely be informing the sect if I receive more memory fragments. Keeping it to myself makes me so queasy.

I’m a mere cultivator at the Foundation Establishment Stage, yet I suddenly learned that I was the creed leader of one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds. Anyone would be uneasy. I need to find a backing; fortunately, the biggest backing is right here where I am—the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“I have one more question.”

“Feel free to ask.”

“You mentioned ‘Dao Fruit’ earlier, but what exactly is a Dao Fruit?”

Only then did Dai Bufan remember that Li Haoran didn’t know what a Dao Fruit was. It does make sense when I think about it. A Dao Fruit is the fundamental aspect of becoming an immortal. How could a Foundation Establishment cultivator have the right to such information?

But why did I previously assume that it was perfectly normal for Foundation Establishment cultivators to know about Dao Fruits?

Dai Bufan shifted his gaze to the two other Foundation Establishment cultivators present—Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Why do you two know about Dao Fruits?

~~~

The matter of Dao Fruits was a top-level secret; even ordinary Fusion cultivators knew little about it. Only those at the Advanced or Apex Fusion Stages were qualified to access affairs related to the Dao Fruit. One example was Su Yiren. She only had a general understanding of the concept but knew even less than Lu Yang did.

On the other hand, Dai Bufan was an exception. Although he was only at the Basic Fusion Stage, he managed the Great Mission Hall and wielded control over numerous intelligence networks, allowing him to acquire considerable information about the Dao Fruit. Moreover, it would be a mistake to treat his combat power as equivalent to that of a Basic Fusion cultivator.

Logically speaking, Li Haoran was not eligible to learn about the Dao Fruit, but since an Incipient Dao Fruit could be hidden within him, it would be unconscionable to keep the involved party in the dark. Therefore, Yun Zhi gave Li Haoran a brief rundown on Dao Fruits.

Only then did Li Haoran understand how important he was. He was connected not only to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed but also to a potential path to immortal ascension.

If outsiders found out about this, countless would be tempted. Just like in his previous life, Li Haoran was a piece of highly coveted Tang Monk flesh.[1] Regardless of whether they could obtain the Reincarnation Dao Fruit, their priority was to kidnap him first.

~~~

Back on Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang was a little worried about Li Haoran’s situation. “The one behind the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit is an immortal. Could it also be the case for the Incipient Reincarnation Dao Fruit?” If an immortal were to take action and abduct Li Haoran, snatching away the Reincarnation Dao Fruit or an incipient form would be effortless; Li Haoran doesn’t have the slightest chance of resisting.

Yun Zhi replied, “That’s why I suggested that Junior Brother Li shouldn’t leave the sect unless necessary. As long as he’s in the Dao-Seeking Sect, he’s safe.” Her tone was calm, but it conveyed absolute confidence.

She didn’t request the same of Lu Yang. Whenever Lu Yang wanted to go out, she would never stop him, even encouraging him to step out of the Dao-Seeking Sect to see the world.

In reality, Lu Yang’s situation was more dangerous than Li Haoran’s. Li Haoran simply might have an incipient Dao Fruit within him, but Lu Yang had a bona fide immortal residing in him that everyone wanted to kill, along with the Everlasting Dao Fruit, which even the four ancient immortals envied.

However, should Lu Yang find himself in peril, he could unleash the ultimate form of the Animal Form Fist and summon his Big Senior Sister. If Li Haoran were the Tang Monk, Lu Yang would be the Tang Monk who could summon Buddha. Their safety levels were on completely different planes.

“I heard from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that the emergence of a Dao Fruit represents the emergence of a new rule in the world. After the ancient era, was there any Dao Fruit that affected the whole world?”

Yun Zhi stared at Lu Yang silently, her eyes as tranquil as the surface of a lake. Lu Yang was on tenterhooks under her gaze. It was unclear how much time had passed—a few seconds, a few minutes, or a whole lifetime—until Yun Zhi slowly said, “Senior, please come out for a chat.”

“What’s going on?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was clueless about the situation.

“Little Junior Brother is still at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Being cognizant of too many secrets that only experts are qualified to know could easily foster an overambitious mindset, which would hinder his future cultivation. Senior, please consider his cultivation realm when sharing such matters in the future.”

“Oh, fine then.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy actually wanted to say that she did consider Lu Yang’s cultivation realm, but she didn’t dare to refute Yun Zhi. Just wait until I regain my strength one day! I’ll be the one suppressing this little lass instead!

“After the ancient era, there was a Dao Fruit that affected the entire world. You are very familiar with its impact.” Yun Zhi reckoned it would be fine for Lu Yang to know about this.

“I’m very familiar with it?” Lu Yang was slightly surprised. Aside from the changes regarding the stars and continent, what else is different from ancient times?

It wasn’t just Lu Yang; even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t figure out what was different.

“It’s the Great Xia Dynasty.” Yun Zhi revealed the answer.

“What about the Great Xia Dynasty?” Lu Yang still hadn’t fully internalized it.

“The entire Great Xia Dynasty.”

Lu Yang’s eyes widened in shock. What do you mean by the entire Great Xia Dynasty?

He repeatedly asked Yun Zhi what she meant, but she felt that the rest was beyond what Lu Yang should know at his current cultivation realm, so she didn’t elaborate further.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered for a bit and seemed to have grasped something.

“Little Junior Brother, have you found any ideas for your golden core formation?” As Lu Yang’s Big Senior Sister in name and shifu in reality, Yun Zhi often paid attention to his progress in cultivation.

Lu Yang shook his head helplessly. “There are too many types of golden cores. It’s honestly hard to choose. I still haven’t decided what kind of golden core I want to form.”

But I can definitely rule out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Unbeatable Golden Core first.

He had followed Li Haoran home, originally hoping to gain some inspiration from encountering different people or events during his journey. The greatest takeaway from my travels is that soft rice is absolutely delicious—being a kept man is great.

So should I form a Woman’s Soft Rice Golden Core?

But it’d be too embarrassing to say that out loud.

“There’s no need to be too anxious and rush into forming a golden core. Just let nature take its course.”

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, I read about the insights to golden core formation from many senior brothers and sisters in the scripture library, but only yours wasn’t written. How did you form your golden core back then, and what type was it?

With the person in question right here, Lu Yang couldn’t help but be curious.

Who knows, perhaps I’m as outstanding as Big Senior Sister?

1. In Journey to the West, Tang Sanzang is a monk and one of the main cast. It is said that demons can gain eternal life if they eat him, which is why he requires the assistance of Sun Wuzong and the other two companions to guard him on his journey (to the West). Thus, the expression “flesh of the Tang monk” refers to something that is coveted by everyone. ☜

Chapter 235: Big Senior Sister’s Golden Core Formation Method

“Do you really want to know?”

“Yes, yes.” Lu Yang nodded vigorously like a small chick pecking at rice grains.

Yun Zhi mulled over it for a while and reckoned that there was no harm in telling him. I’ll just take it as satisfying Little Junior Brother’s curiosity. “Fine, since you want to know, I’ll tell you. Just listen; don’t try to learn from me.”

“I definitely won’t,” Lu Yang promised.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also very interested in the golden core Yun Zhi had formed. It can’t be stronger than my Unbeatable Golden Core, right?

Yun Zhi began to recall her past. “That was a few hundred years ago...”

Lu Yang blurted out in astonishment, “A few hundred years ago?!”

Yun Zhi was a peerless, icy beauty who appeared to be in her twenties. When she and Lu Yang walked together through the streets, they looked like siblings. Moreover, Yun Zhi treated Lu Yang more like a precocious peer rather than an elder, giving Lu Yang the impression that she was about the same age as him.

Now that Yun Zhi mentioned how her golden core formation was several hundreds of years ago, Lu Yang realized that she was the most senior among the disciples. Her actual age was far greater than what he had guessed.

Exactly how old is Big Senior Sister? A few hundreds years old? Could she be almost a thousand years old?

Lu Yang’s thought process might seem complicated, but all of it happened in merely a fraction of a second. He didn’t even have the time to think through these thoughts as he accidentally voiced them out.

As soon as the words left Lu Yang’s mouth, he could sense his impending demise.

Yun Zhi’s gaze slowly shifted to Lu Yang’s shoulder. For a split second, Lu Yang felt like there was a sharp, gleaming saber pressed against his neck, as though he was walking on the boundary between life and death, with only a single thought separating him from death. Fortunately, this sensation came quickly and faded as fast. Yun Zhi withdrew her gaze and didn’t dwell on Lu Yang’s excessive curiosity.

She continued, “A few hundred years ago, I had cultivated until the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage and was preparing to form my golden core. At that time, Shifu saw that I possessed exceptional talent and had the potential to shoulder great responsibility in the future, so he shared with me some secrets to prepare me for what lay ahead. That included the matter of the Ancient Nameless One refining the stars into the continent and how most of the stars we see now are phantom images, while the real stars are beneath our feet.”

It was a consensus in the cultivation world that only those minimally at the Nascent Soul Stage were qualified to learn that the stars were false. The general populace and ordinary cultivators could just believe that the world was at peace; otherwise, they might wonder: if the Ancient Nameless One could refine the stars into the continent, could he once again refine the continent into the stars?

Since it would cause unnecessary worry, it was better not to inform the masses.

Yun Zhi reminded, “I should have told you before that I grew up in a secret domain when I was young. It was only later that I left and came to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang nodded. Big Senior Sister did mention this before. She said she grew up in a secret domain and only interacted with cultivators. It was the same even after she came to the Dao-Seeking Sect. That’s why she doesn’t understand mortal habits and wasn’t aware that mortals can’t bathe in boiling water.

This was the explanation Yun Zhi provided when she applied medicine to Lu Yang’s skin after it became red and swollen from the boiling water bath.

Yun Zhi reminisced, “There was no night sky in the secret domain. After I left and arrived in the outside world, I saw the stars twinkling in the night sky and marveled at the mesmerizingly beautiful vista. In my spare time from cultivation, I often lay on the grass, gazing at the stars and counting them.

“When Shifu told me that the stars had actually long disappeared from the sky, I didn’t show it on the outside, but I was deeply disappointed inside. The stars I usually admired were just vestigial illusions from three hundred thousand years ago. As long as that thought stayed in my mind, I could no longer find the night sky enchanting.

“As I contemplated what kind of golden core I should form, I read in the Golden Core Treatise, ‘Gold is something tough, perpetual, and indestructible; Core is something complete, radiant, and flawless.’”

An absurd thought vaguely emerged in Lu Yang’s mind. Big Senior Sister, surely you wouldn’t have done something so outrageous...

He heard Yun Zhi say, “At that time, I thought, isn’t a flawless and indestructible golden core precisely the stars in my eyes?

“Since the stars are gone, why don’t I use golden cores to replace them and recreate the resplendent night sky of ancient times?”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Just as I thought, Big Senior Sister.

“Among golden cores, first grade is the best. Hence, I formed my golden core according to the stars in my heart and invented a new type of first-grade golden core called the Resplendent Stars Golden Core.

“In the beginning, I was a bit unfamiliar with the golden core formation technique, but the more golden cores I formed, the faster I became. Throughout my Golden Core Stage, I mainly devoted myself to continuously forming golden cores, striving to accumulate enough until their number matched the stars in the sky.”

Lu Yang inhaled sharply. Big Senior Sister, you really dare to dream and act on it.

“At the Golden Core Stage, it was difficult to replace the stars with golden cores. When I broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage, I shattered one of the golden cores to develop a nascent soul, while the rest remained inside me.

“Later, when I was more successful with my cultivation, I took out all the golden cores in me and used them to replace the illusions of stars in the sky. Unfortunately, there were too many of them in the sky. Even though I had tried my best to form golden cores, I still couldn’t make their number equivalent to the stars.

“However, having something is better than nothing. After all, the effort I had poured in to form golden cores was to replace the illusionary stars with them.”

“So, the stars in the sky now...a portion of them are your golden cores?” Lu Yang asked gingerly. Yun Zhi’s actions were so preposterous that Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel a sense of respect.

“Just a small portion.”

“...A small portion is already a lot.” Lu Yang didn’t know what else to say.

Yun Zhi was still worried about Lu Yang, so she exhorted him a few times, “My golden core formation method is different from ordinary people. Don’t try to imitate me just because you find it rare and interesting.”

“I definitely won’t.” If Lu Yang’s previous promise was perfunctory, his promise now stemmed from his true inner thoughts. It’d be too ridiculous if this could be imitated. It’s obvious that forming a golden core is anything but as simple as Big Senior Sister had made it sound.

What did she mean by the more golden cores she formed, the faster she became? Does that even make sense? No wonder she had written in her golden core experience, “My method of forming a Golden Core has no reference value. Please do not imitate. Those who learn from me will die, and those who resemble me will die.”

Sometimes, I feel that the disparity between people is even bigger than the gap between humans and dogs. We’re all cultivators, but why are you the only one so absurd?

“Immortal Fairy, can your Unbeatable Golden Core rival Big Senior Sister’s?” Lu Yang stealthily asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed. “It’s just a bunch of golden cores. No matter how many useless golden cores you have, they’re still trash. As the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage, you must remember that we value quality over quantity. This little lass has a high quantity of golden cores, but my golden core is of a high quality. These two are not comparable.”

“Do you dare repeat this in front of Big Senior Sister?”

“No, I don’t dare to,” she replied, full of self-assurance.

Lu Yang was rendered speechless. I thought that by relying on the backing of Big Senior Sister and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, my journey in cultivation should be smooth sailing. But from the looks of it now, none of them can be relied on.

Speaking of which, exactly how old is Big Senior Sister?

Chapter 236: Big Senior Sister’s Age

“I’ll repeat this: don’t try to imitate me,” Yun Zhi reminded multiple times, worried that Lu Yang might take things too hard and insist on competing with her.

“I’ll definitely definitely not imitate you!” Lu Yang vowed.

“Alright, I’m going to cultivate. You may continue to select a method for forming your golden core.”

“Understood.”

After learning the specifics of Yun Zhi’s golden core formation, Lu Yang immediately abandoned all ideas of learning from her. This method is too outrageous. I’m just someone with a Sword Spirit Root, nondescript and unremarkable. I lack the kind of talent Big Senior Sister has.
