The nursery rhyme is supposed to be “Twinkle, twinkle, little star; How I wonder what you are.” But perhaps it should now be changed to “Twinkle, twinkle, golden cores; How I wonder where you’re from.”[1]

It makes sense, and it’s catchy.

With that question settled, another sprang up in his mind.

Exactly how old is Big Senior Sister? How many hundred years old is she?

Lu Yang was itching to uncover the truth. He recalled that Dai Bufan had been in charge of the first round of the sect’s entrance trials. Senior Dai Bufan could tell a person’s spirit root and age with just a touch. “Immortal Fairy, do you have any spells that can determine other people’s ages?”

“I do.”

Lu Yang had only brought it up casually, not expecting a positive response. Nothing less from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Hehe, this spell of mine is amazing. It can ignore the other party’s cultivation and lets you see their age.”

“So powerful?!” Lu Yang exclaimed.

“Of course! Don’t you know who I am?!”

Since it was a minor spell, or rather, a simple trick, it was easy to pick up. After reciting ancient phrases and practicing twice, Lu Yang had it down. Activating the ancient spell, he felt that the sight before him had broadened, as if he had just comprehended something.

“Let me test it on myself first.” Lu Yang stretched out his hands and saw a number appearing before his eyes: sixteen years old.

Correct, I’m only sixteen years old.

“Let’s try it on the Immortal Fairy now.” Lu Yang shifted the spell to the happy-go-lucky Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and a number again showed up before him: sixteen years old.

“Hmm?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy always brags that she’s a prodigy and beauty who passed away in her prime and is now only sixteen years old.

But I can tell that it’s all rubbish even if I use my buttocks to think.

Sixteen years old and already an immortal? Is a whole era equivalent to one year old?

Completely baffled, he checked a senior male disciple who passed by. It’s also sixteen years old!

“...Immortal Fairy, is there something wrong with your spell? Why does it display ‘sixteen years old’ for everyone?” Considering his dark track record, Lu Yang wondered if he had cultivated it wrong.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke with overwhelming confidence. “Forget whether the age is accurate. Just tell me whether you’re able to ignore one’s cultivation to see the age!”

Lu Yang was at a loss for words.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Back in the ancient era, everyone liked to use age to determine their seniority, but that wasn’t a good thing. Are older people always right and younger people always wrong?

“In order to turn around such a situation, I specifically invented this spell that shows everyone’s age as sixteen years old. Unfortunately, my ideas were too forward-thinking back then, and people couldn’t accept them.”

Lu Yang remarked, “Your idea is still very forward-thinking now.”

So how can I figure out Big Senior Sister’s age? The first method Lu Yang came up with was to find out which cohort of disciples he was from. The Dao-Seeking Sect, or rather, the Five Great Immortal Sects, were very regular in their recruitment cycle; they took in a batch of disciples every year without fail.

However, he soon dismissed the idea. The Dao-Seeking Sect dared to accept even Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Contrary to what it seemed, the bar for entry was set absurdly high. In fact, the cohort Lu Yang belonged to had a larger intake than usual. Some candidates might meet the criterion for spirit root but not their mindset, and they wouldn’t be able to join the Dao-Seeking Sect. This resulted in cases where the Dao-Seeking Sect couldn’t recruit anyone. That meant that Lu Yang couldn’t calculate Yun Zhi’s age by deducing which batch of disciples she was from.

Lu Yang mumbled, “Shall I ask Senior Brother Dai Bufan then? He’s from the same cohort as Big Senior Sister, so he surely knows her age!” He decided to act on his idea right away, but due to what happened during the third round of the selection trials, he couldn’t help but feel guilty when facing Dai Bufan alone.

Let me find a helper.

~~~

“Go ask Senior Dai about Big Senior Sister’s age?” Meng Jingzhou’s countenance betrayed his eagerness. “Won’t Big Senior Sister find out?”

“She won’t. She was still cultivating when I left; she won’t have time to notice us.”

“Then what are we waiting for? Go go go!” Meng Jingzhou urged Lu Yang.

~~~

“You want to ask about Big Senior Sister’s age?” Dai Bufan stared at them with a weird expression. “You two have quite the guts to dare ask about such a secret! Be careful not to invite calamity!” Dai Bufan was kind enough to warn the two of them.

This matter is a top-level secret in the Dao-Seeking Sect, even more confidential than information on Dao Fruits. It mustn’t be divulged to others.

“Do you know what happened to the last disciple who asked this question?!” Dai Bufan asked ominously.

“We’re just asking casually.” Meng Jingzhou put on his professional smile, which looked very fake.

“Yes, that’s right, we’re just concerned about Big Senior Sister. We know how hard it is for her to work day and night for the sect, so we would like to know her age to prepare a suitable gift for her.” Lu Yang flashed the same smile as Meng Jingzhou.

Dai Bufan rolled his eyes. Only a fool would believe them.

This is taboo. I mustn’t say anything.

“Aren’t you afraid that Big Senior Sister will find out?” Dai Bufan questioned.

Meng Jingzhou grinned slyly. “Hehe, Big Senior Sister is cultivating now and can’t spare any attention to what’s happening here. Senior Brother Dai, as long as you keep silent, she definitely won’t know about this!”

Dai Bufan shook his head. “Big Senior Sister is omnipotent. How could she possibly not find out? Let me give you a word of caution, don’t ask anymore; this question is extremely dangerous.”

“It won’t be dangerous.” Meng Jingzhou didn’t think that this matter was a big deal.

Dai Bufan smirked. “Is that so? In that case, why don’t you turn around and ask the person in question?”

“Huh? What do you mean?”

A sense of foreboding immediately swelled within them. They felt as if the surrounding temperature was plummeting drastically, close to freezing them into ice sculptures. They turned their heads stiffly and saw Yun Zhi standing right behind them with an elegant deportment. She was staring at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, her face devoid of emotions.

Dai Bufan sighed. “See? I already told you not to ask this question, for it will invite calamity.”

From the moment the two had found him, Yun Zhi had been standing behind quietly. Dai Bufan tried his best to hint to them, but the two were bent on digging their own graves; no one could stop them.

Perhaps this tribulation is meant to be.

Yun Zhi softly called out, “Little Junior Brother.”

Lu Yang jumped in fright as he hastily answered, “Here!”

“Junior Brother Meng.”

“Here!”

“Do the two of you find cultivation too boring? Is that why you have the time to care about such a trivial matter?” Yun Zhi’s voice contained a rare trace of gentleness, as if she was concerned about Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s progress in cultivation.

Cold sweat poured down Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, drenching their clothes. They shuddered non-stop, lost for words.

1. The Chinese version of this nursery rhyme is somewhat different from the original. Instead of “How I wonder what you are,” it’s “The sky is full of little stars.” Here, it is then changed to “The sky is full of golden cores.” ☜

Chapter 237: Penal Exile

“I suppose you have found your cultivation boring recently and lack the motivation to advance your cultivation realm, so you have decided to concern yourselves with such trivial matters instead.

“Since that’s the case, why don’t you two go to the border between the Central Continent and the Demon Region for some training and experience?”

“Big Senior Sister, this might not...”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou still wanted to resist, but Yun Zhi didn’t give them a chance. Grabbing them by the collar in each hand like she was carrying two little rabbits, she casually tossed them out.

The two only felt the scenery change before their eyes as they appeared mid-air and flew, or rather, were thrown southward at an incredibly terrifying speed. Their surroundings changed so rapidly that they couldn’t even deduce their current speed. They could only catch sight of the occasional flying vessels or cultivation experts passing by in a flash. The passengers on the flying vessels and cultivation experts were left nonplussed, secretly wondering what cultivation level the two had attained for them to fly at such astonishing speeds.

~~~

Thud! As the two descended headfirst with their legs pointing skyward, they were promptly snared by tree vines.

“I feel like my body’s falling apart.” Lu Yang grimaced in pain as he got up. It felt as if he had been dismantled and then reassembled.

“Where are we?” Meng Jingzhou surveyed the environment around them. It was a dense forest with many rare plants growing nearby, and the air was extremely humid.

“Didn’t Big Senior Sister say that we should train at the border with the Demon Region? This is probably the place.” Lu Yang pointed out the local specialties. “Look, these are all rare on the Central Continent. This is the Money Flower, this is the Drifting Cloud Grass, this is the Evergreen Tree, and this is a snake demon whose cultivation realm we can’t tell... Hmm?”

Several dark green snake demons with triangular heads appeared, hissing with their tongues out as they rapidly slithered toward the two.

“Run!”

The two couldn’t see which cultivation stage the snake demons were at, so they dared not act recklessly. Quickly freeing themselves from the tree vines, they somersaulted as they dropped to the ground, taking to their heel right away. These snake demons clearly spelled trouble, though it wouldn’t be a problem if they were at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Their only fear was that these snake demons’ cultivation was higher.

“Handsome brothers, don’t run; come play with us sisters,” the snake demons spoke in human language, their voices seductive and tingling.

“We little sisters will definitely make you feel heavenly~

“Come play~”

The two turned their heads back and noticed that the snake demons had transformed into human form. Their appearances were enchanting and pitiable. They were scantily clad, their get-up practically screaming that they didn’t come from respectable households.

“No no, you’re too ugly,” Meng Jingzhou refused politely.

The snake demons were stunned for a moment before rage took over, and they chased the two even faster.

Fortunately, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were not to be underestimated. Escaping abilities were their forte, and their legs moved at lightning speed.

Unfortunately, misfortune never comes alone. Suddenly, they found themselves falling into a swamp.

Seeing the snake demons almost catching up to them, Lu Yang steeled himself. “This won’t do. Let’s escape with Shrinking Earth.”

“What about me?”

“Stand still. Draw Underground Prison!” Lu Yang quickly drew a circle around Meng Jingzhou. Before the latter could react, he found himself in an underground prison.

Lu Yang performed Shrinking Earth, pushing the underground prison and its inmate, Meng Jingzhou, as he fled.

“These two spells can be used together?”

The snake demons were in a daze, not registering what had just happened. By the time they spread out their spiritual consciousness to search for the two, they were already long gone, leaving no trace behind.

“Are we really so scary?” The snake demons exchanged glances with one another. They had hoped to use their bodies to earn some spirit stones from humans, but they didn’t expect the humans to possess such resolute willpower, running away as soon as they saw them.

What’s even more absurd is that when we offered them to play with our bodies, they ran even faster.

They were from the Jade Sky Green Snake Tribe, known in the Demon Region for such business. Now, they wanted to expand their operations into human society, but they hadn’t clinched a single successful deal.

“Should we go apply for a job at the humans’ brothels instead of coming here for some battles in the wild? I heard that’s what many of our sisters do,” one of the snake demons commented.

“Didn’t they say that humans like to play in the wild? Besides, there’s no need to pay tax out here.”

“I don’t get it.”

~~~

Meanwhile, Lu Yang was still madly fleeing while pushing Meng Jingzhou along, his two legs as nimble as fish swimming.

“Should be good now, right?”

“We should have escaped.”

The two popped their heads out of the earth at the same time, only to see a giant elephant’s foot stomping toward them. Behind the elephant trailed a whole herd, eyes bloodshot and tusks over three meters long—it was clear they spelled trouble.

Lu Yang immediately pulled himself and Meng Jingzhou back underground.

The two peeked out again, only to see a tiger-like and leopard-like demon beast crouching over a deer demon’s corpse and devouring it with relish.

As the two humans and one demon beast made eye contact, they froze for a split second before the demon beast let out a roar.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou retreated underground once more and fled for their lives.

Finally, the two of them burrowed out of the earth, leaning against their crutches. It was unknown what setbacks they had endured yet again.

“How can this be called training? This is simply pe...”

Before the words “penal exile”[1] could leave his mouth, Lu Yang interrupted him. “Don’t talk nonsense! This is the training Big Senior Sister has given us!” He was more cautious than Meng Jingzhou. Fearing that Yun Zhi might have some methods to monitor their situation, he desperately signaled to Meng Jingzhou with his eyes. He was worried that if Meng Jingzhou angered Yun Zhi, she might add even more torture to their ordeal.

Meng Jingzhou instantly got his clue and hastily changed his words. “Pe-perceiving that our cultivation realms are unstable, which is why she wants us to fight it out here and seek an opportunity for breakthrough!”

“Where do we go now? We can’t stay here forever, right?” Lu Yang limped along, deeply appreciating the hardships of survival.

“Don’t worry. Since this is the border between the Central Continent and the Demon Region, there must be large cities nearby! I heard from my family that the Great Xia Dynasty has established six cities here to guard against the demon race. One of my uncles is stationed in one of those cities!”

“Hmm? What’s that on your arm?” Lu Yang noticed a tiny black worm wriggling on Meng Jingzhou’s arm. Its head was thick, while its tail was thin. He didn’t know when it had climbed there.

“It’s a leech!” Meng Jingzhou flung his arm in horror, but the leech seemed stuck, no matter how hard he flailed.

“Don’t panic. I’ve heard that these things are afraid of fire. Let me burn it! Pah!” Lu Yang spat out the Three Flavor True Fire, brushing it slightly against the leech. It immediately burned to death and loosened its grip, falling off from Meng Jingzhou’s arm.

The two had been keeping their spiritual consciousness open, but it was only to watch out for large demon beasts; they didn’t expect that they had to watch out for even the bugs in this place.

The leech was not strong enough to break through Meng Jingzhou’s defenses, but the latter had been pampered since childhood and was physiologically unaccustomed to such things.

After darting into nests of demon beasts seven times, being besieged by demon beasts five times, being forced into battles with demon beasts four times, and crawling out from a demon beast’s stomach one time, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou finally walked out of the jungle and saw a city built by humans.

The two were disheveled and hobbling, with demon beast saliva still clinging to their hair.

The characters “Demon Suppression Pass” above the city gate glistened, emitting an inexplicable sense of oppressive pressure that gave the two an inexplicable sense of reassurance.

“Big Senior Sister bless us, we’ve finally made it out!” The two clasped their hands in gratitude to the heavens and Yun Zhi for sparing their lives.

1. This type of punishment was where people were not only banished to the borders but also required to serve with hard labor. It’s penal servitude but at the borders and in harsh conditions. ☜

Chapter 238: The Difference Between the Barbarian Tribe and the Ancient Barbarian Tribe

This was the most rugged and exuberant city the two had ever seen. Built with large, refined steel stones, it was impregnable and exuded an air of austerity, standing like an upright figure at the boundary between the human and demon races to suppress any invading enemies.

The characters “Demon Suppression Pass” were also not mere decoration. They were a rare treasure capable of distinguishing between humans and shapeshifting demons. Anyone entering the city had to undergo its inspection to prove their innocence. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were no exception.

“My uncle is stationed at the Demon Confinement Pass. Looks like I won’t get to see him.” Meng Jingzhou shook his head regretfully.

“Quick, make way, make way! My brother is injured and needs a physician!”

Just as the two were about to enter the city, they heard shouting from behind. Two burly men were carrying a stretcher with the frail person on it wailing in pain.

Everyone instinctively stepped aside and formed a path for them. However, right before they ran in, the characters “Demon Suppression Pass” enveloped them. The three screamed in agony as white smoke fumed from their bodies, revealing their true forms.

Those two burly men turned out to be giant wolves, and the person on the stretcher was not a human cultivator but an uninjured old bei wolf[1].

The soldiers guarding the gate responded without any hesitation. Decisively raising their spears and halberds, they killed the three demon beasts. From time to time, demon beasts attempted to sneak into the Demon Suppression Pass, but only one outcome awaited them—death!

Upon entering the Demon Suppression Pass, the two saw some people peddling demon beast skins and inner cores on the streets, some selling healing pills and stating that their prices were twenty percent less than the stores, while others claimed that they could be bodyguards with their high cultivation.

Just like their city, these people were rugged and exuberant.

The two first found an inn and rested for the night. After recovering their energy, they could figure out their current situation.

Lu Yang pointed at the map, analyzing the intelligence they had gathered. “This is the Demon Suppression Pass, and it’s two hundred thousand li from the Demon Confinement Pass where your uncle is stationed. The jungle we were previously in is the boundary between the Great Xia Dynasty and the Demon Region. It is a neutral zone that doesn’t belong to any faction. Only after passing through the jungle and crossing a thick mist can one reach the true Demon Region.

“I happened to inquire with the newspaper vendor, and he said that this is a major hub for demon beast trades. The Luodi Merchant Guild’s flying vessels come here regularly; there’s one coming at noon tomorrow. So, do you want to go back?”

Meng Jingzhou was about to answer that it was obvious he wanted to go back, but before the words were about to leave his mouth, he changed his mind. “Go back? Why should we go back? This jungle made us suffer so much. If we don’t show the demon beasts a thing or two and word gets out, how will we show our faces in the future?”

Lu Yang grinned widely. “What a coincidence, that’s what I’m thinking too.”

The two immediately came to an agreement and decided to stick around for a while. They wouldn’t go back until they had some accomplishments to show. Returning in such a miserable state was not their style.

“It’s a pity that little fellow Man Gu didn’t come with us. His Ancient Barbarian bloodline has a natural suppressive effect on demon beasts,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy lamented and shook her head regretfully in the mental space.

Lu Yang suspected that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was well aware that Yun Zhi was standing behind the two of them earlier but had kept quiet just so that she could see him make a fool of himself.

A very logical suspicion.

However, he was intrigued by what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned. “There’s such a thing?”

When it came to this topic, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was exceptionally proud. She placed one hand on her hip, emanating the airs of a ruler commanding the world. “Of course! Did you think I only raised the ceiling of the Barbarian Tribe’s intelligence and shared my wisdom with them? No! I also bestowed them a small portion of my power!

“And who do you think I am? How many ancient demon beasts do you think I’ve eaten just for the sake of compiling the Comprehensive Culinary Compendium? The ancient demon beasts’ fear of me is etched into their bloodline. When Man Gu obtained an insignificant fraction of my power, he indirectly gained this ability that naturally counters demon beasts!

“Thanks to my gift, it’s not an exaggeration to say that the Ancient Barbarian Tribe could flaunt their might to the demon tribes. When they faced an opponent one major level lower, the oppressive pressure of their bloodline alone could instill fear in the other party. If they encountered opponents of the same level, taking on two at once was a breeze!”

Lu Yang was about to exalt the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for her mighty prowess when another question came to mind. “Can this kind of suppression be temporarily concealed? For example, when the Ancient Barbarian Tribe was hunting, they could hide in the shadows. Once a demon beast approached, however, even if it couldn’t see them, it would instinctively fear the Ancient Barbarian’s bloodline and run away in fright.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy paused to ponder for a while, then burst into loud peals of laughter. “...Hahaha, you really think of everything! With my protection, how could the Ancient Barbarians ever face problems with food shortage?”

“Immortal Fairy, please stop laughing first and answer my question.”

“Hahaha, the Ancient Barbarian Tribe has my protection!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Previously, Lu Yang had always wondered what the difference between the Ancient Barbarian Tribe and the current Barbarian Tribe was. Even Man Gu couldn’t answer, only mentioning that the Ancient Barbarian Tribe contained a mysterious power within them which granted them manifold abilities and provided tremendous aid. However, this power was so strong that it caused them to defy the heavenly laws of natural order. Thus, it gradually faded away with time.

As for what this mysterious power was, neither Man Gu nor the elders of his tribe could clarify. They simply said that it was a gift from the heavens.

Now that I think about it, could this mysterious power be a Tame Head Curse placed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

As for why Man Gu was the only one who remained of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, it was unclear whether it was due to natural selection and survival of the fittest or the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s power diluting with every generation of offspring.

“Actually, I was quite popular among the demons.”

Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously. Are you sure? Did the demons lose their minds?

“What, you don’t believe me? The Qiongqi Tribe said that the Taotie Tribe welcomed me, and the Taotie Tribe said that the Qiongqi Tribe welcomed me. I walked all around the demon tribes, and everywhere I went, I was met with cheers as they happily sent me off.

“That’s understandable. After all, when an immortal descends upon the demons, it’s like a blessing from the heavens. Now you know how great of a fortune it is to have me in your mental space, don’t you? Forget everything else, I can easily share ancient secrets with you. No one else can achieve what I do.”

“Immortal Fairy, do any of your ancient secrets actually come in handy?” Lu Yang felt that he was not destined to enjoy such fortune. It’s better to have someone with a tough fate profile to bear it.

Someone like Big Senior Sister would be a good choice.

In the real world, Lu Yang sighed deeply. “Poor Man Gu.”

Meng Jingzhou was befuddled. “What’s wrong with Man Gu?” We’re the ones who suffered in the dense forest. Why is Man Gu the pitiful one?

“It’s nothing. Let’s continue discussing our next steps.”

1. Bei is a folklore creature that is similar to wolves but with shorter hindlegs. It is thought to be companions with wolves, where the bei is the brain that knows where food is while the wolf is the brawn that can carry the bei to travel to the food. This is probably where the idiom “wolf and bei in cahoots” came from. ☜

Chapter 239: What Are You Pretending For?

“I’ll have two bottles of bug repellent; the most expensive kind.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou arrived at the Demon Suppression Pass Branch of the Luodi Merchant Guild to purchase the necessary supplies. The Demon Suppression Pass was one of the notably large cities at the frontier. Every day, an enormous quantity of goods related to demon beasts were sold and transported to various places across the Central Continent to satisfy the needs of cultivators at different realms; the flow of spirit stones was astonishing.

The bug repellent was a specialty from the borderlands. It was a special liquid concocted to counteract the relentless bugs in the jungle. When applied to the skin, it emitted a unique scent that only bugs could detect, keeping them away from cultivators.

With this, things like leeches crawling onto me won’t happen again.

Meng Jingzhou suddenly thought of something. “Do you have a lot of bug repellents in stock?”

The attendant was slightly stunned, not understanding what Meng Jingzhou’s intentions were. He politely asked, “How many bug repellents would you like, esteemed guest?”

“Enough to drive away all the bugs out of the jungle,” Meng Jingzhou replied.

No amount of proper training could have stopped the attendant’s mouth from twitching. “Apologies, esteemed guest, but the quantity of bug repellents you have asked for is far too large. Even if we empty the entire warehouse at our headquarters, we probably still wouldn’t be able to fulfill your request.” Everyone applies bug repellent to their skin, but you want to spray it all over the jungle? No amount of bug repellent would be enough.

Meng Jingzhou pouted, slightly displeased with the merchant guild’s advertised slogan. “And you still claim that you can fulfill any requests as long as the customer has the money? Forget it, I can’t do anything if you don’t have it.”

The environment in the jungle was so harsh that even the mosquitoes were at the Qi Training Stage. If cultivators at the Qi Training Stage entered the jungle, there would be almost no chance of survival. However, from another perspective, if a Qi Training cultivator managed to survive in the jungle, they would undoubtedly achieve great things in the future.

In fact, many famous cultivators in history chose to train in the jungle when they were at the Qi Training Stage to hone their skills, laying a solid foundation for long-term health maintenance to alleviate the body’s excessive internal dampness[1] in the future.

“I’ll have two more bottles of Dampness Removal Pills; the most effective kind.

“And also Detoxification Pills.

“I heard that some demon beasts carry spring philtre poison;[2] I’ll have two antidotes for spring philtre poison... No, I’m not here to ask for the brothel’s address. I meant the pills for curing the spring philtre poison.

Lu Yang remarked, “Poison...the quality of your poison products is subpar. Luckily, I’m well-prepared. I’ve written down the quantity and weight of the herbs on this piece of paper. Just follow this and we’ll mix it ourselves.” He was worried about the Luodi Merchant Guild. The quality is too poor. Even any random disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect can concoct something better than this.

“Would you two like the latest version of the Illustrated Jungle Handbook? It provides information on most of the demon beasts in the jungle, along with potential dangers you may encounter.”

“Good stuff. I’ll take a copy.”

“How about tents? You may need them when camping outdoors. They are hot sellers at this branch. If you buy a tent, we will also gift you the urine of a Golden Core demon beast. Sprinkling it around your sleeping area can effectively ward off lower-level demon beasts.”

“It may also attract higher-level demon beasts instead. That’s not safe; we’ll pass.”

Just then, a talisman caught Lu Yang’s eye. “Targeted Teleportation Talisman? What is it used for?” He clicked his tongue at its high price. Compared to this, the Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill is so much cheaper.

“Excellent eye, esteemed guest. This is an amazing life-saving item. If you encounter a life-or-death crisis in the jungle, you just have to activate this talisman, and it will teleport you back to the Demon Suppression Pass. Even a Nascent Soul demon cannot interrupt the teleportation process!”

“Sounds good! Give me five pieces!” Meng Jingzhou splurged as usual. Whenever he took a liking to something, he would buy it without checking the price.

The attendant was grinning from ear to ear and became much more ardent. Just the commission from selling five Targeted Teleportation Talisman is enough to cover my salary for a month! These two are indeed wealthy patrons. Looks like I’ll be earning quite a bit of commission today.

I wonder where these two young masters come from. They’re probably from some big clan or disciples of a big sect here for training. It’s likely their first time visiting.

The attendant kindly reminded, “Esteemed guests, life here at the border is different from what you may be used to. It’s important to keep your wealth discreet. Not only are the demon beasts here dangerous, but humans are too. People go missing in the jungle every day, and recently, there have been even more disappearances. Though they say that it’s the work of demon beasts, many know that the demon beasts might not be fully responsible.”

He presumed that the two of them would be training here for a while, which meant they would inevitably be in frequent contact, so he naturally tried his best to win them over. “Although His Excellency Town Governor has set ‘Rules’ in the city, stating that ‘No one may steal, rob, or plunder,’ these rules only apply within the Demon Suppression Pass. once you leave and enter the jungle, these rules no longer matter.”

This was the perk of having a cultivator at the Fusion Stage. They could establish rules everyone must follow in the city of their jurisdiction, ensuring order to the largest degree. If Fusion cultivators weren’t so rare, the Great Xia Dynasty would have wanted one in every city.

“Esteemed guests, please proceed to our VIP room.” The attendant bowed slightly and gestured for them to follow, but Lu Yang declined.

“There’s no need for that. My brother and I are at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage after all, and the world is peaceful. Who would dare rob us?”

The attendant saw that it was pointless to continue persuading them, so he simply continued to assist them.

“What kinds of healing pills do you have?”

“Golden Wound Pills[3], which heals one’s injuries rapidly.

“Hemostatic Pills, which are effective for heavy bleeding.

“Qi Restoration Pills, which can speed up the recovery of spirit energy.

“White Bone Pills from the Buddhist Kingdom’s Merit Creation Series, which can bring the dead back to life and revive their flesh—”

“Give me two bottles of each,” Meng Jingzhou interrupted. “Do you also have protective-type magical treasures? Give us two of each as well.”

After they finished shopping, they checked their items and confirmed that nothing was missing. “Let’s settle the bill.”

“Esteemed guests, you are VIPs of our merchant child, so all your future purchases will receive a 10% discount.”

Meng Jingzhou didn’t say anything, casually whisking out a black token with the character “Meng” engraved on it.

The moment the attendant saw the token, his pupils contracted and his hands trembled. The first lesson in his training was to recognize the special tokens issued by the merchant guild. These tokens represented various venerable identities, such as the Imperial Family or the Meng Family. The staff had to treat these people with utmost respect and never offend them.

He had worked here for more than ten years and had seen members of the Meng Family before, but they were from the collateral branches. The token before him now was only inscribed with one “Meng” character, indicating that the owner was from the main branch and was qualified to inherit some of the Meng Family’s power in the future.

A huge background. An absolutely huge background.

It’s laughable that I even mentioned a 10% discount. They probably wouldn’t even care about such a trivial thing.

“Keep this to yourself,” Meng Jingzhou calmly said, but inside, his heart was blooming with joy.

Yes yes yes, this is exactly the expression I want.

Lu Yang cast a sidelong glance at Meng Jingzhou with disdain.

What are you pretending for? The Dao-Seeking Sect also has such tokens, but only Big Senior Sister and the elders have the right to use them.

The attendant took the token, verified its authenticity, and quickly processed the payment, handing over a small pile of complimentary gifts. “Do you two have storage rings? I can directly place everything in them for you.”

Lu Yang calmly took out his Dao-Seeking Sect’s identity jade token which had the characters “Lu Yang” engraved.

Upon seeing the jade tablet, the attendant felt his heart tighten again.

A disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect—this is an identity that can command the winds and rain in the cultivation world. I had guessed that these two come from big ancestral clans or sects, but I didn’t expect it to be this big.

“Keep it to yourself,” Lu Yang calmly said, but inside, his heart was blooming with joy.

It’s finally my turn now.

Meng Jingzhou cast a sidelong glance at Lu Yang. What are you pretending for?

The two grabbed their items and headed for the jungle.

Unbeknownst to them, as soon as they left the merchant guild, five figures with ruthless gazes tailed them stealthily, evidently up to no good.

1. “Dampness” is a concept in Traditional Chinese Medicine. It’s also one of the pathogenic energies in TCM. Though it's linked to many illnesses and ailments, a common example we see in Chinese dramas and novels is aching joints. There are informative articles out there, but I found a short one if you’d like to give it a read. ☜

2. Spring is associated with amorous matters in Chinese. ☜

3. This is adapted from “Golden Wound Medicine” or “Jin Chuang Yao,” the very typical ointment or powder used for open wounds. It's no longer around nowadays, or at least, not in circulation. ☜

Chapter 240: You’ve Got Quite the Guts to Rob the Creed Founder

“Did you see how they were shopping in the merchant guild earlier? They didn’t even ask the price and bought everything outright.”

Five figures cloaked in black moved swiftly through the forest, their raspy voices masking their gender and age. Traversing the jungle nimbly, they avoided detection by Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Fair skin, clean look, and their clothes don’t look like they’re from around here. Probably some disciples from a sect or noble family out here to see the world.”

Another person sneered like a venomous snake hiding in the shadows. “See the world? Then we shall let them see how cruel the world is.”

“Did you hear that effeminate man earlier? He said they’re at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage. Given their background, their combat power should be similar to the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.”

“So what if they rival Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators? All five of us are at this stage, and we’re also veterans. How can these two kids be our match?”

“It’s still best to stay cautious.”

“Remember those few sect disciples we ran into the last time? One big job, and we rested for three months. If we pull this off today, we’ll be set for another three months!”

“Not just that. I bet they’re carrying way more spirit stones than we expect—easy fat lambs for slaughter.”

“This place should do. Not many people come here.”

“Action!”

At the leader’s command, the five figures spread out, deftly moving to encircle the two people. They positioned themselves in predetermined spots, ensuring there was no way for the duo to escape. From how practiced their movements were, it was clear they had done this countless times before.

“Stop right there!” the leader yelled harshly, his voice laced with a soundwave spell to intimidate the mind.

“Who are you?!” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were visibly startled. Although they adopted defensive stances with much vigilance, they couldn’t conceal the fear in their eyes.

“Figures, you’re new here. You don’t even know us, the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes, yet you dare wander the jungle?” The leader pulled back his hood, revealing an angular face, a hooked nose, and a frigid gaze.

As he spoke, the five people unleashed the aura waves of Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators, warning the two not to engage in futile resistance.

“No idea which clan or sect trained you two, but you can’t even tell what we’re here for. So naive,” another person remarked in a terrifying and sinister voice. As he removed his hood, he revealed a face with one eye blinded.

“In the middle of the jungle, with the five of us surrounding you, what else do you two think this could possibly be? We saw you buying a lot of things in the merchant guild earlier. Pretty wealthy, eh?

“Tell us, how many spirit stones do you have? If the price is satisfactory, we can discuss this nicely. But if you don’t have enough spirit stones, don’t blame the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes for not being nice!” His voice grew extremely icy, laced with ruthlessness.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a smile with each other and shrugged helplessly. Who would have thought that our first enemies in the jungle aren’t demon beasts but humans?

“Take action! Show them what we’re capable of!” As the leader commanded, the five acted in unison. With their impeccable coordination, they had never met their match at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Closing in on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, they were ready to seize them the next moment.

To their surprise, the duo acted simultaneously at terrifying speed.

“Draw Ground As Prison!”

“Draw Underground Prison!”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou deftly traced circles and cast similar spells. Invisible barriers materialized around the five people, blocking their escape routes and dragging them into an underground prison.

“What kind of method is this?!”

“The legendary ‘Draw Ground As Prison?’”

“No, we’re inside a dungeon! This is a spatial spell!”

“It’s the Dao of Painting; it must be!”

The five of them babbled in panic. Trapped within an underground prison and invisible barriers, they were completely bewildered by the sudden turn of events.

“You dared to rob me, a branch leader? Tired of living, huh?” Meng Jingzhou sneered.

“You dared to rob me, the creed founder? You’ve got quite the guts!” Lu Yang sneered.

Meng Jingzhou turned his head in shock. “I’m still a branch leader. Since when did you promote yourself?” Due to incompetent management and wrong recruits, the Everlasting Creed has already collapsed. How did you still get promoted?

“What do you mean by I promoted myself? This was specially conferred by an immortal,” Lu Yang replied, full of self-assurance.

Recalling that there was still an immortal residing within Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou figured things out. He was really envious of Lu Yang. Having an immortal’s soul inside you means that you can consult the immortal anytime and receive their guidance. What a great fortuitous opportunity this is.

“Speak up. How many times have you robbed people? Have you killed anyone?”

“Why waste time asking? They definitely have. Look at this face; does it look like he hasn’t killed anyone before? Let’s just send them to the authorities. Whether they’re killed or imprisoned, let the officials handle it.”

“Wait wait wait! Two young heroes, there’s some misunderstanding!” The boss with the aquiline nose hurriedly protested, “I can’t choose how I look! Anyway, we’re not robbers!”

Meng Jingzhou clearly did not buy his nonsense. “Misunderstanding my ass. You tailed us the moment we left the merchant guild, deliberately hid from our spiritual consciousness when we were in the jungle, followed us all the way to this place, and then encircled us! And you say that this isn’t a robbery?”

Lu Yang added, “You also talked about letting us see how cruel the world is, mentioning the last time you encountered some sect disciples and rested three months after one big job.”

The five were floored. They hadn’t expected their movements to be exposed from the very beginning. But didn’t we make sure we stayed outside the range of their spiritual consciousness?

Where on earth did these two disciples come from? Why are they so perceptive?

What they didn’t know was that Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness could already rival that of a Golden Core cultivator. Thus, he could hear their conversations loud and clear.

“We really aren’t robbers! We are bodyguards! Bodyguards!”

“What thing?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou still hadn’t fully registered what they said.

“We saw that you two didn’t even ask about the prices at the merchant guild. We figured you must be disciples of a noble family out here for training, which was why you didn’t fret over spirit stones. Worried that you might not be familiar with the area and end up in trouble, we specifically came to be your bodyguards!”

“Then what did you mean by letting us see how cruel the world is?”

The hook-nosed boss stammered, “It’s because we saw that you were rich, so we wanted to raise the price a little. If we make big bucks this time, we can rest for a few months after the job’s done.”

“Then why did you ask us how many spirit stones we have?”

“To better set a price.”

“What about not blaming the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes for not being nice if we don’t have enough spirit stones?”

“Keep going ahead, and you will enter the territory of a Half-Step Golden Core demon beast. If you didn’t have enough spirit stones, we wouldn’t warn you and let you continue walking straight into danger.”

“What about ordering them to take action just now?”

“We saw you shrugging and assumed that you’d refuse us as bodyguards. We were planning to lure that Half-Step Golden Beast out and fight it to showcase our strength to you.”

Another person mumbled, “But looking at you two, you probably won’t need us as bodyguards.”

“Then why must you talk to us about being bodyguards in the jungle?”

“We don’t have to pay taxes.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So all of you are treating the jungle as a tax-free zone, huh?

Chapter 241: Arhat Fruit Fist

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had heard that the Demon Suppression Pass was notorious for plundering, with many people getting robbed in the jungle after purchasing items at the merchant guild. The two had originally planned to misreport their cultivation to lure the bandits into taking their bait.

In the end, instead of robbers, they attracted a group of bodyguards who wanted to recommend themselves for the job.

“We have the highest ratings and best reviews among the bodyguards at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Not only are our prices reasonable, but we are also meticulous in our service. With long-term partnerships built with multiple Half-Step Golden Core demon beasts, we have largely resolved the problems of intelligence transmission and safety in the jungle.

“Young heroes, if your families or sects have tasked you with a training mission, we can even customize three plans for you to choose from, at no additional cost.” The hook-nosed boss was still fervently promoting their bodyguard services.

“How many spirit stones would it cost to hire all of you?” Meng Jingzhou was interested. We need all the information we can on the jungle, and these local fixers have plenty of intelligence.

We don’t need bodyguards, but they can serve as guides.

From how they carried themselves, the hook-nosed boss could deduce that they were not from ordinary backgrounds. He held up five fingers.

“Five hundred thousand spirit stones? That’s not expensive.”

The hook-nosed boss jumped in astonishment. What I had meant to say was fifty thousand spirit stones, and if they found the price high, I could still lower it. I didn’t expect this generous young master to raise the price tenfold without even blinking.

Meng Jingzhou took out two hundred thousand spirit stones, piling them into a small mound. “Here’s two hundred thousand to start; the rest will be paid after the job is done. If I’m satisfied with your service, I’ll throw in more.”

“Please rest assured. Our service is definitely worth more than what you pay!” The five of them had their eyes sparkling at the sight of the pile of spirit stones.

They had never encountered such a wealthy client before.

“Strange, do you feel like it’s getting hotter here?” Meng Jingzhou shook his shirt.

“I feel it too.” Lu Yang was also puzzled.

The hook-nosed boss faintly voiced his thoughts. “Could it be that the seven of us have absorbed most of the air in this underground prison?”

The dungeon was underground and airtight. While the seven of them spoke, the oxygen was nearly depleted. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou released the spell’s binding, and the seven of them returned to the surface.

“Old Turtle, come out! The terms have been settled,” the hawk-nosed boss called out.

An old turtle, the size of a millstone, slowly crawled over from nearby, emanating a power unlike that of ordinary Foundation Establishment cultivators. Lu Yang reckoned that this was the Half-Step Golden Core cultivator the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes mentioned they planned to spar with.

Quite the complete cast of actors you have; even demon beasts are included.

“This is Old Turtle. Up ahead is a small lake, and Old Turtle controls one-fifth of the territory,” the hook-nosed boss introduced.

Old Turtle shook his head. “Little Eagle, I’ve told you before that your pitch sounds like a robbery and can easily lead to misunderstandings. I saw everything from afar. These two young heroes are geniuses who could execute Draw Ground As Prison. Why would they need you as bodyguards?”

“That was really Draw Ground As Prison?” The five were flabbergasted. It was only speculation they dared not assert, so they assumed it could have been a life-saving method their sect had provided them. After all, Draw Ground As Prison was a spell that only existed in the legends. It was infamously challenging to cultivate and nearly impossible for Foundation Establishment cultivators to master it.

“Old Turtle, you have sharp eyes. What I performed was indeed Draw Ground As Prison,” Lu Yang quickly admitted, eliciting an eye roll from Meng Jingzhou.

“Young Heroes, what is the purpose of your visit to the jungle...”

“Challenge demon beasts. We’ve long heard that this place is rife with demon beasts, many of which are remnants of ancient species with tremendous power. We wish to spar with these demon beasts and hone our skills.”

The hook-nosed boss nodded. This is a common reason.

“May I know what level of demon beasts you would like to challenge? Those who just entered the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage or seasoned veterans of the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

“Golden Core Stage.”

“Golden Core Stage?!” five people and one demon beast exclaimed.

“Please don’t set your sights too high. The gap between the Foundation Establishment and Golden Core stages is like a vast chasm that cannot be crossed easily. Moreover, those who have lived in the jungle for a long time, whether human or demon beast, are all very vicious. You can’t treat them as ordinary opponents!” Old Turtle warned, despite knowing that the two were big clients who could reward them with bountiful spirit stones if the job was done well.

“Putting aside Golden Core cultivators for now, the two of you might not even be able to defeat me!” Old Turtle said with composure. Having been at the Half-Step Golden Core Stage for a long time, he possessed a wealth of experience and extraordinary defense. Even if the tiger demon that refined the tiger-henchman ghosts could be revived, it wouldn’t be able to break Old Turtle’s defenses.

“Then let’s try.” Meng Jingzhou smiled and stretched his muscles. If I don’t demonstrate my potential, the Golden Core demon beasts they select for me won’t be too strong, and I won’t achieve my desired training goals.

Everyone arrived at the small lake, with Old Turtle and Meng Jingzhou standing on opposite sides.

“Start!” Lu Yang announced.

Old Turtle took two deep breaths and circulated the inherent cultivation technique in his bloodline. An indistinct golden mark appeared on his shell, signifying that he was the descendant of the Sky Pathway Turtle—the ancient demon beast renowned for its defense. Old Turtle was fortunate to have inherited this trait from his ancestor.

“If you can’t even break my defenses, don’t even mention...”

“Arhat Fist!” Meng Jingzhou took a large stride forward. His legs were bent like a bow, while his body resembled an arrow. Making himself taut, he suddenly exerted a burst of strength, striking the turtle shell.

The golden mark shattered, and Old Turtle was sent flying far away. Old Turtle bounced on the lake’s surface like a stone skipping across the water before finally landing with a splash.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes couldn’t close their agape mouths for a long while. Old Turtle is famous for his defense. Even all five of us together can’t break its defense, yet Meng Jingzhou knocked it over with a single punch?

This small lake was home to four other Half-Step Golden Core demon beasts who shared dominion over the area with Old Turtle. When they saw Old Turtle being catapulted across the air, the color drained from their faces.

“Arhat Fist? I’ve not seen you use it before. You just learned it?” Lu Yang was curious.

“Shifu said that part of the inspiration for his Heaven-Shaking Six Forms was derived from Arhat Fist, so he wanted me to learn it too. It also aids me in cultivating the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms.”

Lu Yang teased, “I heard that when Arhat Fist is mastered at its highest level, one can achieve the Arhat Fruit Realm. Maybe you can succeed.”

“Enough with that. Attaining the Arhat Fruit Realm? You might as well tell me to leave home to become a monk.”

“You’re not much different from a monk as it is.”

“Get lost! I’m planning to violate the precept of abstinence after becoming an immortal and liberate myself.” Breaking the pure yang state would drastically slow down his cultivation speed, but since becoming an immortal was the pinnacle of cultivation, his cultivation speed wouldn’t really matter then.

“Arhat Fist...” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured after being silent for quite a while. The keywords seemed to have stirred some memories.

“Immortal Fairy, you know Arhat Fist too?” Lu Yang was interested in learning a new fist technique; the only one he knew was the Animal Form Fist.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed. “What’s Arhat Fist? I’ve never even heard of it. I know an even higher-level fist technique. You can head straight for the Arhat Fruit Realm once you master it. Want to learn?”

”What fist technique is that?”

“Arhat Fruit Fist.”[1]

Lu Yang asked, “...Does its effects include clearing heat, moistening the lungs, easing the throat, and enhancing one’s voice?”[2]

“How did you know that?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was extremely surprised. Could Lu Yang have practiced it before?

1. Although I translated the realm as “Arhat Fruit Realm,” it’s actually made up of “arhat” and “Buddhist realm.” The term for the “Buddhist realm” here includes the character for “fruit.” Combining “arhat” with “fruit,” it can form “arhat fruit.” It’s more complicated than this, but you can roughly understand “arhat” as a type of monk. ☜

2. As explained in an earlier chapter, arhat fruit or Luo Han Guo is a very common ingredient in TCM-related food and drinks. It has many therapeutic properties, though its most renowned one is its throat-soothing effect. ☜

Chapter 242: Lu Yang, I Want to Go Out and Play

Arhat Fist was one of the supreme fist techniques of the Golden Buddhist Kingdom. When cultivated to its pinnacle, one could attain the Arhat Fruit Realm. However, this purely existed in theory; Lu Yang had never heard of anyone mastering such a technique.

Arhat Fruit Fist was a fist technique invented by an immortal. Judging by the name, it seemed related to the Arhat Fruit Realm, differing by just one word, and its effects included clearing heat, moistening the lungs, easing the throat, and enhancing one’s voice.

Judging by the origins, the Arhat Fruit Fist was definitely the superior one.

But the problem is that this was invented by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“There’s no need to practice this. Just from the name, I can already guess what this fist technique is for.”

“Hey hey hey, what kind of look is that? I am the creator of the Arhat Fruit Fist, so it’s a legitimate immortal-tier fist technique. That Arhat Fist isn’t even worthy to be compared to my fist technique!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stomped her foot, feeling that Lu Yang was underestimating her.

“It’s not that I’m underestimating you, but the name of your fist technique...I don’t really have words for it... It doesn’t sound formidable at all.”

“What do you know? Are you learning fist techniques just for showing off and fighting with others? No, the most important thing about fist techniques is Yangsheng—health maintenance.” [1]

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy educated Lu Yang to correct his misconceptions. “Isn’t the purpose of cultivation to live better? And what’s most important for a better life? It’s the body.

“To achieve that end, I specifically invented health maintenance fist techniques, including Arhat Fruit Fist, which clears heat and benefits the lungs and throat, as well as Fennel Seed Fist, which dispels cold, relieves pain, rectifies qi, and harmonizes the stomach. There are more than a thousand types in total.

“If you nourish your body properly, what will hinder you from becoming an arhat? If you can master these thousand sets of fist techniques and integrate them, you will be able to learn my supreme fist technique—Immortal Fairy Fist Technique!”

Immortal Fairy Fist Technique was what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had used to beat up the Everlasting Immortal. Its power was astounding, pummeling the Everlasting Immortal until he scurried away while clutching his head.

“So, what do you think? Wanna learn?” It’s about time to showcase some of my skills to Lu Yang, lest he keep wondering whether my becoming an immortal was a fluke.

I’m the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals. How could it have been a fluke?

“Not interested at all,” Lu Yang flatly declined.

In the real world, Old Turtle had just crawled out of the lake, still dizzy from the blow. One punch already contained so much power. If they had gone all out, I’m afraid few Golden Core cultivators would be able to defeat them. The other person has yet to make a move, but their combat prowess should not be inferior to that of Junior Meng.

Which faction produced these geniuses?

Old Turtle no longer held them back, agreeing to assist them with finding opponents. He broke off a tree branch and began drawing on the soft soil, starting with an irregular oval. “This is our current position, by the small lake. Ten li south of here is a black panther with a white spot on its forehead. It’s extremely ferocious and carries an ancient bloodline. Although it is at the Basic Golden Core Stage, even Intermediate Golden Core cultivators would suffer when fighting with it.

“Further south of the black panther is a pack of Moon Shadow Wolves. Most of them are at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, while the wolf king is at the Apex Basic Golden Core Stage. They never act alone. If you encounter one Moon Shadow Wolf, it indicates that a whole pack is hiding nearby. You have to be very cautious.

“Toward the east is...

“Toward the west is...”

True to its status as one of the five hegemons ruling the lake, Old Turtle held considerable intelligence. “Little Eagle and the others know the exact locations; they can take you there.” He still needed to guard the small lake, worried that if he was gone for half a month, his territory would be cleanly divided up by the other four Half-Step Golden Core overlords. It’s not easy to have a small lake as my territory in the jungle.

“These demon beasts with fixed territories are still manageable since you know what to expect. What you really need to watch out for are the nomadic ones. They are extremely cunning and can even transform into human form. They love ambushing and hunting you humans. I’ve seen no fewer than fifty people die under the fangs of such demon beasts.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou thanked the Old Turtle and set off with the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes toward the black panther’s territory.

“Lu Yang, Lu Yang, can we discuss something?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s tone contained a rare trace of cajolery.

“What is it?”

“How many days do you plan on staying in the jungle?”

“At least five days,” Lu Yang calculated. I have to fight various demon beasts and battle during the night; the training results won’t show if it’s too short a time.

He and Meng Jingzhou planned to battle nonstop in the jungle to improve their combat experience and consolidate their cultivation. If they could find an opportunity to form their Golden Core, that would be even better.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy counted with her fingers. “Look, I stay in the mental space all day long. Apart from eating and sleeping, all I do is watch you fight. It’s quite boring. It’s said that the meaning of life lies in moving about. Don’t you think I should go out and explore a bit?”

“So, Immortal Fairy, what you want is...”

“Let me use a Bodhi tree clone,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy requested with a fawning smile. “Of course, if you really don’t want to give me one, there’s nothing I can do. But it would be amazing if you could!”

Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s hesitant yet expectant visage, Lu Yang couldn’t help but chuckle.

“What are you laughing at?!”

“Nothing, nothing.” Lu Yang tried his best to put on a solemn expression. “I can give you a Bodhi tree clone, but you have to behave in the jungle and not cause any big trouble. Also, you must come back before Meng Jingzhou and I return to the city.”

“No problem at all!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy vowed. “My immortal consciousness has a massive range; I can find you anytime.”

“That’s good then.”

In the real world, Lu Yang had suddenly stopped walking.

“What’s the matter?” Meng Jingzhou and the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were bewildered, thinking Lu Yang had sensed some kind of danger.

“Nothing much. I just want to send a clone to explore other parts of the jungle.”

“Clone?” The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes exchanged glances in confusion. Only Meng Jingzhou understood what was going on.

Pinching a Bodhi tree seed, Lu Yang shrank into the earth and cast the Tree-Planting Mantra. A Bodhi tree sprouted from the ground, bearing two Lu Yangs. After both Lu Yangs broke free from the Bodhi tree, the original remained in place, while the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took over the clone and took to her heels, just like the description of the legendary Ginseng Fruit—vanishing the instant it hit the ground.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were dumbfounded, their eyes nearly popping out of their sockets and their mouths agape for a long while.

“C-clone?!” Never mind Foundation Establishment cultivators; even we Golden Core cultivators have never heard of anyone capable of this technique.

“It's just an unpresentable minor spell not worth mentioning.” Lu Yang deliberately displayed a modest expression, earning the admiration of the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes.

“Young Hero Lu, can you control this clone of yours?”

Lu Yang waved his hand. “No need for that. The clone can act on its own.”

“Then your clone better be careful. I heard that some cultivators like to ambush lone cultivators. Quite a few have gone missing.”

“That...that shouldn’t happen, right?” At the thought of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s simple-minded countenance, Lu Yang suddenly felt uneasy.

1. Yangsheng, “health nourishment,” “self-healing,” “life cultivation” or “health preservation” is a very important concept in Traditional Chinese Medicine. TCM believes that “prevention is better than cure,” and it is about regulating and nourishing the body well in all aspects of life to prevent physical and mental ailments. ☜

Chapter 243: Chronicles of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Fortuitous Encounters

“Pick, pick, picking mushrooms, picked a little mushroom...” The song of yore echoed through the jungle. Its voice was dulcet and bright, making it evident that the singer was a lively and cheerful young girl.

However, if someone were to see the singer’s appearance, they would be in for a huge shock.

The singer was a bald man with a dignified visage, who wore clothes made of leaves to cover himself. It was hard to imagine that someone like him could be singing a nursery rhyme.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy squatted by the lake, her eyes shifting as she gazed at her current appearance. “Though Lu Yang isn’t bad-looking, he is still a man. Since he isn’t around, why don’t I just change into my original appearance?”

She acted on her idea right away. It’s rare for me to be out and having fun without anyone around to control me, so of course, I should do whatever I please. Bringing two fingers together and pressing them to her lips, she softly chanted a few words, causing the heaven and earth to resonate as the surrounding space blurred and distorted.

When the space returned to normal, the figure squatting by the lake was no longer the bald Lu Yang but a young girl who looked about sixteen or seventeen years old. The young girl was innocent and unaffected, with large eyes that sparkled and long hair that cascaded down to her waist. She wore a millet-yellow dress and was barefoot, resembling a young miss from some wealthy family who had sneaked out without getting to dress properly.

“Hehe, I’m so cute.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy beamed widely at the reflection of her original appearance in the lake.

Sitting by the lake barefoot, she kicked the water every now and then, sending ripples across the surface and attracting the little fishes that thought food was here. Upon swimming closer, they were disappointed that it was just a human playing with the water.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could conjure anything in Lu Yang’s mental space, they were ultimately mental constructs that lacked the oomph when she played with them. It’s completely different now. Even kicking the water is very fun. As she soaked her dainty feet in the cold and refreshing water, it was so comfortable that she grinned from ear to ear.

She picked up a slightly longer twig from the bank of the lake and used her immortal energy as a fishing line to wrap it around the stick and make it into a simple fishing rod. “Heave-ho.” Without bothering with a bait, she cast the line, her devil-may-care spirit on full display.

The immortal energy that had condensed into the fishing line was just a thin strand, but it was still immortal energy, a power unique to immortals. No bait was needed; the fishing line itself was the best bait.

Squinting her eyes, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy half-lay by the lake. Despite the muddy shore, she seemed to have used some spell to keep herself spotless. If Lu Yang were here, he would have recognized it as the Garment-Cleansing Incantation he had always yearned for. However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s version was much more exquisite than Lan Ting’s, attaining the realm of immortal arts. Casting it hardly required any energy.

Soon, a large fish took the bait, clamping down firmly on the line. The large fish wanted to refine this bit of immortal energy, but the difference in their levels was too great for it to succeed.

“Got a bite?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sprang to her feet, her eyes flickering with excitement. She lifted her right hand forcefully, and a chubby fish leaped out of the water.

“Aiya, it’s a chubby-headed fish. It’s ugly, not tasty, and has no nutritional value.” She shook her head in disappointment as she tapped the fish’s face, signaling it to let go before tossing it back into the lake.

“Be reincarnated as a tastier animal in your next life,” she reminded the fish. I spared its life; a fish should be grateful and repay kindness. [1]

But the chubby-headed fish had yet to gain spirit sentience, so how could it understand what she said?

After it swam away, various lake creatures—fishes, shrimps, crabs, shellfish, and living beings that only emerged after the ancient era—bit the hook; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy knew none of them.

It doesn’t matter even if I don’t recognize them. I have plenty of life experience and cooking experience. I just need one taste to determine what is edible and what isn’t.

In no time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was already surrounded by piles of “lakefood.”[2] Worried they might escape, she even mixed the lake water and black soil together into mud, then used it to form a small circle and trap all the lakefood inside.

Suddenly, a shadow shot out from the surface of the lake. It was covered in sharp spikes like a porcupine, though its spikes were much shorter. This lake was several times larger than the one Old Turtle controlled, so the owner was naturally much stronger; it was at the Advanced Golden Core Stage. Many humans and demons had been swallowed by it while drinking from the lake.

When it saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it was seized by an insatiable craving. Although she appears to be a little lass at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, for some reason, I feel like if I eat her, I will be able to shatter my Golden Core instantly and form my nascent soul. With that, I can expand my territory further and grow even stronger.

Since Lu Yang was at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, and his Bodhi tree clone could inherit eighty percent of his power, it implied that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could only be at the same cultivation stage as him now. Right as she blinked, she was swallowed by the lake’s owner.

The lake master was not worried about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy attacking it from within. Having consumed a powerful corrosive liquid, if the person it swallowed tried to strike back, their attacks would be nullified.

“Water-Repelling... forget it, Fennel Seed Fist.” As a soft punch hit the stomach wall, the lake master felt as if a tempest was raging within. Perhaps it was even more intense than that, as though a gargantuan force was stirring its insides.

“Wait, let me...” Before the lake master could finish imploring, the power from the Fennel Seed Fist ripped it into several pieces.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grabbed a piece of the lake master’s flesh and swam back to the surface.

Initially, she had planned to use the Water-Repelling Mantra to deal with the lake master, but another idea came to mind. The lake master is a creature I’ve never seen before. I wonder what it tastes like. If I had used the Water-Repelling Mantra and desiccated it, how could I still eat it?

Thus, on a whim, she had decided to use the Fennel Seed Fist instead.

The Fennel Seed Fist could rectify qi and harmonize the stomach. When a punch landed on someone, it could nourish their body. However, if the other party was healthy, this punch would accelerate one’s death instead.

“Why doesn’t Lu Yang want to learn such a formidable fist technique?

“Ugh, so wet, it’s really uncomfortable. Water-Repelling Mantra.” As the words “Water-Repelling Mantra” left her mouth, the water around her instantly parted, and an invisible force lifted her.

She stepped onto the surface of the lake with her hands behind her back. Holding a piece of the lake master’s meat and humming a little tune, she made her way back to the shore, relaxed and content.

“I wonder what the lake master tastes like.” My immortal chef’s intuition tells me that it should taste pretty good.

“No pot, huh.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head. There’s not a single decent cooking utensil nearby.

Upon noticing the lotus leaves on the lake’s surface, her eyes lit up. “I got it! I can wrap it with lotus leaves and coat it with mud outside. Once I roast it over fire, I’ll be able to eat it!”

Since she didn’t bring any seasonings with her, she decided to improvise with what was available, using plants that resembled spices by the lake.

“Everlasting True Fire.” She spat out a true fire that was unknown to the world and beyond the 108 True Fires.

The Everlasting True Fire was gentle, gradually heating the food from the inside out, and soon a refreshing aroma began to waft through the air.

Just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was about to dig in, a soft voice sounded behind her. “Little sister, why are you here alone? This place is very dangerous.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned around, her face full of innocence and ignorance. There were even a few mud stains on her cheek, remnants from making Beggar’s Fish.[3]

Four people stood behind her, all at the Golden Core Stage. She didn’t know whether it was an illusion, but she could have sworn their smiles carried a fleeting malice which vanished almost instantly, replaced by geniality.

“Little sister, where are your family members?”

1. This phrase is usually used for humans, but it’s swapped to “fish” here. ☜

2. In case I didn’t manage to translate the wordplay, it’s supposed to be a modification of “seafood.” ☜

3. This is adapted from the dish Beggar’s Chicken. ☜

Chapter 244: This Meal Is Poisonous

“Who are you?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy eyed the four visitors warily. All of them were at the Golden Core Stage, a cultivation realm higher than hers.

Lü Chang's smile grew even wider.

The four of them often roamed the jungle, appearing like ordinary cultivators on the surface, fighting demon beasts and gathering natural treasures. In reality, their original forms were demon beasts, secretly killing and looting people’s possessions, including their storage rings, and trading with humans involved in shady dealings to obtain substantial earnings.

Originally, they had come to discuss their next plan with the lake master, but they hadn’t expected to encounter a young girl here. Foundation Establishment Stage, obedient and adorable, clothes disheveled, and barefoot. She’s probably the young miss of some noble family who has come here to train but got separated from her bodyguards.

This was common. After all, the Golden Core Stage couldn’t be the highest cultivation realm in the jungle. As far as they knew, there was a large elephant demon nearby that was at the Nascent Soul Stage and possessed terrifying strength.

Lü Chang was not as knowledgeable and couldn’t recognize what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was wearing, but one thing was certain—it was of high quality.

A young miss from an aristocratic family will undoubtedly have many valuable items when out for training. I don’t have to be afraid even if her family comes after her. This is the jungle, where life and death are up to the heavens. Who can guarantee that there will be no accidents during their training in the outside world?

If worse comes to worst, I’ll just shift the blame to the humans themselves. After all, they have done things like this many times. Besides, this little lass is even cooking here. It’s obvious that she’s simple-minded—an easy target to deceive.

Lü Chang considered sundry possible scenarios and ascertained that there was no danger before he stepped forward to approach the Everlasting Immortal Fairy amiably. “We are cultivators who have come to gather herbs by the lake. We didn’t expect to find a young girl like you here. This place is very dangerous. Golden Core demon beasts lurk around here; even we don’t dare to stay here for long.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled the lake master she had casually killed with a punch. It was so pathetically weak, no threat at all. She shook her head. “Dangerous? Not at all.”

“That’s because you haven’t encountered danger yet. Where is your family or guardian? It’s very dangerous here!”

“They went to challenge Golden Core demon beasts. I was feeling quite bored, so I ran out... ah, wait, he’s not my guardian!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy instinctively followed Lü Chang's words, only to realize what she had said and hurriedly corrected herself.

The logic is wrong. Lu Yang is just a junior. I’m the elder.

Lü Chang and the other three exchanged glances, convinced that she had sneaked out.

“Fish King, are you here?” Lü Chang secretly tried to communicate with the lake master with his spiritual consciousness, planning to inquire about the girl’s situation and whether they should team up for a big score.

Not around? Lü Chang called out several times with his spiritual consciousness but received no response from the Fish King.

Could he have transformed and gone ashore to search for prey elsewhere? If that’s the case, the lake master can only blame himself for his bad luck. The four of us will be enjoying this unexpected windfall by ourselves.

“Are you looking for fish?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words startled Lü Chang.

I was using my spiritual consciousness to communicate with the lake master. How could an outsider have noticed?

“Let’s eat then. It’s freshly prepared.”

The Everlasting True Fire burned the branches into ash, then warmed the Beggar’s Fish with the residual heat. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy dug out large chunks of mud from the ashes. After knocking the outer layer of mud and tearing through the lotus leaves beneath, a refreshing aroma suffused the air, prompting Lü Chang and the others to inhale a deep breath.

We’ve lived in the wild for so long, yet this is the first time we have smelled such fragrant food. So this is the wealth and foundation of a big clan? Even the food they eat in the wild is totally different from what we’re used to.

“Eat up, this is the fish you were looking for.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words seemed to be disjointed.

I may be an immortal chef, but what are immortal chefs? They are still chefs. And chefs love nothing more than to have guests eat their food. Hence, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy generously shared her freshly made Beggar’s Fish with the other four.

Seeing how guileless she appeared, the four didn’t think she would poison them. Moreover, the Beggar’s Fish smelled heavenly. They decided to finish this meal before sending the little girl on her way to the afterlife. We’ll make sure to go easy on her.

The four found a large rock and sat in a circle, enjoying the delicious meal. Lü Chang took out a pair of chopsticks from his storage ring and picked up a piece of fish. However, the fish was so soft that it fell apart with the slightest pressure. He had no choice but to readjust his strength and gingerly pick up another piece. It melted in his mouth, giving the sensation of a ball of water. He couldn’t even taste its flavor before it slid down his throat.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy picked up two small twigs and washed them in the lake, using them as chopsticks. She carefully picked up a piece of fish and placed it in her mouth, savoring the flavor.

“Mmm, delicious.

“By the way, why do you demon beasts want to transform into human form?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly asked, “Isn’t it said that demon beasts are more agile in their original forms in the jungle?”

The four shot to their feet, towering over the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and staring at her fixedly.

“You know we are demon beasts?!”

“Ah, I’ve long noticed it.”

“Then why didn’t you react at all?”

“Why do I need to react?”

Lü Chang was about to praise her bravery when he felt that the fish meat in his stomach seemed to have turned from water into fire, burning within him until his Eight Extra Meridians were severed. He was drained of strength, and huge beads of sweat broke out on his forehead.

Thud!

He collapsed to the ground, writhing as he clutched his stomach. The other three followed suit, falling to the ground and staring at the seemingly harmless Everlasting Immortal Fairy in disbelief.

The four of them revealed their true forms. Lü Chang was a fox, while the others were a hedgehog, a snake, and a large lynx.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy realized that the fish was highly poisonous, capable of corroding even Lu Yang’s wooden clone. If this continues, I’ll have to return to Lu Yang’s side very soon.

She secretly activated the Everlasting Dao Fruit and dispersed the poison of the fish.

“What kind of fish is this?! How did you poison us?!” Lü Chang’s eyes were wide open. He was trying to divert the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attention as he stealthily circulated his cultivation technique to resist the poison.

After seeing through our disguise, this person acted nonchalant and even invited us to eat the meal she had poisoned.

What a schemer!

“It’s the Fish King you were looking for. It wanted to eat me, but I ate it instead.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said artlessly, “You wanted to look for it, right? It’s a bad demon beast; don’t look for it anymore.” She scrunched up her nose, displeased with the Fish King’s unreasonable behavior.

If this were the ancient era, how could any demon beast have dared to act like this toward me? It would be considered a severe transgression and warranted suicide.

“Isn’t the Fish King a pufferfish?!” Lü Chang was appalled. The Fish King is the master of this lake and an Apex Golden Core pufferfish with lethal poison throughout its body. Most importantly, this little girl is just at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. How could she possibly have defeated the Fish King?

“Go, kill her!” She’s fine after eating the fish; she must have the antidote!” Lü Chang and the other three temporarily suppressed the pufferfish’s poison with their cultivation and launched their attacks.

“Grab her storage ring too!” The four Golden Core cultivators surrounded the Foundation Establishment cultivator. I don’t believe this little lass can still win!

“So you’re just like the big fish. You’re all bad demon beasts!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was upset with the four of them.

I wanted to help cure them of the poison; I didn’t expect them to want to kill me.

Chapter 245: One Punch

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was taken aback, instinctively slapping downward. This was a reflex action that remained from fighting during the ancient era, and her combat style was long ingrained in her.

Just as Lü Chang got up, he felt as if a massive boulder had smashed into his head. With a thud, he collapsed to the ground.
