“All of you are bad people. Arhat Fruit Fist.” Hearing that they wanted to steal her storage ring, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was reminded of some unpleasant memories and slapped each of them once.

Despite her soft, delicate hands, they concealed immense power. When it was combined with a special force technique, the four Basic Golden Core demon beasts couldn’t withstand even a single hit. They lay sprawled on the ground once more, coughing up black blood.

The blood in demon beasts boiled with more exuberance than in humans. However, after receiving a slap from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, their originally roiling blood cooled rapidly. Even its circulation slowed until it stopped completely, their fiery blood fading into a deathly silence.

The Arhat Fruit Fist cleared heat and moistened the lungs. Along with the lethal toxin from the pufferfish, the four demon beasts perished on the spot.

In less than an hour, five Golden Core demon beasts had died here.

“Even the Qilin Immortal doesn’t dare bully me, yet you four little demon beasts think you could?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy harrumphed and planted her hands on her hips, pride swelling in her.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured to herself, “People like you have existed since ancient times, always trying to bully me. How hateful; three hundred thousand years have gone by, yet nothing has changed.” Walking away, she soon put the incident behind her and hummed a lighthearted tune while leaving four corpses behind her.

In ancient times, some people saw that I was a pretty woman and assumed I was gullible. They tried to deceive me, but the outcome was always the same—I saw through them with my sharp wit and killed them all.

“Pick, pick, picking mushrooms, picked a little mushroom...”

~~~

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sauntered around, snapping off a branch and casually refining it into a magical treasure. She waved it around in the jungle as if she was holding an unparalleled sword. As she radiated a strange power, no insect dared to go near her.

“Humans are really so fragile; they can get poisoned. If only everyone could learn my health maintenance fist techniques and turn themselves into a powerful medicine, wouldn’t poison be useless on them then?

“Jeez, Lu Yang’s the same too. I kindly offered to teach him, but why did he refuse to learn? The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others had to beg me on their knees, and even then, I didn’t teach them.”

This jungle felt very familiar to her. Before she became an immortal, she often wandered through the woods, in search of herbs to boost her cultivation or fend off surprise attacks from various prodigies.

Back then, I was very famous, not only because of my beauty but also my terrifying combat abilities and mysterious, unfathomable thoughts. No one could guess what I was thinking or what I would do next.

But one thing is for certain—I was the nightmare and greatest obstacle standing in the way of anyone seeking to become an immortal.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal and Qilin Immortal had yet to make a name for themselves, and the world knew nothing about them. Their biggest wish was to defeat the powerful Everlasting Immortal Fairy and rise to fame in one battle.

However, they never fulfilled their wish.

As such, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was adept at dealing with a myriad of dangers and battles. Ambushing her in the jungle was impossible.

Roar!

The furious bellow of a demon beast reverberated from nearby, piquing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s interest. Before she could head over, she noticed the ground shaking. The source of the tremors drew closer, as if some colossal creature was sprinting.

Boom! Boom!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy jumped onto a boulder and stood on tiptoe. Placing her right hand to her forehead, she peered into the distance. “That is...”

Trees fell, and dust billowed. The colossal figure towered above the trees in the jungle, revealing a coarse back.

It was a maddened elephant chasing a few people. The elephant was snow-white like jade, with six long tusks.

The few people being chased were highly skilled cultivators at the Advanced Golden Stage. However, when faced with the rampaging giant elephant, they didn’t have the slightest intention of resisting, simply focusing on running ahead and escaping.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy leaped off the boulder.

When they saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, their faces turned pallid as they desperately yelled to her, “This is a Basic Nascent Soul Elephant King! It carries a legitimate ancient bloodline of the Six-Tusked White Elephant! For some reason, it has gone mad. Little girl, quickly run!”

Although the Six-Tusked White Elephant was not as prestigious as the Dragon, Phoenix, Taowu[1], or Qiongqi in ancient times, it was still a renowned demon race second only to them. At least three Transcendent Tribulation experts had emerged from their tribe.

These few people could tell the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s cultivation stage at a glance, concluding that she was only at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. Even cultivators similarly at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage didn’t dare to face the deranged Elephant King head-on.

If this little girl doesn’t flee, her fate is obvious. We don’t wish to see her die tragically. She seems to be paralyzed by fear.

One of them suddenly mustered his strength, planning to drag the Everlasting Immortal Fairy along, but to his surprise, she seemed to have merged with the earth. I’m an Advanced Golden Core cultivator, yet I can’t even pick up this little girl? What’s going on with her?

The others also tried to heave the Everlasting Immortal Fairy away but to no avail. As the Six-Tusked White Elephant was right on their trail, they dared not waste any more time and could only continue running.

“Elephant, you’re being naughty. Back then, your tribe leader swore an oath to me to never harm the humans.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed a secret even the Six-Tusked White Elephant Tribe didn’t know of.

Unfortunately, this white elephant has lost its sanity and can’t be reasoned with. She sighed. If I don’t stop it, those few people will be doomed.

It’s a pity for this body.

Taking a deep breath, she assumed a stance, clenched her right hand into a fist, and placed it at her waist.

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.”

She slowly threw a punch.

~~~

The bodyguards rushed over, panting. “Young Master Song Hua and other young masters, are you alright? We noticed some commotion here earlier. You didn’t accidentally trespass on the Six-Tusked White Elephant’s territory, did you? You mustn’t go there!”

These were young masters from the Song Family in the imperial capital. They had come to the Demon Suppression Pass to burnish their credentials for a smoother path to promotion in the future. Out of safety considerations, the Song Family even hired several bodyguards for them.

At the start, the young masters were somewhat well-behaved, but they became increasingly annoyed by the bodyguards who forbade them from doing this and that. Why are we here if we’re not allowed to do anything? Are we here on vacation?

Hence, they sneaked away while the bodyguards weren’t paying attention. Before they could even go far, they had stumbled across the Six-Tusked White Elephant’s territory and inadvertently provoked it.

Song Hua and the others sat slumped on the ground, their eyes wide and mouths agape as they stared at something. The bodyguards followed their gaze and were equally dumbfounded, standing there in a daze.

It was a terrifying ravine, as if some colossal creature had slid through and knocked down countless massive trees. At the end of the ravine lay an unconscious white elephant the size of a small mountain.

“What on earth happened?”

Song Hua and the others couldn’t answer, or rather, they didn’t know how to describe what had just happened.

A petite girl, about sixteen or seventeen and at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, faced the rampaging Nascent Soul giant elephant, and with just one punch, she sent the elephant sprawling.

That punch seemed to have drained all the girl’s strength. She fell limply to the ground, fusing with the earth and vanishing from sight.

~~~

“You’re saying there’s a Nascent Soul Six-Tusked White Elephant nearby?” Lu Yang was panting heavily, having experienced successive days of battles. He sat on the ground to rest as he listened to the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes describe the extremely dangerous demon beasts in the vicinity.

“That giant elephant is said to be at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage and possess a strong territorial instinct. Whoever trespasses on its territory can expect to be trampled to death with no mercy.

“Moreover, the white elephant has a hot temper. It also treats the other Basic Nascent Soul demon beasts the same way. As long as they dare to intrude upon its territory without permission, they will bear the brunt of its attacks without fail. This was the reason it once fought with another Basic Nascent Soul demon beast. In the end, the white elephant won, and the other demon beast died.”

“Whew...” Meng Jingzhou sucked in a cold breath of air. So ruthless?

“You bet! I know that you two young heroes have displayed astonishing combat prowess, easily defeating several Golden Core demon beasts one after another. But even then, I doubt going up against the Six-Tusked White Elephant will be in your favor.”

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes exhorted, “And that is why we mustn't get close to its territory.”

Lu Yang nodded. “I understand.” I always listen to people's advice.

“Lu Yang, I'm back.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s soul drifted back into his mental space, unnoticed by everyone else.

“You're back so soon? It's not even three days yet.” Lu Yang was stunned. Based on my understanding of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, I thought she'd need at least three full days to have enough fun.

“Umm...your wooden clone wasn't sturdy, and I damaged it,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy confessed, her face full of grievances.

“What did you do?”

She stuck out her tongue, embarrassed about breaking the wooden clone. “Not telling you.”

If I had used the true Lu Yang to fight, I’d have the confidence to send the white elephant sprawling in one punch, all without damaging his body.

1. The Taowu is also one of the four fearsome beasts, along with the Qiongqi. It’s said to have the head of a human, the body of a tiger, and long tusks. ☜

Chapter 246: Twin Golden Cores

In the crystal-clear lake, a graceful figure swam through the water, her movements light and fluid as her hands parted the surface like a fish leaping out of water; it was a scene of mesmerizing beauty.

The graceful figure lay in the lake and flowed with the current, enjoying this moment of peace and relaxation.

Beside the lake, Lu Yang wore a helpless expression. “Immortal Fairy, can you not swim here?”

“Why are you meddling with me swimming too? Tch, take this spray.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted and clasped her hands. A jet of water sprayed out from the gaps between her fingers and sprayed toward Lu Yang, who easily dodged it.[1]

“I naturally won’t care about you swimming, but please don’t swim inside my mental space; it makes it seem like my mind is dimwitted with nothing but water.”[2] Lu Yang implored in exasperation.

Ever since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy came back, she has developed a peculiar love for playing with water, even conjuring a lake in my mental space.

“Go go go, continue your training. Don’t mind me.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kicked Lu Yang out of his mental space, as if she was the real owner.

Lu Yang was indeed in the middle of his training. At the moment, he was surrounded by three Golden Core wild boars, while Meng Jingzhou and the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were watching the showdown from the trees.

The wild boars charged recklessly with overwhelming strength. Lu Yang tried to avoid their frontal attacks and strike from the side, but the three boars worked together so seamlessly that they left him no opportunity to attack from the flank.

Bang!

One of the wild boars slammed right into Lu Yang, sending him flying away as dust swirled in the air.

“Wild boars, jiayou! Crush him!” Meng Jingzhou gloated at the side.

“Young Hero Lu, are you alright? It seems like one of the wild boars is at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage, and the other two are at the Apex Basic Golden Core Stage.” The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes had a conscience and were concerned about Lu Yang’s safety.

“It’s fine; no problem at all. If he can’t even defeat them, how can he call himself the top of our cohort? He might as well give the position up to me.” Meng Jingzhou waved his hand nonchalantly. The last time, Lu Yang had kicked me down from a tree to meet the enemy head-on. It’s time for the roles to be reversed.

The three wild boars wanted to press their advantage, but when the smoke cleared, Lu Yang had vanished.

Suddenly, they became alert and tried to dodge, but it was too late. A cold gleam of light shot up from beneath the ground, and the meter-long Qingfeng Sword pierced the belly of one of the wild boars.

The wild boar attempted to resist, but Lu Yang flicked his wrist and changed his sword move, softly commanding, “Slash.” He cleanly cleaved the wild boar right down the middle, splitting it into two.

One swing of the sword was all it took to kill an Intermediate Golden Core demon beast.

After training in the jungle for several days, Lu Yang had already fought with more than a dozen kinds of Golden Core demon beasts. His biggest takeaway was that it felt completely different from sparring with the senior disciples at the Dao-Seeking Sect. The Golden Core cultivators outside here are so much easier to deal with.

If I want to build self-confidence in the future, I shouldn’t do it in the Dao-Seeking Sect but come out here instead.

“I’ve told you. You are capable of challenging opponents above your level. It’s just that the opponents you faced before were too abnormal!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy protested in the mental space.

When I just resurrected, I wanted to use Lu Yang’s body to show off my skills and what it means to challenge those at higher levels. Who would have thought that each of those fellows in the Dao-Seeking Sect was more outrageous than the next? All of them could rank among the top talents even in the ancient era of prodigies; I couldn’t beat any of them.

Fortunately, relying on my exceptional wisdom later, I used Lu Yang’s body to challenge those at higher levels and even defeated a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, successfully restoring my reputation.

The other two wild boars saw that their big brother had died and hastily turned to flee.

“Chase them! We can’t let them escape!” Lu Yang reminded Meng Jingzhou.

“I know, no need for you to tell me.” Meng Jingzhou jumped down from the tree and joined Lu Yang, each hunting down one wild boar.

These wild boars were roving demon beasts that attacked human cultivators; no one knew how many human cultivators they had killed. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were certainly not letting them get away.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes waited in place. In just a few minutes, they heard the sounds of battle nearby, though they faded as quickly as they came. By the time the five of them regained their senses, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were each hauling a wild boar back.

“Dinner tonight is settled.”

~~~

Night fell, and the Three Flavor True Fire was ignited, casting a rosy glow on the faces of the seven people. A wild boar was placed over the fire to be slowly roasted. As it sizzled, oil dripped onto the true fire, causing the flames to flare even higher.

“I never thought we’d get to eat food roasted with true fire in our lifetime. We owe it all to Young Hero Lu,” the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes remarked. They didn’t expect a young man like Lu Yang to master a type of true fire.

While Lu Yang was roasting the boar, the Five Heroes were busy dissecting the other two boars. Inner cores, hide, tusks, and beast bones were valuable commodities that could fetch high prices in the Demon Suppression Pass. The inner cores could be used as the primary materials for concocting pills, the hide for refining magical artifacts, tusks for accessories to symbolize one’s status, and beast bones for brewing nourishing bone broth.

“Look! This wild boar demon has Twin Golden Cores!” One of the Five Heroes exclaimed.

“What? There’s such a thing?” The hook-nosed boss immediately walked over to inspect the situation.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were also intrigued and set aside their tasks. They had only seen Twin Golden Cores in the Dao-Seeking Sect and never heard of anyone outside the sect possessing such an ability to form two golden cores.

Two golden cores lay on the ground: one a dazzling gold and the other pitch-black. They represented two extremes—one bright and one dark—carrying a charm of “Dao” within them.

The more Lu Yang mulled over it, the more he felt that these two golden cores were impressive and encompassed boundless principles.

Good stuff.

Lu Yang marveled at his own growth. “I never thought I’d defeat a demon beast with Twin Golden Cores one day.”

Meng Jingzhou was equally amazed; he had never heard of anyone with a black golden core.

Golden cores were divided into nine grades: the first grade was the brightest and a brilliant gold, while the ninth grade was the most inferior, dull and lusterless but still gold.

This wild boar’s appearance is nothing extraordinary, yet it could form a black golden core. Is it because it has an ancient bloodline, or did it experience some fortuitous encounter?

“This wild boar is the descendant of the ancient Mountain-Shouldering Boar[3] that was capable of carrying two enormous mountains on its shoulders. It was full of gall but lacked the brains, so it had a low rank among the demons,” the hook-nosed boss mused. Having lived in the jungle for a long time, he was highly knowledgeable about demon beasts.

“That means it had some other fortuitous encounter?”

Meng Jingzhou speculated, “I heard there’s a rare natural treasure in the jungle, called the Twin Lotus Flower. One lotus seed is bright, while the other is dark. Consuming them can reverse yin and yang, altering one’s constitution. Could this wild boar have accidentally consumed the Twin Lotus Flower and formed the black and white golden cores?”

The hook-nosed boss nodded, agreeing with Meng Jingzhou’s theory. “If that’s the case, this wild boar really was lucky. Numerous people have come to the jungle to seek the Twin Lotus Flower and ended up empty-handed, yet this wild boar found it and ate it!”

Everyone could feel fiery excitement pumping through them. Are there any remaining Twin Lotus Flowers? Could we possibly find clues from this wild boar demon’s body and trace it to the Twin Lotus Flower?

“Immortal Fairy, what do you think? Can you tell where these Twin Golden Cores came from?” Lu Yang secretly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Twin Golden Cores? Isn’t the black one a gallstone?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was befuddled. Isn’t it because the Mountain-Shouldering Boar was full of gall? Secreting bile for a long time can result in it accumulating and forming gallstones, right?

I’ve seen this sort of thing too many times in the ancient era. What were these people babbling about for so long? Where did Twin Golden Cores come from?

Lu Yang, “...”

1. I used “spray” three times here because that’s what the original text did. To be more specific, it’s used when someone wants to spit saliva or spray urine at the other party in a more playful context. ☜

2. You might have come across expressions about how a person’s mind is full of water. It is a figure of speech that means there’s something wrong with someone’s mind. I tried my best to combine the figurative and literal meanings here. ☜

3. The name “Danshan,” translated as “Mountain-Shouldering” here, is from a Chinese folk tale of a man named Danshan who chased the suns away with mountains. ☜

Chapter 247: Would You Believe Me if I Said This Was an Accident?

With Lu Yang’s explanation, everyone finally realized they had made a huge mistake—the black “golden core” they had been examining for half a day wasn’t a golden core at all.

However, they couldn’t be entirely blamed. The excessive bile secretion leading to the formation of gallstones in Mountain-Shouldering Boars only happened to those minimally at the Golden Core Stage. Since the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes never had the chance to be in close quarters with Golden Core demon beasts, it was understandable that they weren’t aware.

Most importantly, who would have thought that Golden Core cultivators could develop gallstones?

“That’s perfectly normal,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied in a matter-of-fact tone. “Mortals develop ordinary gallstones, so it’s only natural that Golden Core cultivators develop Golden Core gallstones. It makes perfect sense.

“You just lack experience. You know about viruses, right? Those things that live in your body and make you sick? I’ve witnessed cases of cultivators growing stronger, only to have their viruses grow stronger too. Ever seen a Nascent Soul cultivator catch a cold virus?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proudly showed off her bizarre knowledge.

Lu Yang shook his head. Not only have I not seen such a thing, but I have never even heard of it.

“In ancient times, the viruses’ cultivation grew stronger alongside living beings, causing all sorts of trouble. When the Heaven Mandate Immortal established the lightning tribulation system, part of the consideration was to help high-level cultivators purge these viruses.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy disclosed yet another secret.

“Old Three, next time you can’t recognize something, don’t blindly shout nonsense!” the hook-nosed boss chided the third member of their group, who was in charge of dissection.

Old Three felt wronged. Just moments ago, all of you were making wild guesses so enthusiastically, and none of you could tell that this was a gallstone. Now you’re pinning the blame on me?

You can’t be unreasonable just because you’re the boss.

As he mulled over it, he casually pulled out the mountain boar’s gallbladder.

One, two, three, four, five... The phrase “Mountain-Shouldering Boars are full of gall” was not just a figure of speech—it was stating facts.

“Mountain-Shouldering Boars indeed had the gall. They charge at any demon they see, even dragons and phoenixes,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke from her personal experience.

“Wouldn’t they make enemies out of everyone?”

“Not really. Everyone shunned them. Think about it, most demon beasts rely on their mouths and claws in battle. But if you defeat a Mountain-Shouldering Boar, their bile will splatter all over you, and it’ll be unbearably bitter and nasty. Who could stand that?

“That said, I did create a delicacy based on the Mountain-Shouldering Boar’s unique trait, and it was widely praised.”

“What did you create?”

“Bile-stewed bitter melon. It’s great for clearing heat and detoxifying the body.”

Lu Yang involuntarily shuddered. “And you’re saying this was widely praised? Who had the honor of trying it?”

“The Nine-Layers Immortal! Back when he wasn’t an immortal yet, I saved him when he was severely poisoned. As he was on the brink of death, I made him a bowl of bile-stewed bitter melon to cleanse the toxins. When he slowly came to, he took a sip, commented ‘good,’ and then passed out again.

“Maybe it was because of the poison that he lost control of his body. When he saw me carrying the food over, he struggled desperately, his face contorted in a grimace as he uttered the word ‘good.’ So pitiful.”

“...That is quite pitiful.

“Was he cured of the poison?”

“Yes. After he woke up, he vomited for half a day and spat all the poison out.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does this detoxification method of yours sound completely different from what I had imagined?

“Enough talk, time for battle.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kicked Lu Yang out of his mental space again.

“Battle?” Lu Yang muttered under his breath before reacting quickly. He extended his spiritual consciousness and scanned his surroundings.

“No one? Wait, no...they’re underground!” Lu Yang looked down and saw a depression in the ground—a demon beast was lurking underneath.

“Prepare for battle!” Lu Yang hollered to everyone, his heart palpitating as he felt a sense of dread from the demon beast beneath the ground.

Boom!

A giant earthworm as thick as a water vat emerged from the soil. It had four silver rings that shimmered under the moonlight. Opening its wide, bloodstained maw, it swallowed the two wild boars that had just been dissected.

Due to Lu Yang’s warning, everyone managed to dodge in time, swiftly jumping away and retreating before the earthworm fully emerged.

“What is this?” Meng Jingzhou was flabbergasted. An earthworm can be this powerful?

“It’s a Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm!” Lu Yang instantly recognized the demon beast. It was the king of the earthworm species. There’s a pair of these earthworms tilling the soil in the herb garden that Old Ba oversees.

Oh, it’s two pairs now.

The earthworm couple in the herb garden had five silver rings, with the sixth one in the process of forming, signifying that they were at the Apex Divine Transfiguration Stage. The earthworm before us has four silver rings, so it should be at the Nascent Soul Stage.

The more troublesome thing was that Lu Yang’s proud sword techniques hardly posed a threat to this earthworm. One swing of the sword could result in two earthworms, exacerbating matters.

After the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm devoured the third wild boar demon that was roasted over the Three Flavor True Fire, it shifted its gaze to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, clearly yet to be satiated.

The two had never faced a Nascent Soul opponent before, and the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes couldn’t help in such a situation.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Meng Jingzhou was the first to strike. As his fists clenched with bulging veins, he displayed a vast aura, as if he could shake heaven and earth.

However, the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm was coated in a layer of mucus. Meng Jingzhou’s packed punch couldn’t even make a scratch on its skin before its force was neutralized.

The Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm swung its tail and sent Meng Jingzhou flying, breaking several of his bones. If he weren’t a physique cultivator, this strike could have cost him his life.

The divide between the Nascent Soul and Foundation Establishment stages was colossal, with the Golden Core Stage still separating them.

“Break!” Lu Yang yelled as he unleashed his Breaking Word Mantra. Sword light cascaded like a waterfall, breaking the sound barrier and tearing through the darkness. The blade of the sword carried the moonlight, resembling a strike from a god of death.

This was Lu Yang’s most powerful move.

The Qingfeng Sword pierced through the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm’s mucus layer and embedded itself in its body. The earthworm shrieked in pain. Thrashing around violently, it intended to crush this human to death.

Whenever Lu Yang contacted the ground, he used Shrinking Earth to avoid crashing to the ground and getting smashed. He exerted force on his fist, trying to thrust himself upward, but the earthworm’s physical body was too powerful. With its body taut, the Qingfeng Sword was stuck.

The Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm growled a few times as if it was mocking Lu Yang’s futile attempts.

Naturally, it could speak, but it didn’t deign to communicate with these weak humans. Opening its gaping mouth, it aimed to bite Lu Yang. At the last second, Lu Yang pulled out the Qingfeng Sword and narrowly evaded the attack.

Lu Yang’s heart sank. The Breaking Sword Mantra strike contains my full strength, capable of killing Advanced Golden Core or even Half-Step Nascent Soul demon beasts in one slash. Yet, this strike didn’t even harm the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm’s foundation and only angered it.

Worst of all, this sword strike has also drained most of my powers.

“Tsk, this is a pain.”

On the other side, Meng Jingzhou noticed that Lu Yang was also at his wits’ end. Suddenly, he remembered something. Reaching into his robes, he pulled out five Targeted Teleportation Talismans.

But there are seven of us here. If Lu Yang and I escape, the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm will definitely not let the Five Heroes off.

“Young Heroes, don’t worry about us! Hurry and go!” The hook-nosed boss shouted upon seeing the Targeted Teleportation Talismans in Meng Jingzhou’s hands. Those in our line of work have long put life and death aside.

Meng Jingzhou gritted his teeth.

What should I do?! What should I do?!

Running away is not my style, but if I don’t, everyone will die here!

In the end, he closed his eyes and took one teleportation talisman, throwing it to Lu Yang. “Lu Yang, catch!”

Lu Yang bent over and dashed forward. However, the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm sneered and placed its gigantic body between him and Meng Jingzhou

“Trying to run?” The earthworm spoke for the first time, snickering repeatedly and ridiculing Lu Yang’s pointless effort.

“Now!” Lu Yang hollered.

“Do I need you to tell me?” Meng Jingzhou’s lazy voice sounded from the other side as he activated the Targeted Teleportation Talisman.

This was the moment he had been waiting for.

An invisible cubic light curtain enveloped the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm. It didn’t understand what was happening and tried to shake free with all its might, but the light curtain was exceptionally firm and couldn’t be broken.

~~~

The moment Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou saw the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm, they remembered the instructions from the attendant at the merchant guild. “If you encounter a life-or-death crisis in the jungle, you just have to activate this talisman, and it will teleport you back to the Demon Suppression Pass. Even a Nascent Soul demon cannot interrupt the teleportation process!”

Looking at it from a different perspective, if humans can be safely teleported back to the Demon Suppression, why can’t demon beasts also be teleported back?

~~~

The cubic light encasing the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm morphed into a streak of light and flew toward the Demon Suppression Pass, where the large characters “Demon Suppression Pass” at the city gate froze the earthworm in place.

The guards were bewildered to see a Nascent Soul demon beast suddenly appear. Despite having worked in this job for over ten years, it’s our first time encountering such a haughty demon beast. It didn’t even try to disguise itself and charged directly at the Demon Suppression Pass.

“What audacity, you vile beast! How dare you attack the Demon Suppression Pass in the middle of the night!” A deep voice bellowed from within the city; it was a Divine Transfiguration cultivator on duty.

The Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm watched helplessly as a burly man flew out from the city toward it. Its heart was filled with despair.

“Would you believe me if I said this was an accident?” The earthworm tried its best to squeeze out a smile.

The burly man snorted. “Do you think I’ll believe you?”

He reached out his massive hand and slapped the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm dead.

Chapter 248: Immortal Fairy, Please Stop Sharing So Many Ancient Tales, I’m Afraid I Won’t Live Long Enough

“You can use Targeted Teleportation Talismans like that?!” The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes were stupefied to see the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm forcibly teleported away.

What left the deepest impression was the hopeless look in the earthworm’s eyes.

The great Nascent Soul demon’s fate was evident.

Due to the rules established in the Demon Suppression Pass, any demons below the Fusion Stage that got close to the city would die. A Nascent Soul demon might sound formidable, but when confronted with a truly colossal entity such as the Demon Suppression Pass, only death awaited.

“Ah? Isn’t this the proper way to use it?” Lu Yang was taken aback. He had thought only demon beasts were slow-witted and couldn’t come up with such a usage method. The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes are fellow humans, yet they also can’t think of this idea?

Look at Meng Jingzhou—he figured it out in an instant.

“Are there really so many Golden Core and Nascent Soul demon beasts in the jungle? Lu Yang thought back about their encounters in the past few days. Not counting the ones that intentionally came seeking them at their doorstep, the group had met quite a few demon beasts that were criminals on the run, all of them at the Golden Core Stage.

Tonight was crazier; even a Nascent Soul demon beast came looking for us. Fortunately, Meng Jingzhou had the Targeted Teleportation Talisman and sent the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm back to the Demon Suppression Pass; otherwise, the last resort would have been Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist.

The hook-nosed boss shook his head. “How is that possible? Be it humans or demons, most of those who wander this jungle are at the Foundation Establishment Stage. If things were like now, constantly getting ambushed by Golden Core demon beasts, no one would dare come here anymore.”

Lu Yang thought about it and agreed. Those demon beasts were unlucky to have bumped into us. Had it been any other Foundation Establishment cultivators, they would have been dead by now.

The hook-nosed boss analyzed, “It’s probably because you two young heroes have killed too many demon beasts, and the scent attracted the attention of other demon beasts.” The five of us are at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, and we struggle to fight demon beasts at the same level, yet here are these two young heroes, slaying Basic and Intermediate Golden Core demon beasts as effortlessly as chopping vegetables.

So this is disparity.

“I propose we wait until the city gate opens tomorrow morning to return to the city. We’ll rest well, change our clothes, and wash off the scent,” the hook-nosed boss suggested.

Lu Yang nodded. That makes sense. Over the past few days, the seven of us have been on edge. If we weren’t fighting, we were on our way to fight. That’s too much mental strain.

Since my mental strength is far superior to those at the same level, it shouldn’t have depleted so quickly. Meng Jingzhou and the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes may feel exhausted, but I shouldn’t be.

But what can I do? I have the Everlasting Immortal Fairy always stirring up chaos. I need to spare part of my mental strength to deal with her and listen to her ramblings about ancient tales.

Ancient tales included, but were not limited to the following:

The jealousy and rivalry for affection between the prodigies of the Dragon and Phoenix tribes.

The Qilin Immortal fled to a foreign land when a fire broke out in his harem, earning him the nickname “Fire Qilin.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal urged everyone to hold back from taking action to elevate the prestige of immortals.

The Epoch Immortal felt that time dragged on like years while eating the food prepared by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Comprehending the theory of relativity, he strongly supported having the Everlasting Immortal Fairy also cook for the other three immortals.

The Nine-Layers Immortal published an academic paper proving himself to be the first immortal and managed archaeological excavation projects to prove his legitimacy.

To be honest, these were all wondrous ancient tales related to immortals and worth a great deal; they could fetch a sky-high price at an auction. If the old pedants studying ancient history heard these stories, they would likely be so excited they couldn’t sleep. The amount of information contained within was vast enough to overturn people’s impression of the ancient era.

However, when it came to Lu Yang, he was deeply worried that one day, he would wake up to find the four ancient immortals standing beside him, looking down at him with a malevolent smile and telling him, “You know too much. Time to die.”

I have no Everlasting Dao Fruit to save me.

To look on the bright side, by the time Big Senior Sister arrives, she may be able to collect my corpse.

Lu Yang expressed his concerns to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but she remained her simple-minded and devil-may-care self. “Aiya, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others are good people. They are easy to talk to and won’t treat you like that. Look at me, even though I know so many things, am I not alive and doing just fine?”

Lu Yang silently looked at the soul state of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, wanting to remind her that she had been dead for over three hundred thousand years and had only been resurrected two months ago.

After all the fights these few days, both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s combat experience had improved significantly, and they had also become more proficient in delivering deadly blows. Their cultivation was also steadily rising. Consolidating their Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivation, they were slowly advancing toward the Golden Core Stage.

“Why does it feel like you have more combat experience than me?” Meng Jingzhou was nonplussed, believing it wasn’t an illusion.

Lu Yang replied expressionlessly, “If you get beaten up by our senior brothers and sisters from night until morning, your combat experience will also increase.” I still remember that when I was getting thrashed, this grandson was clapping and cheering beneath the stage.

Meng Jingzhou mused, “There’s such an effect?” I’ve never been weaker than others in my life; I can’t lose to Lu Yang in combat experience.

~~~

Their supposed rest night was not a peaceful one. Another Golden Core demon beast attempted an ambush and was punched to death by Meng Jingzhou, who was on night watch.

It was a rabbit the size of a domestic pig, with two large incisors about three to four inches long and two eyes as red as rubies.

“Do we really attract this much hatred? Can’t even get a good rest at night!” Meng Jingzhou furiously kicked the rabbit demon. He was distracted for a moment during the fight earlier, and the rabbit took the chance to bite his hair. Fortunately, I had long tempered my whole body, including my hair, and saved myself from catastrophe.

The Eagle Mountain Five Heroes couldn’t offer an explanation either. They had limited experience and had never seen anyone kill demon beasts so ruthlessly. “It really shouldn’t be the case. Logically speaking, this area is on the outskirts of the jungle, so there won’t be so many Golden Core demon beasts. It’s not worth it for them to come here.”

“Never mind, let’s discuss this after we get back.” Lu Yang asked everyone to head back and rest at the Demon Suppression Pass.

~~~

When the group returned to the Demon Suppression Pass, they overheard the people chattering at the city gate.

“Have you heard? Last night, a great Nascent Soul demon tried to ambush the Demon Suppression Pass under the cover of the night and was slapped to death by a Divine Transfiguration expert on night duty.”

“Is that for real? Did the demon beast have too much to drink? It was only at the Nascent Soul Stage, yet it dared attempt an ambush?” His companion was astonished.

The Demon Suppression Pass was one of the six major cities guarding the border with the Demon Region. Unless several Fusion cultivators joined hands, one shouldn’t dream of breaking through this fortress.

However, there were precedents for this. A few great demons had gotten drunk and run to the Demon Suppression Pass to train their courage. The lucky ones were driven away, while the unlucky ones ended up in the pot the next day for the whole city to feast on.

“Of course, it’s true. Haven’t you noticed there are more guards at the city gates today? The higher-ups suspect that the demons are planning something big, which is why they sent cannon fodder to test our defenses!”

“Is another fight going to break out again?”

“That’s unlikely. They’re probably just testing the waters. There’s also another unreliable rumor.”

“What is it?”

“They say the demon beast was sent here by someone using a Targeted Teleportation Talisman?”

“That can’t be real, right? How can Targeted Teleportation Talismans be used like that?”

“That’s why I said it’s an unreliable rumor.”

“So are we getting a good meal today?” The Demon Suppression Pass often distributed demon beast meat killed at the city gates to everyone.

“I doubt it’s enough.”

“Why’s that?”

“It was an earthworm demon that died. How are you going to eat that?”

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was surprised. “Hey, you guys here don’t eat earthworms?”

“...Immortal Fairy, do you want to listen to what you’re saying?”

Chapter 249: Twin Lotus Flower

After much effort, Lu Yang finally managed to dissuade the Everlasting Immortal Fairy from showing off her skills with the argument, “Mortals are not worthy to enjoy an immortal’s cooking.”

“Lu Yang, that’s not the right mindset. All are equal before gourmet food. But I’ll let it slide this time.”

“Immortal Fairy, you truly have lofty ideals with the big picture in mind.” Lu Yang was extremely generous with his compliments. He felt that his actions were of boundless beneficence, saving countless lives. If only the cultivation world had a theory of ascending to immortality through accumulated merit, I believe I could eventually become an immortal.

~~~

The seven of them arrived at the Luodi Merchant Guild and retrieved various corpses of demon beasts from their jade tablets, their spoils of war eliciting multiple gasps.

“These...these are all Golden Core demon beasts?!” It was the same attendant who had served Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou before. He could tell the cultivation of these demon beasts at a glance, and these corpses were intact and hardly damaged.

This was mainly due to Lu Yang’s sword, which prioritized killing the target in one strike, and Meng Jingzhou’s fists, which pulverized the demon beasts’ brains with covert force.

Upon associating it with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s backgrounds, the attendant came to terms with it.

One is a disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect—that needs no further explanation. His combat prowess has to be outstanding and invincible among his peers of the same level.

In reality, disciples of the Five Great Immortal Sects were analogous to being invincible among peers of the same level. They would be embarrassed to call themselves disciples of the Five Great Immortal Sects if they couldn’t defeat opponents beyond their level. However, what the attendant didn’t know was that even within the Five Great Immortal Sects, Lu Yang was particularly formidable, defeating the strongest Foundation Establishment cultivator from the Five-Elements Sect.

The other is a direct descendant of the Meng Family. The Meng Family is infamous for stirring up trouble in the imperial capital, with the line of enemies seeking vengeance stretching from the Meng Estate to the imperial palace. If a member from the main branch of the Meng Family has no genuine skills, they would have been beaten to death a long time ago.

The attendant even heard that the headquarters was considering launching a “Meng Family Personal Accident Insurance.”

“Esteemed guests, do you not want the inner cores too?” The attendant picked out the inner cores, the most valuable parts of a Golden Core demon beast. These could be used to refine pills that increased the probability of forming a golden core, making it highly sought after by Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators. For some Half-Step Golden Core cultivators, this single pill could be the only thing standing between them and the true Golden Core Stage.

“We have no use for them. Just sell them all together.” Meng Jingzhou waved his hand dismissively.

The attendant quickly appraised the value of the demon beast corpses. The three mostly intact corpses were worth one Targeted Teleportation Talisman, even after applying a discount through the Meng Family's influence.

“Give me five more Targeted Teleportation Talismans.” Having tasted the benefits, Meng Jingzhou decided to purchase more. Now, I have nine Targeted Teleportation Talismans for dealing with nine Nascent Soul demon beasts. With this set-up, it’s enough for me to traverse the jungle like it’s a no-man’s land.

“I’ll give you four.” Meng Jingzhou handed four talismans to Lu Yang.

Then, he turned to the attendant, “Do you have any higher-grade teleportation talismans?”

“Higher-grade?”

“Ones that won’t be interrupted even under the attacks of Divine Transfiguration demon beasts.”

“Hold on a bit, let me check.” Due to the exorbitant prices of Targeted Teleportation Talismans, few people bought them, so the attendant wasn’t very knowledgeable in this regard. “Apologies, we only have Nascent Soul Targeted Teleportation Talismans in stock here. Divine Transfiguration Targeted Teleportation Talismans are only available at our headquarters. Would you like to have some transferred here?”

“Have your headquarters send three over.” Meng Jingzhou always prioritized safety.

“Aye.”

“Has there been any news about rare natural treasures in the jungle recently? Lu Yang inquired. The merchant guild offered a service that claimed to uncover any intelligence as long as one could provide sufficient spirit stones.

Of course, this is false advertising. At the very least, the merchant guild doesn’t know Big Senior Sister’s age.

The attendant made a polite gesture, inviting the two into a soundproof room and activating an array to prevent outsiders from probing. Important information naturally couldn’t be disclosed in public.

The attendant went straight to the point. “Someone discovered a Twin Lotus Flower.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were stunned. We just mentioned this rare natural treasure last night, and now it has appeared?

“Where?”

The attendant spread out a map and pointed to one of the lakes. “It was found in a lake one hundred and ten li south of the Demon Suppression Pass. Originally, that lake was home to an Advanced Golden Core Fish King, a pufferfish demon. Its body contained deadly poison that few at the same cultivation stage could withstand. It was undisputedly the local overlord. Moreover, it was rumored to have formed an alliance with four other Golden Core demon beasts, inflicting harm on countless people.

“Just three days ago, someone accidentally entered the Fish King’s territory and thought that death was inevitable. To their surprise, they were not attacked. On the shore were the corpses of four Golden Core demon beasts that had died from poisoning. This was verified after an autopsy. The person also found the corpse of the Fish King in the lake, chunks of its flesh strewn everywhere.

“We suspect that the Fish King and these four demon beasts had a falling-out over an unequal distribution of the spoils, leading to internal strife. In the end, the four demon beasts were poisoned to death by the Fish King, while the Fish King was also ripped to pieces and met its demise.

“Later, people discovered the Twin Lotus Flower in that lake, which had been guarded and hidden by the Fish King all this while. This Twin Lotus Flower will bloom in five days. Many people have received the news and are preparing to snatch it.”

“Twin Lotus Flower, huh...” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged an intrigued smile.

Neither of them had decided what type of golden core they wanted to form. Lu Yang didn’t want a Sword Golden Core, while Meng Jingzhou didn’t want a Single’s Golden Core, so they needed external inspiration. Observing the Twin Lotus Flower could lead to insights into golden core formation, and there were examples of this in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

When a senior male disciple was forming his golden core, the Twin Lotus Flower happened to bloom in his room. Studying the lotus flowers under the moonlight, he had an epiphany and formed a highly aggressive Yin-Yang Golden Core.

When he activated his Yin-Yang Golden Core, sarcastic words as mystifying as yin and yang[1] would spill from his mouth, remarkably effective at drawing hostility and making enemies.

Lu Yang knew this person; it was none other than his second senior brother, who was still training in the Golden Buddhist Kingdom.

The abbot of the Hanging Monastery, the only Transcendent Tribulation cultivator among the leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects, had also drawn inspiration from the Twin Lotus Flower when he was at the Golden Core Stage. His golden core was engraved with a lotus flower design. That way, whenever he debated or lectured on scriptures, he could awe people with the special effects of spouting lotus flowers and leaving a trail of lotus flowers with every step.

This was different from spells, which were external forces. His special effects were a pure and natural phenomenon. It earned the admiration of many formidable figures, demonstrating the potent effects of the Twin Lotus Flower.

“The lotus seeds are also delicious,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded Lu Yang of another effect of the Twin Lotus Flower.

When she killed the Fish King, she had noticed the Twin Lotus Flower. However, it hadn’t bloomed yet, and picking it prematurely could cause the flower to lose its spiritual nature. As an immortal chef, or rather, the only immortal chef in the world, I naturally can’t waste such a precious treasure.

“The lotus seeds can be used to make lotus seed soup, symbolizing fertility and fortune. When you want children in the future, you can prepare this for your wife.”

“...Immortal Fairy, your thinking is way ahead of its time. I don’t even have a fiancée.”

“You’ll have one sooner or later. This is the blessing of an immortal!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was brimming with confidence. My blessings have never gone wrong.

Lu Yang felt that his life was tough and fraught with misfortune.

1. There is a chengyu or four-character idiom in Chinese which is “yin yang guai qi.” As you can see, the term “yin yang” is the same as the yin and yang we know. This idiom describes someone deliberately speaking in an eccentric, bizarre, insincere, and ambiguous manner, which leaves the other party perplexed. If it is complicated to wrap your head around this, you can think of it as a less-confrontational version of sarcasm, if it helps. ☜

Chapter 250: The Sensible Huang Doudou

After leaving the merchant guide and temporarily parting ways with the Eagle Mountain Five Heroes, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou returned to the inn. They asked the waiter to buy some quality dishes nearby and deliver them to their rooms.

“By the way, no tofu,” Lu Yang reminded the waiter before heading upstairs.

“The bed is still the best!” Upon returning to his room, Lu Yang pounced onto the bed with an expression of pure bliss.

“Right? Sleeping is very comfortable.” Having been dead for three hundred thousand years, a certain Huang Doudou wholeheartedly agreed with Lu Yang’s sentiment.

She now spent her days sleeping in the mental space, sleeping more when she was in a good mood and less when in a bad mood. Thankfully, I’m always in a good mood.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waited a long time but didn’t receive a response from Lu Yang. Only then did she realize that Lu Yang had fallen deeply asleep, his mouth slightly open.

The past few days in the jungle had been exhausting. Lu Yang had to be on constant alert like a taut string. The moment he encountered a comfortable environment, his entire body relaxed.

Meng Jingzhou’s situation was not much different. He fell asleep as soon as his head hit the pillow. Pampered since childhood, his family could give him anything, even plucking the stars from the sky. He naturally had never experienced such hardships in the jungle.

“Guests, your meal has arrived.” The waiter knocked on the door lightly.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was worried that the noise would wake Lu Yang up, so she temporarily took control of Lu Yang’s body and went to open the door.

“Shh, keep it down, he’s sleeping!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed a finger to her lips, signaling to the waiter that he was too loud.

The waiter handed over the tray and instinctively lowered his voice, “Understood, guest.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy took the meal and closed the door. She placed the food on the table and controlled Lu Yang’s body to return to the bed, arranging him in the same position, as though nothing had happened.

“So boring, I’ll sleep too.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned and fell asleep inside the mental space.

When the waiter reached the stairs, he suddenly remembered the state of the room he had glimpsed from the corner of his eye. “Wasn’t the guest who opened the door the only person in the room? Who’s sleeping?”

He felt an inexplicable chill run down his spine, as if someone was watching him, and subconsciously sped up his pace down the stairs.

“Immortals, please bless me! Immortals, please bless me! I haven’t done anything wrong!”

~~~

“Feels amazing!” Lu Yang stirred awake. “What smells so good?”

He was stupefied to see the spread on the table—three meat dishes, one vegetable dish, and one soup.

Where on earth did the food come from? I remember telling the waiter to deliver the food, but I don’t remember opening the door.

“Do I have the habit of sleepwalking?” Lu Yang scratched his head, thinking his mind was still foggy from just waking up.

To be fair, the waiter had a decent taste in food. The dishes were delicious and packed with local flavor. It was tender, likely made with Foundation Establishment demon beasts, which could replenish spirit energy and rejuvenate the mind.

Originally, Lu Yang thought about asking the Everlasting Immortal Fairy whether she wanted to occupy his body for the time being to try the local specialties, but he noticed that she was still asleep and didn’t wake her up.

After having his fill, Lu Yang was invigorated and in high spirits, completely different from last night.

He went next door to look for Meng Jingzhou.

“You’re saying you want me to teach you the Arhat Fist?” Meng Jingzhou was slightly stunned to hear Lu Yang’s request.

“I thought about it this morning. I’ve made decent progress in spells and sword techniques, but I lack a fist technique in my repertoire. The battlefield is unpredictable, and who knows when a fist technique might come in handy?”

“Don’t you know the Animal Form Fist?”

“And then summon Big Senior Sister?”

Meng Jingzhou agreed that it was a bit overboard. If you fight like that, the battle won’t be fun anymore; it’s practically summoning a deity. Besides, Lu Yang’s Animal Form Fist is more like a Shapeshifting Technique rather than a fist technique.

“Is it possible for you to teach me?”

“My shifu is not averse to sharing this technique with others. Though the Arhat Fist is rare, you can also learn it from Big Senior Sister when you go back. It’s just a matter of whether you learn it from me or her.”

As long as you know the name of a spell or technique, you can learn it from Big Senior Sister. If she really doesn’t know, she could create a new version based on the name.

“That’s great then.” Lu Yang was fired up at the thought of learning another fist technique.

“You’d rather learn the Arhat Fist than my Arhat Fruit Fist?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stomped her feet in anger. The name “Arhat Fist” doesn’t sound strong at all, nowhere as nice-sounding as the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.

“When you master Arhat Fruit Fist, you can continue to learn over a thousand other fist techniques like the Sichuan Peppercorn Fist[1], Star Anise Fist, and Cumin Fist. Once you internalize them all, you’ll be able to learn the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique, and you’ll be unbeatable in the world!”

Lu Yang could only sigh at the imaginary grand vision the Everlasting Immortal Fairy promised. “As long as you change the name of your fist techniques, I’ll learn it.”

In battles, others display mighty moves like the Eight-Extremes Fist[2] and Heaven-Shaking Six Forms. If someone asks me who I learned it from and what fist technique I’m using, I can’t possibly say that this is the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.

I’ll lose in terms of grandeur before the battle even begins.

~~~

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou rented a closed-off training ground and began learning the Arhat Fist.

“I won’t tell you about the history of the Arhat Fist since it’s just memorization; you can look it up yourself when you have time.” Meng Jingzhou skipped the formalities and went straight to hands-on teaching.

“The overall sequence emphasizes breaking the bottom from the top and the top from the bottom, pointing to the right and striking the left, making a feint in the east and attacking the west, and highlighting unpredictability, speed, and variation. At the same time, it uses qi to emit sounds like thunder to boost morale and amplify one’s might.

“Just like this.”

Meng Jingzhou stood upright with his arms naturally at his sides. Staring straight ahead, his left foot stepped half a step to the left, while both palms moved upward and outward in an arc.

“Ha!”

His demonstration looked the part, resembling an angry vajra with an imposing might that seemed to have come from hell, while his booming and resonant voice sounded like the Buddhist Lion Roar Art.

“The sea of suffering is boundless; turning back leads to the shore![3]

“This is the Horse Stance Single Whip!

“This is the Extended Step Piercing Fist!

“This is the Great Peng Sweeping Claw!”

Meng Jingzhou showcased every move of the Arhat Fist, making Lu Yang’s heart surge with exhilaration. When he finished his sequence, he had fully displayed the essence of the Arhat Fist, as though an actual arhat monk had appeared before Lu Yang, vanquishing demons and dispelling evil.

Upon recalling that Third Elder’s unique technique, the “Heaven-Shaking Six Forms,” was derived from the Arhat Fist, Lu Yang was even more excited. Perhaps I can also comprehend other fist techniques through studying the Arhat Fist.

“Speaking of which, has Third Elder ever told you how he comprehended ‘Heaven-Shaking Six Forms’ from the Arhat Fist?” Lu Yang asked, thinking he might be able to draw on Third Elder’s experience.

“Yes, he did.” Meng Jingzhou thought back. “Shifu said that when he was younger, he traveled to the Golden Buddhist Kingdom and met an old man proficient in the Arhat Fist. The elderly man was called the Devil-Subduing Arhat, and he beat Shifu like he was a grandson.

“Shifu was forced to flee and scurry away while covering his head to avoid being beaten further. In his desperate straits, he exploded with power and invented his own fist technique, the ‘Heaven-Shaking Six Forms.’”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does this process of developing a fist technique sound so different from what I’d imagined?

“So, did Third Elder defeat him in the end?”

“No, the other party was one major cultivation realm above Shifu.”

1. If you’re curious about what Sichuan peppercorn is called in Chinese, it’s huajiao. ☜

2. Baijiquan is one of the various Chinese martial arts. ☜

3. It’s a well-known Buddhist saying. I’ve tried to maintain the same words in each of the two parts. ☜
